Oracle SCM Cloud 完整學習指南 Oracle SCM Cloud Complete Learning Guide

從供應鏈基礎到各模組實作，系統化掌握 Oracle SCM Cloud 全貌。適合初學者、顧問及企業 Key User 使用。

A systematic guide covering all Oracle SCM Cloud modules — from foundations to hands-on implementation. Designed for beginners, consultants, and enterprise key users.

10 個模組Modules 60+ 關鍵術語Key Terms 雙語中英Bilingual ZH/EN 互動學習Interactive

什麼是 Oracle SCM Cloud？

What is Oracle SCM Cloud?

🌐

端對端供應鏈平台

End-to-End Supply Chain Platform

Oracle SCM Cloud 是一套雲端 SaaS 系統，涵蓋從原料採購、生產製造、庫存管理到產品交付的完整流程，幫助企業降低成本、提高效率。

Oracle SCM Cloud is a cloud-based SaaS platform covering the complete flow from raw material sourcing, manufacturing, inventory management to product delivery — helping enterprises reduce costs and improve efficiency.

⚙️

兩條核心業務主線

Two Core Business Flows

Procure-to-Pay（P2P）：從請購需求到付款給供應商的採購流程。
Order-to-Cash（O2C）：從客戶下單到收款的銷售履行流程。

Procure-to-Pay (P2P): The procurement cycle from purchase request to supplier payment.
Order-to-Cash (O2C): The sales fulfillment cycle from customer order to cash receipt.

🤖

AI 驅動的現代供應鏈

AI-Driven Modern Supply Chain

從 24A 版本起，Oracle 導入 AI Agent 技術，實現收料、付款應計、備件推薦等流程的自動化，持續降低人工干預。

Starting with version 24A, Oracle introduced AI Agent capabilities to automate receiving, accruals, spare parts recommendations, and more — continuously reducing manual intervention.

💡
所有模組共享同一套基礎資料（組織架構、料號、日曆），因此模組 0 的設定必須最先完成，才能啟用其他功能。 All modules share the same master data (org structure, items, calendars). This means Module 0 foundation setup must be completed first before enabling other modules.

模組 0：共通基礎建置 Module 0: Common Foundation Setup

所有 SCM 模組的地基——必須最先完成，否則其他功能無法正常運作 The foundation for all SCM modules — must be completed first before any other module can function

FSM Enterprise Structure Item Master UOM
🔑
為什麼這個模組如此重要？Why does this module matter so much?
沒有正確的組織架構與品項主檔，採購、庫存、製造模組通通無法啟動。這不是選項，而是先決條件。 Without correct org structure and item master setup, procurement, inventory, and manufacturing modules simply cannot start. This is not optional — it is a prerequisite.

2024 年初，ABC Electronics Taiwan 決定導入 Oracle Fusion SCM Cloud。IT 專案經理陳小明在第一次會議就遭遇了難題：採購團隊急著要測試請購單，倉儲團隊要測試收貨，製造部門要設定工單——但所有人都必須等待，因為基礎架構還沒建立。沒有 Inventory Organization，就無法設定倉庫位置；沒有 Item Master，就無法建立採購品項；沒有正確的 UOM，收貨數量就會計算錯誤。整個專案在第一週就卡關了。 In early 2024, ABC Electronics Taiwan decided to implement Oracle Fusion SCM Cloud. IT Project Manager Alan Chen hit a wall at the very first meeting: the procurement team was eager to test purchase requisitions, the warehouse team wanted to test receipts, and manufacturing wanted to configure work orders — but everyone had to wait because the foundational structure was not yet built. Without an Inventory Organization, warehouse locations could not be defined; without an Item Master, purchasing items could not be created; without correct UOMs, receipt quantities would calculate incorrectly. The entire project stalled in its very first week.

經過顧問團隊的評估，他們制定了「先打地基」策略：第一步啟用 FSM Offerings、第二步建立法律實體與業務單位、第三步設定台灣總部與上海廠兩個 Inventory Organization、第四步設定品項類別與 UOM 換算表。整個過程花了兩週，但讓後續每個模組的設定都能順暢進行，避免了日後龐大的資料修正成本。 After consulting team assessment, they adopted a "build the foundation first" strategy: Step 1 — enable FSM Offerings; Step 2 — create Legal Entity and Business Units; Step 3 — set up Taiwan HQ and Shanghai factory Inventory Organizations; Step 4 — configure item classes and UOM conversion tables. The process took two weeks, but it allowed every subsequent module to be configured smoothly and avoided massive data-correction costs later.

本模組將帶你完整走過 ABC Electronics Taiwan 的實際建置流程，讓你理解每個設定背後的業務邏輯，並避免新手最常犯的七種錯誤。完成本模組後，你將能獨立建立一套完整的 Oracle SCM 組織架構，並讓所有其他模組可以正常運作。 This module walks you through ABC Electronics Taiwan's complete real-world setup process, helping you understand the business logic behind each configuration step and avoid the seven most common beginner mistakes. After completing this module, you will be able to independently build a complete Oracle SCM org structure and enable all other modules to function correctly.

核心功能

Key Features

⚙️

FSM Offerings 功能啟用FSM Offerings Enablement

透過 Setup and Maintenance 啟用 Manufacturing and Supply Chain Management Offering，並 Opt-In 子功能如 Inventory、Procurement、Order Management。ABC Electronics 選擇啟用全部 SCM 功能以支援未來擴充。Enable the Manufacturing and Supply Chain Management Offering via Setup and Maintenance, then Opt-In sub-features like Inventory, Procurement, and Order Management. ABC Electronics opted in all SCM features to support future expansion.

🏢

企業組織階層Enterprise Org Hierarchy

五層架構：Legal Entity（ABC Electronics Taiwan Ltd.）→ Business Unit（台灣採購 BU）→ Inventory Org（TW-WH-01 台北倉）→ Subinventory（RAW-MAT 原料區）→ Locator（A-01-01 貨架）。每層都有不同的財務與操作控制。Five-tier structure: Legal Entity (ABC Electronics Taiwan Ltd.) → Business Unit (Taiwan Procurement BU) → Inventory Org (TW-WH-01 Taipei Warehouse) → Subinventory (RAW-MAT) → Locator (A-01-01 shelf). Each tier carries different financial and operational controls.

📦

品項主檔 (Item Master)Item Master

品項 "ABC-LAPTOP-15" 在 Item Master Org 建立後，指派到台北倉與上海廠兩個 Inventory Org，各自可以設定不同的存貨成本方式、最小採購量與安全庫存，但品號與描述全公司共用。Item "ABC-LAPTOP-15" is created in the Item Master Org, then assigned to both the Taipei and Shanghai Inventory Orgs. Each org can have different costing methods, minimum order quantities, and safety stock levels, while the item number and description are shared enterprise-wide.

📐

計量單位 (UOM) 與換算UOM & Conversions

筆記型電腦的 UOM 體系：Each（基本單位）→ 1 Dozen = 12 Each → 1 Carton = 6 Dozen = 72 Each → 1 Pallet = 20 Cartons = 1,440 Each。採購時用 Carton，庫存計量用 Each，帳務計算自動換算。Laptop UOM hierarchy: Each (base unit) → 1 Dozen = 12 Each → 1 Carton = 6 Dozen = 72 Each → 1 Pallet = 20 Cartons = 1,440 Each. Purchasing uses Carton, inventory counts use Each, and financials convert automatically.

🏷️

品項類別 (Item Class)Item Class

ABC Electronics 建立三個 Item Class：Electronics（序號追蹤、保固期管控）、Accessories（批次管理）、Packaging Material（無序號、先進先出）。Item Class 決定了哪些屬性頁籤可見，以及哪些欄位為必填。ABC Electronics creates three Item Classes: Electronics (serial number tracking, warranty control), Accessories (lot management), Packaging Material (no serial number, FIFO). Item Class controls which attribute tabs are visible and which fields are required.

🔄

生命週期階段 (Lifecycle Phase)Lifecycle Phase

ABC-LAPTOP-15 的生命週期：Draft（初建）→ Prototype（樣品測試）→ Production（量產，開放所有交易）→ End of Life（停止採購，仍可出貨庫存）→ Obsolete（完全停用，所有交易鎖定）。當前階段直接控制哪些 SCM 交易被允許。ABC-LAPTOP-15 lifecycle: Draft (initial) → Prototype (sample testing) → Production (mass production, all transactions open) → End of Life (stop purchasing, still ship existing stock) → Obsolete (fully retired, all transactions locked). Current phase directly controls which SCM transactions are permitted.

🔧 深入解析一：FSM Offerings 與 Opt-In 機制 🔧 Deep Dive 1: FSM Offerings and Opt-In Mechanism

▼

FSM（Functional Setup Manager）是 Oracle Fusion 的核心設定框架。每個「Offering」代表一個大功能領域，例如 Manufacturing and Supply Chain Management。在啟用 Offering 之後，你必須透過「Opt-In」機制選擇要啟用的子功能，未被 Opt-In 的功能不會出現在任何導覽選單中，相關的設定任務也不會被列在 Task List 裡。 FSM (Functional Setup Manager) is Oracle Fusion's core configuration framework. Each "Offering" represents a major functional area, such as Manufacturing and Supply Chain Management. After enabling an Offering, you must use the "Opt-In" mechanism to select which sub-features to activate. Features that are not Opted-In will not appear in any navigation menu, and their setup tasks will not be listed in the Task List.

具體範例：ABC Electronics 的 FSM 設定Concrete Example: ABC Electronics FSM Configuration

Offering / 功能Offering / Feature Opt-In 狀態Opt-In Status 原因說明Reason
Inventory Management ✓ 啟用 所有模組必要前提Required prerequisite for all modules
Procurement ✓ 啟用 採購請購、PO 處理Requisitions and PO processing
Order Management ✓ 啟用 客戶訂單出貨Customer order fulfillment
Manufacturing ✓ 啟用 上海廠工單管理Shanghai factory work orders
Cost Management ✓ 啟用 成本核算必要Required for cost accounting
Quality Management ✗ 暫不啟用 Phase 2 再導入Deferred to Phase 2

導航路徑：Setup and Maintenance → Offerings → Manufacturing and Supply Chain Management → Opt In Features → 勾選所需功能 → Save and Close Navigation Path: Setup and Maintenance → Offerings → Manufacturing and Supply Chain Management → Opt In Features → Check desired features → Save and Close

Opt-In 之後我還需要做什麼？ What do I need to do after Opt-In? ▶
Opt-In 只是「開啟功能開關」，你還需要進入 Task List 完成具體的設定任務。例如 Opt-In Inventory 後，你需要執行：① 建立 Inventory Organization、② 設定 Subinventory、③ 設定 Locator（如果需要）、④ 設定 Picking Rules 等。FSM 會為你列出所有必做任務（Required）與選做任務（Optional）。 Opt-In only "flips the feature switch." You still need to enter the Task List and complete specific setup tasks. For example, after Opting-In Inventory, you must: ① Create Inventory Organizations, ② Set up Subinventories, ③ Configure Locators (if needed), ④ Set up Picking Rules, etc. FSM lists all Required and Optional tasks for you.
可以之後再 Opt-In 新功能嗎？ Can I Opt-In new features later? ▶
可以。Opt-In 是可以隨時追加的。ABC Electronics 在 Phase 1 上線六個月後，回到 FSM Opt-In Quality Management，系統會立即在導覽選單中出現品質模組，並列出所有需要補設定的 Task。不過要注意：若有品項已完成大量交易，新增品質屬性時需要評估對現有資料的影響。 Yes. Opt-In can be added at any time. ABC Electronics returned to FSM after six months to Opt-In Quality Management for Phase 2. The quality module immediately appeared in the navigation menu with all required setup tasks listed. Note: if items already have extensive transaction history, adding quality attributes requires evaluating the impact on existing data.
⚠️
常見錯誤：跳過 Opt-In 直接設定Common Mistake: Skipping Opt-In and Setting Up Directly
許多新手直接在 Inventory 模組中建立倉庫，卻沒有先確認 Offering 是否正確 Opt-In。這會導致部分進階功能（如 Serial Number Tracking 或 Lot Control）的欄位根本不出現。正確做法是：先確認 FSM Opt-In → 確認 Task List → 再開始設定。 Many beginners directly create warehouses in the Inventory module without first verifying that the Offering is correctly Opted-In. This causes certain advanced feature fields (like Serial Number Tracking or Lot Control) to simply not appear. The correct approach is: confirm FSM Opt-In first → confirm Task List → then begin configuration.

🏢 深入解析二：企業組織架構階層 🏢 Deep Dive 2: Enterprise Organization Structure Hierarchy

▼

Oracle Fusion 的企業架構是嚴格的五層階層，每一層控制不同範圍的業務功能。理解這個階層是所有 SCM 設定的基礎——你後面設定的每一個品項、交易、採購單，都必須指定到某個層級的組織節點。 Oracle Fusion's enterprise structure is a strict five-tier hierarchy, with each tier controlling different scopes of business functions. Understanding this hierarchy is the foundation of all SCM configuration — every item, transaction, and purchase order you create later must be assigned to an organizational node at a specific tier.

ABC Electronics Taiwan 實際架構設計ABC Electronics Taiwan Real Architecture Design

層級Tier Oracle 名稱Oracle Name ABC Electronics 實例ABC Electronics Instance 控制範圍Controls
L1 Legal Entity ABC Electronics Taiwan Ltd. 法律、稅務、財報實體Legal, tax, financial reporting entity
L2 Business Unit (BU) 台灣採購 BU / 上海製造 BUTaiwan Procurement BU / Shanghai Manufacturing BU 採購、訂單、應付帳款控制Procurement, orders, AP control
L3 Inventory Organization TW-WH-01（台北倉）/ SH-FAC-01（上海廠） 庫存交易、成本核算範圍Inventory transactions, costing scope
L4 Subinventory RAW-MAT（原料區）/ FG-AREA（成品區）/ REJECT（不良品區） 品項存放分區、允收/保稅控制Item storage zones, receiving/bonded control
L5 Locator A-01-01（A 排第1列第1格） 精確貨架位置（揀貨路徑優化）Precise shelf location (pick path optimization)
💡
設計原則：Inventory Organization 是 SCM 交易的最小獨立單位。同一 Inventory Org 內的品項交易不需要「轉移訂單」，跨 Org 移動品項則必須建立 Internal Transfer Order，且會產生跨組織成本記錄。因此，規劃幾個 Inventory Org 是一個重要的業務決策。 Design Principle: Inventory Organization is the smallest independent unit for SCM transactions. Transactions within the same Inventory Org do not require a "Transfer Order," but moving items across Orgs requires an Internal Transfer Order and generates cross-org cost entries. Therefore, deciding how many Inventory Orgs to create is an important business decision.
Item Master Org 和一般 Inventory Org 有什麼差異？ What is the difference between Item Master Org and a regular Inventory Org? ▶
Item Master Org 是品項的「原籍」組織，存放品項的通用屬性（品號、描述、品項類別、UOM），這些屬性全公司共用，不能在各組織中各自修改。品項必須先在 Item Master Org 建立，再「指派」到各個 Inventory Org。被指派的 Inventory Org 可以設定組織層級的屬性（如安全庫存量、採購前置時間、成本方式），但不能修改 Master-level 欄位。ABC Electronics 指定 TW-MASTER 為品項主檔組織，台北倉 TW-WH-01 和上海廠 SH-FAC-01 都是被指派的目標組織。 Item Master Org is the item's "home" organization, storing generic attributes (item number, description, item class, UOM) that are shared enterprise-wide and cannot be independently modified by individual orgs. Items must first be created in the Item Master Org, then "assigned" to each Inventory Org. Assigned Inventory Orgs can configure org-level attributes (safety stock, procurement lead time, costing method) but cannot modify Master-level fields. ABC Electronics designated TW-MASTER as the Item Master Org; Taipei Warehouse TW-WH-01 and Shanghai Factory SH-FAC-01 are target assigned orgs.
上線後可以更改 Inventory Org 架構嗎？ Can I change the Inventory Org structure after go-live? ▶
這是最需要謹慎的問題。理論上可以，但實際上風險極高。如果 Inventory Org 已有庫存交易記錄（收貨、移轉、出貨等），要停用或合併 Org 需要：① 先清零所有庫存（Misc Issue 出帳）、② 關閉所有進行中的交易（PO、SO、Transfer Order）、③ 執行 Period Close、④ 再停用組織。許多企業在上線後才發現倉庫分法不合理，但因為交易量太大，實際上只能以「虛擬分區」（Subinventory）來彌補。因此：在 Go-Live 前必須確認組織架構設計的正確性。 This is the question requiring the most caution. Theoretically possible, but in practice extremely risky. If an Inventory Org already has inventory transaction history (receipts, transfers, shipments), deactivating or merging an Org requires: ① Zero out all inventory (Misc Issue write-off), ② Close all in-progress transactions (PO, SO, Transfer Orders), ③ Execute Period Close, ④ Then deactivate the org. Many companies realize their warehouse structure is wrong after go-live, but due to transaction volume, they can only compensate with "virtual zones" (Subinventories). Therefore: the org structure design must be confirmed correct before Go-Live.
⚠️
常見錯誤：Subinventory 設定為 Nettable = NoCommon Mistake: Setting Subinventory Nettable = No
如果一個 Subinventory 的 Nettable 設為 No，供應鏈計劃（GOP/Supply Planning）在計算可用庫存時會完全忽略這個區的庫存。ABC Electronics 曾將 REJECT（不良品區）誤設為 Nettable = Yes，導致計劃系統把待維修品算成可出貨庫存，造成客戶下單後才發現庫存不足。 If a Subinventory's Nettable flag is set to No, Supply Chain Planning (GOP/Supply Planning) will completely ignore inventory in that zone when calculating available stock. ABC Electronics once mistakenly set REJECT (defective goods area) to Nettable = Yes, causing the planning system to count items awaiting repair as shippable inventory, resulting in stock shortfalls discovered only after customers placed orders.

📦 深入解析三：品項主檔與品項類別 📦 Deep Dive 3: Item Master and Item Class

▼

品項主檔（Item Master）是 Oracle SCM 中所有品項資料的單一來源。每一個品項都有數百個屬性，分佈在多個頁籤中（General、Purchasing、Inventory、Manufacturing、Order Management、Costing 等）。品項類別（Item Class）決定哪些屬性頁籤可見，以及哪些欄位是必填的——這就是為什麼在建立品項前必須先設計好 Item Class。 The Item Master is the single source of truth for all item data in Oracle SCM. Each item has hundreds of attributes distributed across multiple tabs (General, Purchasing, Inventory, Manufacturing, Order Management, Costing, etc.). Item Class determines which attribute tabs are visible and which fields are required — this is why Item Class must be designed before creating items.

範例：ABC-LAPTOP-15 筆記型電腦主檔設定Example: ABC-LAPTOP-15 Laptop Item Master Configuration

屬性頁籤Attribute Tab 關鍵欄位Key Field ABC-LAPTOP-15 設定值ABC-LAPTOP-15 Value 業務影響Business Impact
General Item Class Electronics 決定可見屬性集合Determines visible attribute set
General Lifecycle Phase Production 允許所有採購/庫存/出貨交易Allows all purchase/inventory/shipping transactions
General Primary UOM Each 所有庫存計算基準Baseline for all inventory calculations
Inventory Serial Number Generation At Receipt 每台電腦收貨時自動指派 SNEach laptop auto-assigned SN at receipt
Inventory Safety Stock Quantity 50 Each (台北倉) 低於 50 台時觸發補貨計劃Triggers replenishment plan when below 50 units
Purchasing Min Order Quantity 10 Each PR 自動補足至最小採購量PR auto-adjusted to minimum order quantity
Purchasing Lead Time: Fixed Days 14 計劃系統倒推建議採購日期Planning system back-calculates suggested PO date
Costing Costing Method Standard 以標準成本計算庫存價值Inventory valued at standard cost
如果設定了錯誤的 Item Class 會發生什麼？ What happens if I set the wrong Item Class? ▶
Item Class 一旦設定並儲存後，無法直接更改。如果設錯，你需要：① 確認該品項沒有任何交易記錄（若有則無法改）、② 將品項停用（設為 Inactive）、③ 建立一個新品項，使用正確的 Item Class、④ 若有庫存，執行 Inventory Transfer 將庫存移轉到新品項。因此，Item Class 的設計必須在建立任何品項之前完成並確認。常見錯誤：把原物料設成 Finished Good Class，導致 BOM 和工單設定出現異常。 Once Item Class is set and saved, it cannot be directly changed. If set incorrectly, you must: ① Confirm the item has no transaction history (cannot change if it does), ② Deactivate the item (set to Inactive), ③ Create a new item with the correct Item Class, ④ If stock exists, execute an Inventory Transfer to move stock to the new item. Therefore, Item Class design must be completed and confirmed before any items are created. Common mistake: setting raw materials as Finished Good Class, causing abnormalities in BOM and work order configuration.
同一個品項在不同組織可以有不同的 UOM 嗎？ Can one item have different UOMs in different organizations? ▶
Primary UOM（主要計量單位）是在 Item Master Org 層級設定的，全公司統一，不能在各個 Inventory Org 中各自設定不同的 Primary UOM。但是，各個 Inventory Org 可以使用不同的「交易 UOM」——例如台北倉以 Each 收貨，上海廠以 Carton 收貨，系統會自動依照 UOM 換算表換算成 Primary UOM 記錄庫存。此外，採購 UOM、銷售 UOM 可以與 Primary UOM 不同，這些在品項主檔的 Purchasing / Order Management 頁籤中設定。 Primary UOM (primary unit of measure) is set at the Item Master Org level and is unified company-wide — it cannot be set differently for individual Inventory Orgs. However, each Inventory Org can use different "transaction UOMs" — for example, Taipei Warehouse receives in Each while Shanghai Factory receives in Carton, and the system automatically converts to Primary UOM using the UOM conversion table. Additionally, Purchasing UOM and Sales UOM can differ from Primary UOM — these are configured in the item's Purchasing / Order Management tabs.
⚠️
常見錯誤：沒有指派品項到目標 Inventory OrgCommon Mistake: Forgetting to Assign Items to Target Inventory Orgs
品項在 Item Master Org 建立後，不會自動出現在其他 Inventory Org 中。必須手動執行「指派到組織」（Assign to Organization）。ABC Electronics 曾發生台北倉的採購人員在建立 PO 時找不到品項，原因就是品項只在 TW-MASTER 建立，沒有指派到 TW-WH-01。導航路徑：Product Management → Items → Actions → Assign to Organizations After an item is created in the Item Master Org, it does NOT automatically appear in other Inventory Orgs. You must manually execute "Assign to Organization." ABC Electronics once had procurement staff unable to find items when creating POs because the item was only created in TW-MASTER and not assigned to TW-WH-01. Navigation: Product Management → Items → Actions → Assign to Organizations

📐 深入解析四：計量單位 (UOM) 體系與包裝字串 📐 Deep Dive 4: Unit of Measure (UOM) System and Packaging String

▼

UOM（Unit of Measure）設定是所有數量計算的基礎。Oracle Fusion 使用「UOM 換算表」將各種計量單位相互連結，確保採購用 Carton、生產用 Each、出貨用 Pallet 時，系統的庫存數量始終保持一致。錯誤的 UOM 換算會造成庫存數量異常、成本計算錯誤，甚至影響財報。 UOM (Unit of Measure) configuration is the foundation of all quantity calculations. Oracle Fusion uses a "UOM Conversion Table" to link various units, ensuring that when procurement uses Carton, production uses Each, and shipping uses Pallet, the system's inventory quantities always remain consistent. Incorrect UOM conversions cause inventory quantity discrepancies, cost calculation errors, and can even affect financial statements.

ABC Electronics 筆記型電腦 UOM 換算矩陣ABC Electronics Laptop UOM Conversion Matrix

UOM Each Dozen Carton Pallet 使用場景Usage Scenario
Each Primary 1 0.0833 0.01389 0.000694 庫存計量、成本核算、序號追蹤Inventory count, costing, serial tracking
Dozen 12 1 0.1667 0.00833 配件類採購Accessory purchasing
Carton 72 6 1 0.05 電腦主機採購、收貨Laptop purchasing and receiving
Pallet 1440 120 20 1 整板出貨、倉庫空間管理Full-pallet shipping, warehouse space management
✅
實際計算範例Practical Calculation Example
採購部門以 5 Cartons 下 PO，收貨後系統自動換算：5 Cartons × 72 Each/Carton = 360 Each 入庫到台北倉。帳務以 NT$30,000/Each 標準成本計算：360 × 30,000 = NT$10,800,000 庫存價值。 Procurement places a PO for 5 Cartons. After receiving, the system auto-converts: 5 Cartons × 72 Each/Carton = 360 Each added to Taipei Warehouse inventory. Financials calculate at NT$30,000/Each standard cost: 360 × 30,000 = NT$10,800,000 inventory value.

包裝字串 (Packaging String) — 多層包裝架構Packaging String — Multi-Level Packaging Structure

Packaging String 是一個更進階的功能，用於定義品項的多層包裝結構。ABC Electronics 的筆記型電腦包裝字串定義為：1 Pallet = 20 Cartons, 1 Carton = 6 Dozens, 1 Dozen = 12 Each。系統用此資訊自動計算所需的包材用量（外箱、棧板貼紙等），並在 WMS 揀貨時建議使用整箱揀貨以提升效率。 Packaging String is an advanced feature that defines an item's multi-level packaging structure. ABC Electronics defines the laptop packaging string as: 1 Pallet = 20 Cartons, 1 Carton = 6 Dozens, 1 Dozen = 12 Each. The system uses this to automatically calculate required packaging materials (carton labels, pallet stickers, etc.) and suggests case-pick in WMS to improve efficiency.

UOM 換算只能設置固定比例嗎？可以設小數嗎？ Can UOM conversions only be fixed ratios? Can I use decimals? ▶
Oracle Fusion 支援小數點 UOM 換算，最多可以到小數點後 6 位。例如你可以定義 1 Kg = 2.20462 Pound。但要特別注意：如果換算比例的小數位數太多，在大量計算時可能產生微小的四捨五入差異，累積後會造成庫存帳面與實際不符。建議儘量使用整數比例，或確認換算精度是否足夠。 Oracle Fusion supports decimal UOM conversions up to 6 decimal places. For example, you can define 1 Kg = 2.20462 Pound. However, note: if the conversion ratio has too many decimal places, large-volume calculations may produce minor rounding differences that accumulate into inventory discrepancies. It is recommended to use whole-number ratios whenever possible, or confirm that the conversion precision is sufficient.
⚠️
常見錯誤：採購 UOM 與庫存 UOM 不一致導致系統拒絕交易Common Mistake: Purchasing UOM vs. Inventory UOM Mismatch Causes Transaction Rejection
如果你在採購品項屬性設定 Purchasing UOM = Carton，但忘記在 UOM 換算表中建立 Carton → Each 的換算關係，系統在建立 PO 時會報錯「UOM conversion not found」。解決方法：Setup and Maintenance → Manage Units of Measure Conversions → 新增 Carton → Each 的換算規則。 If you set Purchasing UOM = Carton in the item's purchasing attributes but forget to create the Carton → Each conversion in the UOM Conversion Table, the system will throw an error "UOM conversion not found" when creating a PO. Solution: Setup and Maintenance → Manage Units of Measure Conversions → Add the Carton → Each conversion rule.

🔄 深入解析五：品項生命週期階段控制 🔄 Deep Dive 5: Item Lifecycle Phase Control

▼

Lifecycle Phase（生命週期階段）直接控制品項在各個業務模組中可執行的交易類型。這是一個非常強大的控制機制——例如你可以設定「End of Life」階段的品項禁止新採購，但仍可以出貨現有庫存，這樣就能在不封存品項的情況下，自然地結清庫存。 Lifecycle Phase directly controls which transaction types can be performed for an item across all business modules. This is a powerful control mechanism — for example, you can configure "End of Life" phase items to prohibit new purchasing while still allowing shipment of existing stock, enabling natural inventory rundown without archiving the item.

生命週期階段Lifecycle Phase 採購 POPurchase PO 庫存移轉Inventory Transfer 工單生產Work Order 客戶出貨Customer Shipment ABC 範例ABC Example
Draft ✗✗✗✗ 品項資料輸入中Data entry in progress
Prototype ✗✓✓✗ 樣品試產，不對外銷售Sample production, no external sales
Production ✓✓✓✓ ABC-LAPTOP-15 目前狀態ABC-LAPTOP-15 current status
End of Life ✗✓✗✓ 舊款清倉，不採購不生產Clearance, no purchasing or production
Obsolete ✗✗✗✗ 完全停用，所有交易鎖定Fully retired, all transactions locked
✅
最佳實踐：ABC Electronics 的品項管理流程規定，所有新品必須在 Prototype 階段完成至少 3 批次試產並通過品質驗收，才能由 PLM 工程師將 Lifecycle Phase 改為 Production。這樣可以防止未驗證的品項出現在正式採購和銷售訂單中。 Best Practice: ABC Electronics' item management process requires all new products to complete at least 3 prototype production batches and pass quality acceptance in the Prototype phase before a PLM engineer can change the Lifecycle Phase to Production. This prevents unvalidated items from appearing in official purchase and sales orders.

📋 端對端案例：ABC Electronics Taiwan 導入實錄 📋 End-to-End Case Study: ABC Electronics Taiwan Implementation Record

▼

以下是 ABC Electronics Taiwan 在 Oracle SCM Cloud 導入第一週的完整基礎建置流程，包含真實的設定值與遭遇的問題。 The following is ABC Electronics Taiwan's complete foundation setup process during the first week of Oracle SCM Cloud implementation, including real configuration values and issues encountered.

Day 1-2：啟用 FSM OfferingsDay 1-2: Enable FSM Offerings

顧問登入 Setup and Maintenance，找到 Manufacturing and Supply Chain Management Offering，執行 Opt-In：選擇 Inventory Management、Procurement、Order Management、Manufacturing、Cost Management 共 5 個功能。完成後，系統生成 347 個 Setup Tasks（其中 Required 任務 89 個）。 Consultants logged into Setup and Maintenance, located the Manufacturing and Supply Chain Management Offering, and executed Opt-In: selecting Inventory Management, Procurement, Order Management, Manufacturing, and Cost Management — 5 features total. Afterward, the system generated 347 Setup Tasks (89 Required tasks).

Day 3-4：建立企業架構Day 3-4: Build Enterprise Structure

💡
建立順序（必須嚴格遵守）：
1. 建立 Legal Entity：ABC Electronics Taiwan Ltd.（稅籍號碼：12345678）
2. 建立 Business Units：TW-PROC-BU（台灣採購）、SH-MFG-BU（上海製造）
3. 建立 Item Master Org：TW-MASTER（不做任何庫存交易，只管品項主檔）
4. 建立 Inventory Org：TW-WH-01（台北倉，Nettable）、SH-FAC-01（上海廠）
5. 建立 Subinventory：TW-WH-01 下設 RAW-MAT、FG-AREA、REJECT 三個分區
6. 建立 Locator：RAW-MAT 下設 A-01-01 至 A-20-10 共 200 個儲位 Creation sequence (must be strictly followed):
1. Create Legal Entity: ABC Electronics Taiwan Ltd. (Tax ID: 12345678)
2. Create Business Units: TW-PROC-BU (Taiwan Procurement), SH-MFG-BU (Shanghai Manufacturing)
3. Create Item Master Org: TW-MASTER (no inventory transactions, manages item master only)
4. Create Inventory Orgs: TW-WH-01 (Taipei Warehouse, Nettable), SH-FAC-01 (Shanghai Factory)
5. Create Subinventories: RAW-MAT, FG-AREA, REJECT under TW-WH-01
6. Create Locators: 200 locators A-01-01 through A-20-10 under RAW-MAT

Day 5-6：設定 UOM 體系Day 5-6: Configure UOM System

在 Setup and Maintenance → Manage Units of Measure 中建立 UOM Class「Count」，包含 Each（基礎）、Dozen、Carton、Pallet。接著在 Manage Units of Measure Conversions 中建立換算關係：Dozen = 12 Each、Carton = 72 Each、Pallet = 1440 Each。遭遇問題：第一次測試收貨時發現 Carton 換算錯誤（設成了 60 Each 而非 72），導致 5 Carton 收貨只入帳 300 Each（少了 60 Each）。立即修正換算比例，並對已入帳的 300 Each 執行 Miscellaneous Receipt 補帳 60 Each。 Under Setup and Maintenance → Manage Units of Measure, created UOM Class "Count" containing Each (base), Dozen, Carton, Pallet. Then in Manage Units of Measure Conversions, created conversion relationships: Dozen = 12 Each, Carton = 72 Each, Pallet = 1440 Each. Issue encountered: During the first test receipt, the Carton conversion was found incorrect (set to 60 Each instead of 72), causing 5 Cartons to receive only 300 Each (missing 60 Each). The conversion was immediately corrected, and a Miscellaneous Receipt was executed to add the missing 60 Each to the already-posted 300 Each.

Day 7-8：建立品項主檔Day 7-8: Create Item Master

建立 3 個 Item Class：Electronics、Accessories、Packaging Material。接著在 TW-MASTER 建立第一個品項 ABC-LAPTOP-15，設定所有屬性，並指派到 TW-WH-01 和 SH-FAC-01。完成後，採購部門成功在 TW-WH-01 建立了第一張採購訂單，倉儲部門也成功執行了第一筆測試收貨，確認整個基礎架構正確運作。 Created 3 Item Classes: Electronics, Accessories, Packaging Material. Then created the first item ABC-LAPTOP-15 in TW-MASTER with all attributes configured and assigned to TW-WH-01 and SH-FAC-01. Upon completion, the procurement team successfully created the first purchase order in TW-WH-01, and the warehouse team successfully executed the first test receipt, confirming the entire foundation architecture was functioning correctly.

🔑
案例關鍵學習Key Case Study Lessons
① UOM 換算一定要在第一次交易前測試驗證；② Subinventory 的 Nettable 屬性影響供應計劃，必須按業務需求設定；③ 品項在 Master Org 建立後，記得指派到所有需要的 Inventory Org；④ 整個基礎建置應預留至少 2 週時間，不要壓縮。 ① UOM conversions must be tested and verified before the first transaction; ② Subinventory Nettable attribute affects supply planning and must be set per business requirements; ③ After creating items in Master Org, remember to assign to all required Inventory Orgs; ④ Allow at least 2 weeks for complete foundation setup — do not compress this timeline.

常見問題 FAQ

Frequently Asked Questions

Q1：上線後可以更改 Inventory Org 架構嗎？ Q1: Can I change the Inventory Org structure after go-live? ▶
技術上可以，但業務上風險極高。如果要停用一個已有交易的 Inventory Org，你必須：① 清零所有庫存（需要 Miscellaneous Issue 帳務出帳）；② 關閉所有進行中的 PO、SO、Transfer Order；③ 完成當前會計期間的 Period Close；④ 才能將 Org 設為 Inactive。實務上，很多客戶在上線後發現組織設計不合理，但交易量太大無法重新設計，只好以增加 Subinventory 來模擬需要的分區。建議：導入前必須花足夠時間做組織架構設計，最好邀請業務部門一起確認。 Technically possible, but the business risk is extremely high. To deactivate an Inventory Org that already has transactions, you must: ① Zero out all inventory (requires Miscellaneous Issue accounting write-offs); ② Close all in-progress POs, SOs, and Transfer Orders; ③ Complete Period Close for the current accounting period; ④ Only then can you set the Org to Inactive. In practice, many customers discover their org design is flawed post-go-live but cannot redesign due to transaction volume, and instead add Subinventories to simulate the needed zones. Recommendation: Invest sufficient time in org structure design before implementation, ideally with business stakeholders participating in the confirmation.
Q2：Item Master Org 和一般 Inventory Org 的差異是什麼？ Q2: What is the difference between Item Master Org and a regular Inventory Org? ▶
Item Master Org 是品項的「主資料管理中心」，只有在這裡建立的品項才能被指派到其他組織。它通常不執行任何庫存交易（不收貨、不發貨），純粹用於管理品項屬性。在 Manage Inventory Organization 中建立 Item Master Org 時，你要將其設為「Item Master Organization」角色。

一般 Inventory Org 是實際發生庫存交易的地方（台北倉 TW-WH-01），品項必須先「指派」到這個 Org 才能在這裡執行收貨、出貨、盤點等操作。你可以在組織層級覆寫某些屬性（安全庫存、前置時間），但 Master 層級屬性（品號、描述、UOM）無法修改。

簡單記憶法：Item Master Org = 品項的戶籍；Inventory Org = 品項的居住地。 Item Master Org is the item's "master data management center" — only items created here can be assigned to other organizations. It typically does not execute any inventory transactions (no receipts, no shipments) and is purely for managing item attributes. When creating an Item Master Org in Manage Inventory Organization, you designate it with the "Item Master Organization" role.

Regular Inventory Org is where actual inventory transactions occur (Taipei Warehouse TW-WH-01). Items must first be "assigned" to this Org before receipts, shipments, and cycle counts can be executed there. You can override certain attributes at the org level (safety stock, lead time), but Master-level attributes (item number, description, UOM) cannot be modified.

Simple memory aid: Item Master Org = item's registered address; Inventory Org = item's current residence.
Q3：同一個品項在不同組織可以有不同的 UOM 嗎？ Q3: Can one item have different UOMs in different organizations? ▶
Primary UOM（庫存主計量單位）是 Master-level 屬性，全公司統一，不可以在各組織中設定不同值。

但是，各組織可以在交易時使用不同的 UOM：
• 採購時在 PO 上選擇 Carton，系統自動換算為 Each 入庫
• 銷售時在 SO 上選擇 Dozen，系統自動換算為 Each 出庫
• 生產時在工單 BOM 中使用 Each

重點：帳面庫存永遠以 Primary UOM 記錄，其他 UOM 只是「顯示用途」的換算呈現。這確保了全公司的庫存數量統一可比。 Primary UOM (primary inventory unit of measure) is a Master-level attribute that is unified company-wide — it cannot be set differently for individual organizations.

However, organizations can use different UOMs when performing transactions:
• Purchasing: select Carton on PO, system auto-converts to Each for inventory entry
• Sales: select Dozen on SO, system auto-converts to Each for inventory reduction
• Manufacturing: use Each in work order BOM

Key point: On-hand inventory is always recorded in Primary UOM. Other UOMs are merely "display-purpose" converted presentations. This ensures inventory quantities are consistently comparable across the entire company.
Q4：設定了錯誤的 Item Class 會怎樣？有辦法改嗎？ Q4: What happens if I set the wrong Item Class? Can it be changed? ▶
Item Class 建立並儲存後無法直接更改。錯誤的 Item Class 影響包括：
• 某些必要屬性欄位不出現（例如序號欄位未顯示）
• 某些不應有的屬性被設為必填（例如批次欄位強制填寫）
• BOM 或工藝路線設定出現異常

補救方法（無交易記錄時）：
① 將錯誤品項設為 Inactive；② 建立新品項選擇正確 Item Class；③ 確認沒有 PO/SO 引用舊品號後刪除舊品項。

補救方法（已有交易記錄時）：
情況複雜，可能需要建立新品項 + 庫存移轉 + 歷史 PO/SO 修改（若尚未關閉）。建議在導入初期就用測試品項驗證每個 Item Class 的屬性設定是否符合業務需求。 Item Class cannot be directly changed after being created and saved. Incorrect Item Class impacts include:
• Certain required attribute fields do not appear (e.g., serial number field missing)
• Certain inappropriate attributes become required (e.g., lot fields forced mandatory)
• BOM or routing configuration behaves abnormally

Remediation (no transaction history):
① Set incorrect item to Inactive; ② Create new item with correct Item Class; ③ After confirming no PO/SO references the old item number, delete the old item.

Remediation (transaction history exists):
Situation is complex — may require creating a new item + inventory transfer + modifying historical PO/SO (if not yet closed). It is recommended to use test items during early implementation to validate that each Item Class's attribute configuration meets business requirements.

模組 1：庫存管理 Module 1: Inventory Management

追蹤物料在組織內的移動、數量與補貨，是所有物料流的核心中繼站 Track material movement, quantities, and replenishment — the central hub of all physical material flows

🔑
業務場景：聯合食品電子集團Business Scenario: United FoodTech Group
一家橫跨食品製造與消費電子的跨國集團，在同一個 Oracle Cloud 實例上管理兩個截然不同的業務線。 A multinational group spanning food manufacturing and consumer electronics, managing two fundamentally different product lines on a single Oracle Cloud instance.

聯合食品電子集團（United FoodTech Group）旗下食品事業部「鮮途乳業」每月生產 200 噸鮮乳製品，每批次都有嚴格的效期規範——一旦 FEFO（先效期先出）沒有落實，過期品流入市場不僅面臨食安罰款，還可能召回整條生產線。過去使用傳統 ERP，倉庫人員靠手寫批號卡片追蹤效期，每次盤點要花整整三天，而且常常發現有效期只剩 5 天的產品被壓在最底層，損耗率高達 4.8%。 United FoodTech Group's food division, "FreshPath Dairy," produces 200 tonnes of fresh dairy products monthly, with strict expiry compliance per batch. Without rigorous FEFO (First Expired, First Out) enforcement, expired goods reaching market trigger food-safety fines and full production-line recalls. Under their legacy ERP, warehouse staff tracked expiry with handwritten lot cards — cycle counts took three full days, and products with only 5 days of shelf life were routinely found buried at the bottom of shelves. Spoilage ran at 4.8%.

同集團的電子事業部「閃芯科技」則面對截然不同的挑戰：每台出廠的筆記型電腦都需要序號追蹤，從製造工單、倉庫移轉到最終交貨給客戶，保固期間若發生維修退換，必須能即時查到該機器的完整履歷。舊系統序號管理全靠 Excel，每季稽核時都要耗費一週進行人工比對，錯誤率約 2%，導致保固理賠糾紛頻繁。 The group's electronics division, "FlashCore Tech," faced entirely different challenges: every laptop leaving the factory required serial-number tracking — from manufacturing work orders through warehouse transfers to final customer delivery. Warranty repairs needed instant access to a unit's complete history. Their old system managed serial numbers entirely in Excel; quarterly audits consumed a full week of manual reconciliation with a ~2% error rate, generating constant warranty-claim disputes.

導入 Oracle Fusion Cloud Inventory Management 後，兩個事業部共用同一套系統卻各自維持獨立的庫存組織。鮮途乳業透過「批號控制 + FEFO 揀貨 + 週期盤點（ABC 分類）」將損耗率降至 0.9%，並能在 30 秒內完成任一批次的追溯報告。閃芯科技則以「序號控制 + 製造交易整合 + 組織間轉移」建立完整序號履歷，保固查詢從一週縮短為 10 秒。本模組將帶你逐步了解這套系統背後的核心機制。 After deploying Oracle Fusion Cloud Inventory Management, both divisions share one instance yet maintain independent inventory organizations. FreshPath Dairy uses Lot Control + FEFO picking + Cycle Count (ABC classification) to bring spoilage down to 0.9%, with full lot-traceability reports available in 30 seconds. FlashCore Tech leverages Serial Number Control + manufacturing transaction integration + inter-org transfers to build complete unit histories, reducing warranty lookups from one week to 10 seconds. This module walks you through the core mechanisms powering these outcomes.

核心功能

Key Features

🔁

庫存交易類型Transaction Types

涵蓋收料、發料、調撥、調整、WIP 領料 15+ 種交易，每筆交易自動過帳至 SLA 規則對應的總帳科目。例：工單 WO-2024-0821 領用 Widget A 50 個 → 自動借記 WIP 物料科目。15+ transaction types: Receipt, Issue, Transfer, Adjustment, WIP Pick. Each auto-posts to GL via SLA rules. E.g., Work Order WO-2024-0821 issues 50 units of Widget A → auto-debits WIP Material account.

📉

Min-Max 補貨計劃Min-Max Replenishment

設定最低/最高庫存水位，低於最低時自動產生請購單。例：Widget A 最低 500、最高 1000，現有 450 → 系統建議採購 550 單位，PR 自動帶入供應商與交期。Set Min/Max stock levels; drops below Min trigger auto-PR. E.g., Widget A Min=500, Max=1000, stock=450 → system generates PR for 550 units, auto-populated with vendor and lead time.

🏥

PAR 補貨（定點補充）PAR Level Replenishment

適合醫院或門市的定點自動補充模式。例：手術室 OR-3 的無菌手套 PAR=50，每日清晨掃描現有 18 雙 → 系統自動補 32 雙至中央倉庫揀貨任務。Point-of-use auto top-up for hospitals or retail. E.g., OR-3 sterile gloves PAR=50, morning scan finds 18 on hand → system auto-creates replenishment pick for 32 units from central storeroom.

🗂️

ABC 週期盤點ABC Cycle Count

依物料價值分 A/B/C 類，設定不同盤點頻率。A 類（高價值）每月一次、B 類每季一次、C 類每年一次，自動產生盤點任務與差異調整審核流程。Classify items A/B/C by value; assign different count frequencies. A-class (high value) monthly, B-class quarterly, C-class annually. Auto-generates count tasks and variance-approval workflows.

🧪

批號控制（Lot Control）Lot Number Control

食品/醫藥業必備，記錄批號來源、效期、製造日。例：鮮途乳業 LOT-20240915-A 全脂鮮奶，效期 2024/09/22，系統強制 FEFO 出庫，確保最近效期先出。Essential for food/pharma — captures lot origin, expiry, manufacture date. E.g., FreshPath LOT-20240915-A whole milk, expiry 2024/09/22; system enforces FEFO to guarantee earliest-expiry lots ship first.

💻

序號控制（Serial Control）Serial Number Control

電子/醫療設備逐台追蹤。例：閃芯科技筆電 SN-FCT-000823 從製造工單 → 倉庫收料 → 組織間調撥 → 客戶交貨，每個環節時間戳記完整保存，保固查詢 10 秒出結果。Unit-level tracking for electronics/medical devices. E.g., FlashCore laptop SN-FCT-000823: Manufacturing WO → Warehouse Receipt → Inter-org Transfer → Customer Delivery — every touchpoint time-stamped; warranty lookup returns in 10 seconds.

🔁 庫存交易類型詳解🔁 Inventory Transaction Types — Deep Dive

▼

Oracle Fusion Inventory 的每一筆交易都會自動觸發兩件事：①更新子庫存帳（Subinventory）的現有量，②透過 SLA（Subledger Accounting）規則產生財務憑證過帳至總帳。了解每種交易類型的觸發時機與過帳邏輯，是正確設定系統的基礎。 Every Oracle Fusion Inventory transaction automatically does two things: ① updates on-hand quantity in the Subinventory, and ② generates a financial journal entry via SLA (Subledger Accounting) rules and posts to GL. Understanding when to use each transaction type and its accounting impact is the foundation of correct system setup.

主要交易類型一覽Primary Transaction Types

交易類型Transaction Type 觸發情境When to Use 庫存影響Inventory Impact 會計處理Accounting
Receipt 收料Receipt PO 到貨、退貨退倉PO delivery, RMA return 現有量 ↑On-hand ↑ 借：庫存；貸：應計負債Dr Inventory / Cr Accrual
Issue 發料Issue 工單領料、銷售出貨WO pick, sales shipment 現有量 ↓On-hand ↓ 借：銷貨成本；貸：庫存Dr COGS / Cr Inventory
Transfer 調撥Transfer 子庫間移動、組織間調撥Sub-inv move, inter-org 來源 ↓ / 目的 ↑Source ↓ / Dest ↑ 同組織內不過帳；跨組織走在途庫存Intra-org: no GL; Inter-org: In-Transit
Adjustment 調整Adjustment 盤點差異、損耗認列Count variance, spoilage 增加或減少現有量Increase or decrease on-hand 借/貸：庫存調整科目Dr/Cr Inventory Adjustment
WIP Issue 工單自動發料Auto-issue to work order 現有量 ↓On-hand ↓ 借：WIP 物料科目；貸：庫存Dr WIP Material / Cr Inventory
WIP Completion 製成品完工入庫Finished goods receipt from WO 成品庫存 ↑FG inventory ↑ 借：庫存；貸：WIP 完工科目Dr Inventory / Cr WIP Completion
💡
具體案例：閃芯科技工單 WO-FCT-2024-0821Concrete Example: FlashCore WO-FCT-2024-0821
工單生產 100 台筆電。① WIP Issue：從「原料倉-A1」發料主機板 100 片（On-hand -100）。② WIP Completion：完工 100 台筆電入「成品倉-FG」（On-hand +100），每台自動指派序號 SN-FCT-000801 ~ SN-FCT-000900。 Work order produces 100 laptops. ① WIP Issue: 100 motherboards issued from "Raw-A1" (on-hand -100). ② WIP Completion: 100 laptops received into "FG" sub-inventory (on-hand +100), each auto-assigned serials SN-FCT-000801 through SN-FCT-000900.
組織間調撥（Inter-org Transfer）vs. 出貨/收料（Ship/Receive）何時用哪個？When to use Inter-org Transfer vs. Ship/Receive?▶

同一法律實體、相鄰廠區間移動物料，用「組織間調撥（Inter-org Transfer）」——系統建立在途庫存（In-Transit），接收端確認後完成。帳務走內部調撥科目，不產生應收/應付。Same legal entity, adjacent plants: use Inter-org Transfer — system creates In-Transit inventory; destination confirms to complete. Accounting uses internal transfer accounts; no AR/AP generated.

不同法律實體、或需要產生 PO/SO 憑證時，用「內部訂單（Internal Order）→ 出貨 → 收料」流程：Source Org 建內部 SO → Shipping → In-Transit → Destination Org 發 Internal PO 收料。帳務走銷售收入與採購成本，適合集團內部轉售。Different legal entities, or when PO/SO documents are required: use Internal Order → Shipment → Receipt: Source Org creates internal SO → ships → In-Transit → Destination Org receives via Internal PO. Accounting uses sales revenue and purchase cost accounts — suitable for intercompany resale.

✅
快速判斷：需要 AP/AR 分錄 → Ship/Receive；只是移動物料 → Inter-org Transfer。Quick rule: need AP/AR entries → Ship/Receive; just moving stock → Inter-org Transfer.
可以做負庫存調整嗎？Can I do a negative inventory adjustment?▶

可以，但需要特別授權。在 Oracle Fusion 中，負庫存調整（Negative Adjustment）需要設定「允許負數現有量（Allow Negative Balances）」參數在庫存組織層級開啟，且操作者需要 INV_ADJUST_INVENTORY 權限。常見場景：① 盤點後數量少於帳面（發現損耗）；② 緊急退料但系統數量已為 0。Yes, but it requires special authorization. In Oracle Fusion, negative adjustments require the "Allow Negative Balances" parameter enabled at the Inventory Organization level, and the user needs the INV_ADJUST_INVENTORY privilege. Common scenarios: ① Count reveals fewer units than system shows (spoilage); ② Emergency return but system quantity already reads 0.

⚠️
負調整會使庫存餘額為負值，影響成本計算（平均成本法可能計算出異常單位成本）。建議在月結前確認所有負庫存並修正，避免財務報表異常。Negative adjustments drive on-hand below zero, affecting cost calculations (average costing may produce abnormal unit costs). Confirm and resolve all negative balances before period close to avoid financial reporting anomalies.
⚠️
常見錯誤：交易來源設定錯誤Common Mistake: Wrong Transaction Source Type
手動發料時若誤選「Miscellaneous Issue」而非「WIP Issue」，系統不會連結工單，導致工單成本計算錯誤，且後續完工結帳時差異科目無法自動沖轉。 If you manually select "Miscellaneous Issue" instead of "WIP Issue," the transaction won't link to the work order. This corrupts WO cost accounting, and the variance account cannot auto-reverse at WO completion.

📉 Min-Max 補貨計劃詳解📉 Min-Max Replenishment Planning — Deep Dive

▼

Min-Max 是 Oracle Fusion Inventory 內建的簡易補貨方法，適合品項數量少、需求穩定的物料。系統依排程（通常為每日一次）掃描每個子庫存的現有量，一旦低於最低量（Min），立即產生採購請購單（PR）或內部申請單，補至最高量（Max）。 Min-Max is Oracle Fusion Inventory's built-in lightweight replenishment method, ideal for items with a small catalog and stable demand. The system scans each subinventory's on-hand quantity on a scheduled basis (typically daily); whenever on-hand drops below Min, it immediately generates a Purchase Requisition (PR) or internal request to replenish up to Max.

計算公式與實例Calculation Formula & Example

💡
Widget A 補貨計算（完整範例）Widget A Replenishment Calculation (Full Example)
參數Parameter 設定值Value Set 說明Notes
最低量 MinMin Qty500低於此值觸發補貨Triggers replenishment when below
最高量 MaxMax Qty1,000補貨目標上限Replenishment target ceiling
現有量On-hand450低於 Min → 觸發Below Min → triggers
建議採購量Suggested PR Qty550Max (1,000) − On-hand (450) = 550
最小採購量Fixed Lot Size100若設定，採購量取整為 600If set, PR rounds up to 600

結果：系統自動建立 PR，物料 Widget A，數量 600（取整為最小採購量），供應商來自物料主檔首選來源，交期依採購前置時間計算。Result: System auto-creates PR for Widget A, quantity 600 (rounded to fixed lot size of 100), vendor pulled from item's preferred source, need-by date calculated from purchasing lead time.

Min-Max 設定路徑Oracle Navigation Path

Inventory Management → Setup → Organizations → Manage Min-Max Planning Parameters
或：供應鏈執行 → 庫存 → 物料 → 維護物料補貨點（Item → Inventory tab → Min/Max Qty） Or: SCM → Inventory → Items → Manage Items → Inventory tab → Min/Max Qty fields

Min-Max 與供應鏈計劃（Supply Planning）如何互動？How does Min-Max interact with Supply Planning?▶

兩者是互斥且互補的補貨策略：They are mutually exclusive yet complementary replenishment strategies:

  • Min-Max：Inventory 模組內建，無需 Supply Planning 授權。適合 C 類低價值、需求平穩的物料（如辦公用品、MRO 備品）。Min-Max: Built into Inventory module, no Supply Planning license needed. Best for C-class low-value, stable-demand items (e.g., office supplies, MRO spares).
  • Supply Planning（MRP/MPS）：依銷售預測、生產計劃動態計算需求，考慮前置時間、批量、替代料。適合 A/B 類高價值、需求波動大的物料。Supply Planning (MRP/MPS): Dynamically calculates demand from sales forecasts and production plans, factoring in lead times, lot sizes, and substitutes. Best for A/B-class high-value, demand-variable items.
✅
建議：同一物料不要同時開啟 Min-Max 和 MRP，否則會產生重複的補貨建議。在物料主檔 → 計劃方法（Planning Method）欄位設定其中一種即可。Recommendation: don't enable both Min-Max and MRP for the same item — duplicate replenishment suggestions will result. Set only one in the item master → Planning Method field.
⚠️
常見錯誤：Min 大於 MaxCommon Mistake: Min Set Greater Than Max
若設定 Min=600、Max=500，Min-Max 計劃程式永遠不會觸發補貨（因為現有量不可能同時低於 600 又補至 500 以上）。系統不會報錯，但結果是永遠缺料。設定後請執行「Run Min-Max Planning」確認輸出報告有產生 PR。 If Min=600 and Max=500, the Min-Max planning program will never trigger replenishment (on-hand can never be below 600 while also targeting 500). The system won't error, but the result is perpetual stockout. After setup, run "Run Min-Max Planning" and confirm the output report shows generated PRs.

🏥 PAR 補貨（定點補充）詳解🏥 PAR Level Replenishment — Deep Dive

▼

PAR（Periodic Automatic Replenishment）是針對固定消耗點（Point-of-Use）的補貨模式，廣泛用於醫院、航空 MRO、餐廳廚房等場景。與 Min-Max 不同，PAR 以「定點補滿」為邏輯：每次盤點後，系統計算「PAR 水位 − 現有量 = 補貨量」，並直接發出補貨任務（揀貨 → 送達指定貨位）。 PAR (Periodic Automatic Replenishment) is a point-of-use replenishment model widely used in hospitals, aviation MRO, and restaurant kitchens. Unlike Min-Max, PAR uses a "top-up to level" logic: after each count, the system calculates PAR Level − On-Hand = Replenishment Qty, then issues a replenishment pick task (pick from main storeroom → deliver to point-of-use location).

醫院場景完整範例Hospital Scenario — Full Example

1. 設定：手術室 OR-3，無菌手套 PAR=50 雙1. Setup: OR-3, Sterile Gloves PAR=50 pairs
▶
2. 每日 06:00：護士長掃描現有量 = 18 雙2. Daily 06:00: Nurse scans current on-hand = 18 pairs
▶
3. 系統計算：50 − 18 = 32 雙 → 自動建立補貨任務3. System calculates: 50 − 18 = 32 pairs → auto-creates replenishment task
▶
4. 中央倉庫揀貨員收到任務：從 A-3-2 貨位揀 32 雙4. Central storeroom picker receives task: pick 32 pairs from bin A-3-2
▶
5. 確認送達 OR-3：現有量恢復為 50 雙5. Delivery confirmed to OR-3: on-hand restored to 50 pairs
✅
PAR 補貨來源可設定為「同組織子庫（Subinventory）」或「外部採購」。醫院通常以中央藥局為來源子庫，零售門市則可設定觸發採購訂單補充至門市倉。 PAR replenishment source can be set to "same-org subinventory" or "external purchase." Hospitals typically source from the central pharmacy subinventory; retail stores can configure PAR to trigger a purchase order replenishing the store stockroom.
⚠️
常見錯誤：PAR 水位設定過高造成過量積壓Common Mistake: PAR Level Too High Causing Overstock
PAR 水位應以「平均每日用量 × 補貨週期天數 × 安全係數」計算，而非主觀設定一個「安全的大數字」。例如無菌手套日均用量 8 雙、補貨週期 2 天、安全係數 1.5 → PAR = 8×2×1.5 = 24 雙，而非隨意設 50。過高的 PAR 導致積壓，尤其對效期短的醫療耗材有浪費風險。 PAR level should be calculated as Average Daily Usage × Replenishment Cycle Days × Safety Factor — not an arbitrarily "safe" large number. E.g., sterile gloves: 8 pairs/day, 2-day cycle, 1.5 safety factor → PAR = 8×2×1.5 = 24, not 50. Over-set PAR levels cause overstock, especially wasteful for short-shelf-life medical supplies.

🗂️ 週期盤點與 ABC 分類詳解🗂️ Cycle Count & ABC Classification — Deep Dive

▼

週期盤點（Cycle Count）是 Oracle Fusion Inventory 替代傳統年度全盤（Physical Inventory）的精確方法。透過 ABC 分類，將物料依「年消費額 × 單價」排序，自動分配不同盤點頻率，讓有限的人力資源優先盤點高價值物料，低價值物料減少盤點次數。 Cycle Count is Oracle Fusion Inventory's precision alternative to traditional annual physical inventory. ABC classification ranks items by "annual consumption × unit cost," then assigns different count frequencies — focusing limited labor on high-value items and reducing count frequency for low-value items.

ABC 分類標準與盤點頻率ABC Classification Criteria & Count Frequencies

分類Class 年消費額占比% Annual Value 物料數量占比% Item Count 建議盤點頻率Suggested Frequency 範例物料Example Items
A 類 ~70% ~10% 每月 1 次Monthly 晶片、主機板、高端原料Chips, motherboards, premium ingredients

差異容許值（Tolerance）如何設定？How do I set count tolerances?▶

在「週期盤點定義」中可設定兩種容許值：① 數量容許值（如差異 ±2 個以內自動核准）；② 金額容許值（如差異金額在 NT$500 以內自動核准）。超出容許值的差異項目，系統自動送審核工作流程（Workflow），需主管電子簽核後才能過帳調整。Two tolerance types can be set in the Cycle Count Definition: ① Quantity tolerance (e.g., ±2 units auto-approved); ② Value tolerance (e.g., variance ≤ NT$500 auto-approved). Variances exceeding tolerances are automatically routed to an approval workflow requiring supervisor e-signature before posting.

⚠️
常見錯誤：沒有先執行 ABC 分析就產生盤點任務Common Mistake: Generating Count Tasks Without Running ABC Analysis First
若未執行 ABC 分析，所有物料預設為「未分類（Unclassified）」，週期盤點計劃程式不知道應該多久盤一次，結果是所有物料都只盤一次（類似年度全盤），失去週期盤點的優化效果。 Without ABC analysis, all items default to "Unclassified," and the cycle count planner doesn't know the count interval — resulting in all items being counted once (equivalent to an annual physical inventory), defeating the optimization purpose of cycle counting.

🧪 批號控制（Lot Control）與 FEFO 詳解🧪 Lot Number Control & FEFO — Deep Dive

▼

批號控制（Lot Control）讓系統在每筆交易中強制記錄物料所屬的「批次」，並附加效期（Expiration Date）、製造日期、供應商批號等屬性。食品/製藥/化學品公司必須啟用此功能以符合法規（如 FDA 21 CFR Part 820、Taiwan GMP）。出庫時可搭配 FEFO（先效期先出）或 FIFO（先進先出）揀貨規則。 Lot Control forces the system to record which "batch" every inventory transaction belongs to, plus attributes like expiration date, manufacture date, and supplier lot number. Food, pharma, and chemical companies must enable this to comply with regulations (FDA 21 CFR Part 820, GMP, etc.). Outbound transactions can use FEFO (First Expired, First Out) or FIFO (First In, First Out) picking rules.

FEFO vs FIFO：核心差異FEFO vs FIFO: Core Difference

揀貨規則Picking Rule 排序依據Sort Criterion 適用場景Best For 範例Example
FEFO 效期最近的批次先出Earliest expiry date ships first 食品、乳品、醫藥Food, dairy, pharma LOT-A 效期 09/22 先出，LOT-B 效期 09/28 後出LOT-A expiry 09/22 ships first; LOT-B 09/28 second
FIFO 收料日期最早的批次先出Earliest receipt date ships first 電子零件、一般物料Electronics, general materials 1 月到貨的庫存先出，3 月到貨的後出January receipts ship before March receipts
💡
鮮途乳業 FEFO 完整範例FreshPath Dairy FEFO Full Example
  • LOT-20240913-A：全脂鮮奶 300L，效期 2024/09/20，收料 2024/09/13LOT-20240913-A: Whole milk 300L, expiry 2024/09/20, received 2024/09/13
  • LOT-20240915-B：全脂鮮奶 500L，效期 2024/09/22，收料 2024/09/15LOT-20240915-B: Whole milk 500L, expiry 2024/09/22, received 2024/09/15
  • 客戶訂單要求 200L → FEFO 系統自動選擇 LOT-20240913-A（效期 09/20 更早）優先出貨，避免效期更近的批次被壓在後面。Customer order for 200L → FEFO system auto-selects LOT-20240913-A (expiry 09/20 is earlier) to ship first, preventing the nearer-expiry batch from being left behind.
如何在物料主檔啟用批號控制？How do I enable Lot Control on an item?▶

Product Management → Items → Manage Items → [Select Item] → Edit → Inventory tab
→ Lot Control: Full Control
→ Shelf Life Days: 7（鮮奶 7 天保質期）
→ Picking Rule: FEFO

⚠️
批號控制一旦對有庫存的物料啟用，現有庫存必須先清零（零庫存），才能切換控制級別。建議在導入初期、庫存為零時設定。Lot control cannot be changed for items with existing on-hand quantity. The item must be at zero stock before switching control level. Set this up during initial implementation when inventory is zero.
批次追溯報告（Lot Genealogy）怎麼查？How do I run a Lot Genealogy (traceability) report?▶

路徑：Inventory Management → Transactions → Lot Genealogy Report。輸入批號（如 LOT-20240913-A），系統顯示：① 原料來源（供應商 + 供應商批號）；② 所有入庫/出庫交易（含日期、數量、目的地）；③ 已出貨的客戶訂單清單。食品召回演練時 30 秒內可取得完整追溯鏈。Path: Inventory Management → Transactions → Lot Genealogy Report. Enter lot number (e.g., LOT-20240913-A); system shows: ① Raw material source (vendor + vendor lot); ② All inbound/outbound transactions (date, qty, destination); ③ List of customer orders already shipped. Full traceability chain available in 30 seconds during food recall drills.

⚠️
常見錯誤：收料時未輸入效期Common Mistake: Not Entering Expiry Date at Receipt
若在物料主檔設定了「效期天數（Shelf Life Days）」，收料時系統會自動計算效期；但若設定為需手動輸入（Expiration Date Required = Yes），倉庫人員漏填效期，系統仍允許收料但效期為空，導致 FEFO 揀貨無法正確排序。建議在 Lot Control 設定中啟用「Expiration Date Required」並設定不允許空效期收料。 If Shelf Life Days is set on the item, the system auto-calculates expiry at receipt. But if Expiration Date is set to "Required = Yes" for manual entry, warehouse staff who leave it blank will still complete the receipt — but FEFO picking cannot sort correctly with null expiry dates. Enable "Expiration Date Required" in Lot Control settings and configure the system to reject receipts with no expiry.

💻 序號控制（Serial Number Control）詳解💻 Serial Number Control — Deep Dive

▼

序號控制（Serial Number Control）讓每一個物理個體都有唯一識別碼，並在整個供應鏈生命週期中記錄其所在位置與狀態。Oracle Fusion 支援在不同階段指派序號：收料時、完工入庫時、出貨時（各有適用場景）。 Serial Number Control gives every physical unit a unique identifier and tracks its location and status throughout the entire supply chain lifecycle. Oracle Fusion supports assigning serial numbers at different stages: at receipt, at WIP completion, or at shipment — each suited to different scenarios.

序號控制等級比較Serial Control Levels Compared

控制級別Control Level 序號指派時機When Assigned 追蹤範圍Tracked Through 適用情境Best For
At Receipt PO 收料時PO receipt 收料 → 出庫全程Receipt → Issue 購入即有序號的零件（如進口晶片）Purchased parts with vendor serials (e.g., imported chips)
At Completion 工單完工入庫時WO completion 成品倉 → 出庫全程FG warehouse → Shipment 自製成品（如筆電整機）Self-manufactured goods (e.g., assembled laptops)
At Shipment 出貨時才指派At time of shipment 僅出庫記錄Outbound record only 只需出貨序號記錄，不需倉內追蹤Only needs shipping serial; no in-warehouse tracking required
💡
閃芯科技筆電 SN-FCT-000823 完整生命週期FlashCore Laptop SN-FCT-000823 Full Lifecycle
  1. 工單 WO-FCT-2024-0821 完工 → 系統自動指派序號 SN-FCT-000801~000900（100 台）WO-FCT-2024-0821 completes → system auto-assigns SN-FCT-000801–000900 (100 units)
  2. SN-FCT-000823 入庫「成品倉-FG-B2」，狀態：AvailableSN-FCT-000823 received to "FG-B2" bin, status: Available
  3. 調撥至「台北配送倉」：Inter-org Transfer，在途時狀態：In-TransitTransferred to "Taipei DC": Inter-org Transfer; status during transit: In-Transit
  4. 台北配送倉確認收料，狀態：AvailableTaipei DC confirms receipt, status: Available
  5. 銷售出貨：SO-2024-5678，出貨至客戶王先生，狀態：Issued/ShippedSales shipment: SO-2024-5678, shipped to customer Mr. Wang, status: Issued/Shipped
  6. 客戶保固查詢：10 秒內完整顯示上述所有歷史記錄Customer warranty query: complete history displayed within 10 seconds
⚠️
常見錯誤：序號重複或序號格式不一致Common Mistake: Duplicate Serials or Inconsistent Serial Formats
若允許手動輸入序號，倉庫人員可能輸入 "SN000823" 和 "sn000823"（大小寫不同）造成追蹤混亂。建議：① 在系統層面設定序號產生規則（Generation: System-Defined），由 Oracle 自動遞增產生，避免人工錯誤；② 或設定序號掩碼（Mask）強制格式為 "SN-FCT-XXXXXX"。 When manual serial entry is allowed, staff may enter "SN000823" and "sn000823" (different case), causing tracking confusion. Recommendations: ① Set serial generation to "System-Defined" so Oracle auto-increments, eliminating human error; ② Or define a serial mask enforcing format "SN-FCT-XXXXXX".

Each closes its period independently without impact on the other, yet Finance can consolidate at group level.

設定清單

Setup Checklist

常見問題（FAQ）

Frequently Asked Questions

組織間調撥（Inter-org Transfer）和出貨/收料（Ship/Receive）什麼時候用哪個？ When should I use Inter-org Transfer vs Ship/Receive? ▶

Inter-org Transfer（組織間調撥）：適用於同一法律實體（Legal Entity）旗下的不同庫存組織間移動物料。例如台北廠（INV-TW01）→ 高雄倉（INV-KH01）。過帳科目走「組織間調撥」科目，不產生應收/應付憑證。流程：來源組織建立調撥，指定「在途子庫存（In-Transit）」，目的組織收料確認後完成。Inter-org Transfer: Use when moving materials between inventory organizations under the same Legal Entity. E.g., Taipei Plant (INV-TW01) → Kaohsiung WH (INV-KH01). Posts to "Inter-org transfer" accounts; no AR/AP vouchers. Flow: source org creates transfer to In-Transit subinventory; destination org confirms receipt to complete.

Ship/Receive（內部訂單出貨/收料）：適用於不同法律實體間，或需要留下 PO/SO 文件軌跡的情境（如集團內部採購、審計要求）。這個流程會產生內部銷售訂單（Internal SO）和內部採購訂單（Internal PO），對應應收/應付分錄，適合需要集團內部轉售會計處理的場景。Ship/Receive (Internal Order): Use for different legal entities, or when PO/SO document trails are required (intercompany procurement, audit requirements). This flow generates an Internal SO and Internal PO with corresponding AR/AP entries — appropriate for intercompany resale accounting.

✅
判斷快捷：「這次移動需要產生應收/應付憑證嗎？」需要 → Ship/Receive；不需要 → Inter-org Transfer。Quick test: "Does this move need to generate AR/AP documents?" Yes → Ship/Receive. No → Inter-org Transfer.
可以做負庫存調整嗎？有什麼注意事項？ Can I do a negative inventory adjustment? What should I watch out for? ▶

可以。Oracle Fusion 允許負向調整（將現有量調低，使其低於 0），但需要：① 庫存組織設定「允許負數庫存（Allow Negative Balances = Yes）」；② 操作人員擁有 INV_ADJUST_INVENTORY 職能；③ 若差異超過容許值，需主管核准。Yes. Oracle Fusion allows negative adjustments (reducing on-hand below 0), but requires: ① Inventory organization has "Allow Negative Balances = Yes"; ② User has the INV_ADJUST_INVENTORY duty role; ③ If variance exceeds tolerance, supervisor approval is required.

注意事項：負庫存餘額會影響平均成本計算——當現有量為負值時，下一筆收料的平均成本計算邏輯可能產生異常高或異常低的單位成本。建議在月結前必須將所有負庫存清零，並調查原因（通常是交易順序問題或收料延遲）。Watch out for: Negative on-hand balances distort average cost calculations — when on-hand is negative, the next receipt's weighted-average cost computation may yield abnormally high or low unit costs. Always resolve all negative on-hand to zero before period close, and investigate the root cause (usually transaction sequencing issues or delayed receipts).

FIFO 和 FEFO 揀貨有什麼區別？Oracle 如何設定？ What is the difference between FIFO and FEFO picking, and how do I configure them in Oracle? ▶

FIFO（先進先出）：依收料日期排序，最早收料的批次最先出庫。適用電子零件、工具等沒有效期的物料。設定路徑：物料主檔 → Picking Rule = FIFO（或在 Inventory Organization 層級設定預設值）。FIFO (First In, First Out): Sort by receipt date; earliest received goes out first. Suitable for electronics, tools, and other items without expiry. Configuration: Item Master → Picking Rule = FIFO (or set as org-level default).

FEFO（先效期先出）：依效期（Expiration Date）排序，效期最近的批次最先出庫，與收料日期無關。適用食品、藥品、試劑等有效期物料。前提是物料必須啟用批號控制（Lot Control）且每個批次都有填入效期，否則系統無法排序。設定路徑：物料主檔 → Picking Rule = FEFO。FEFO (First Expired, First Out): Sort by Expiration Date; lot with earliest expiry ships first, regardless of receipt date. Suitable for food, pharmaceuticals, and reagents. Prerequisite: item must have Lot Control enabled and every lot must have an expiration date entered — otherwise the system cannot sort. Configuration: Item Master → Picking Rule = FEFO.

💡
關鍵差異：今天收到效期 10 天的批次，昨天收到效期 30 天的批次。FIFO 先出昨天的（收料早）；FEFO 先出今天的（效期近）。食品公司必須用 FEFO，否則效期遠的批次會被持續壓後，最終過期損耗。Key difference: Today you receive a batch expiring in 10 days; yesterday you received one expiring in 30 days. FIFO ships yesterday's first (earlier receipt); FEFO ships today's first (nearer expiry). Food companies must use FEFO, or far-expiry batches keep getting pushed back and eventually expire.
Min-Max 如何與供應鏈計劃（Supply Planning / MRP）互動？會不會產生重複 PR？ How does Min-Max interact with Supply Planning / MRP? Will they create duplicate PRs? ▶

會。如果同一物料同時在庫存模組設定了 Min-Max 水位，又在 Supply Planning 中被 MRP/MPS 計劃，兩個系統都會獨立計算補貨需求，產生重複的請購單（PR）。Yes. If the same item has Min-Max thresholds set in Inventory AND is planned by MRP/MPS in Supply Planning, both systems independently calculate replenishment needs and generate duplicate PRs.

最佳實踐：在物料主檔「計劃方法（Planning Method）」欄位選擇其中一種：Best Practice: In the item master "Planning Method" field, choose one:

  • Min-Max Planning：由庫存模組管理，Supply Planning 跳過此物料Min-Max Planning: managed by Inventory module; Supply Planning skips this item
  • MRP 或 MPS：由 Supply Planning 管理，庫存模組不跑 Min-MaxMRP or MPS: managed by Supply Planning; Inventory Min-Max program skips this item
  • Not Planned：兩者都不管（如一次性採購物料）Not Planned: neither manages it (e.g., one-time-buy items)
⚠️
A 類高價值物料建議用 MRP（考慮需求波動、前置時間、批量）；C 類低價值物料用 Min-Max 即可，不需佔用 Supply Planning 運算資源。High-value A-class items: use MRP (considers demand variability, lead times, lot sizes). Low-value C-class items: Min-Max is sufficient; no need to consume Supply Planning compute resources.

ABC Classification ABC 分類ABC Classification 依年消費金額將物料分 A/B/C 三類，決定不同管理強度Classifies items A/B/C by annual consumption value to determine management intensity

從請購需求到付款的完整 Procure-to-Pay 流程，企業控制採購成本的核心工具 Complete Procure-to-Pay from request to payment — the core tool for controlling procurement costs

Procure-to-Pay PO Types Sourcing Supplier Mgmt Contracts

為什麼採購管理至關重要？

Why Does Procurement Management Matter?

GlobalTech 是一家年營收 20 億美元的製造商，三年前採購流程完全依賴 Email 與 Excel。採購人員每週花 30% 的時間追蹤 PR 狀態；供應商詢問「你們的訂單在哪？」時，沒人能立刻回答。2023 年一次因漏訂原物料導致的停產事件，直接損失達 800 萬元，震驚了整個管理層。 GlobalTech is a $2B manufacturer that, three years ago, ran its entire procurement process on email and Excel. Buyers spent 30% of their week just chasing PR statuses. When suppliers asked "where is your order?" no one could answer immediately. A 2023 production shutdown caused by a missed raw material order cost $8M and shook management to its core.

導入 Oracle Fusion Procurement 後，GlobalTech 建立了三條截然不同的採購策略：辦公耗材透過自助型採購目錄（Self-Service Procurement）讓員工直接下單，無需採購人員介入；原物料則利用空白採購合約（BPA）與核心供應商事先議價，每次補貨只需發放 Release 而非重新議價；而全新的 CNC 機台則走 RFQ 競標流程，確保最優惠的市場價格。三種策略、一套系統、全程可追蹤。 After implementing Oracle Fusion Procurement, GlobalTech established three distinct buying strategies: office supplies go through Self-Service Procurement catalogs so employees order directly without buyer involvement; raw materials use Blanket Purchase Agreements (BPA) with key suppliers so each replenishment is a Release against pre-negotiated prices; and the new CNC machine goes through a formal RFQ competitive bidding process. Three strategies, one system, fully auditable.

本模組將帶你走完完整的 Procure-to-Pay 循環——從員工提出請購單（PR）、採購人員建立採購單（PO）、倉庫確認收貨（Receipt）、到財務三方比對（Three-Way Match）後付款。你將學習如何根據採購場景選擇正確的 PO 類型、設定核准層級、建立供應商合格名單（ASL），以及利用 ERS（Evaluated Receipt Settlement）實現無發票自動付款。 This module walks you through the complete Procure-to-Pay cycle — from employee purchase requisitions (PR), buyer creation of purchase orders (PO), warehouse receiving (Receipt), to three-way match for payment. You'll learn how to choose the right PO type for each buying scenario, configure approval hierarchies, set up Approved Supplier Lists (ASL), and leverage ERS (Evaluated Receipt Settlement) for touchless invoice-free payment.

🔑
本模組核心業務場景：Core Business Scenario: GlobalTech 同時需要採購辦公耗材（目錄採購）、原物料（BPA 協議採購）、CNC 機台（競標採購）——同一系統內三種截然不同的採購策略。 GlobalTech needs to buy office supplies (catalog buying), raw materials (BPA agreement), and a CNC machine (competitive RFQ) — three very different buying strategies within one system.

核心功能概覽

Core Features Overview

📄

多種 PO 類型Multiple PO Types

Standard PO（一次性採購）、BPA（框架合約釋放）、Contract PO（複雜服務合約）。例：與台積電議定年度矽晶圓 BPA，每次補貨只需 Release，無需重談價格。Standard PO (one-time), BPA (blanket release), Contract PO (complex services). Example: Annual silicon wafer BPA with TSMC — each replenishment is just a Release, no renegotiation.

🛍️

自助型採購Self-Service Procurement

員工透過購物車介面選購預核准目錄品項。例：IT 耗材目錄含 200 款 SKU，員工自行下單，系統自動路由至供應商，採購人員零介入。Employees shop from pre-approved catalogs in a shopping-cart UI. Example: IT supplies catalog with 200 SKUs — employees order directly, system routes to supplier automatically, zero buyer involvement.

🏆

詢價 / 競標 SourcingRFQ / Auction Sourcing

RFI → RFQ → 拍賣三階段。例：CNC 機台 RFQ 邀請 5 家供應商，以價格 40%、品質 30%、交期 30% 加權評分，自動比較報價單。RFI → RFQ → Auction three stages. Example: CNC machine RFQ sent to 5 suppliers, scored by price 40%, quality 30%, delivery 30%, auto-comparing bids.

📋

合格供應商清單 ASLApproved Supplier List (ASL)

為每個品項 / 採購組織設定合格供應商、前置時間、分配比例。例：Item X「鋼板 3mm」設定 A 廠 60%、B 廠 40%，Lead Time 分別 14 天 / 21 天。Set approved suppliers per item/org with lead times and split %. Example: Item X "Steel Sheet 3mm" assigned to Vendor A 60% / Vendor B 40%, lead times 14 / 21 days.

🤖

Touchless Buying 免人工採購Touchless Buying

符合條件的 PR 自動轉 PO，無需採購員手動建立。例：金額低於 NT$5,000 且 ASL 中有唯一供應商的 PR，10 分鐘內自動產生並發出 PO。Qualifying PRs auto-convert to PO without buyer action. Example: PRs under NT$5,000 with a single ASL supplier generate and dispatch a PO within 10 minutes.

⚡

ERS 免發票自動付款ERS Auto Settlement

收貨即觸發付款，無需供應商寄發票。例：GlobalTech 對 A 廠的 BPA 啟用 ERS，每週一倉庫確認收貨後，系統自動產生 Invoice 並排入付款排程。Receipt triggers payment, no supplier invoice needed. Example: GlobalTech enables ERS on BPA with Vendor A — every Monday warehouse confirms receipt, system auto-generates invoice and queues payment.

📄 深度解析：PO 類型選擇決策矩陣 📄 Deep Dive: PO Type Decision Matrix

▼

Oracle Fusion 提供四種採購單類型，不同場景應選擇不同類型。錯誤的類型選擇不僅造成流程混亂，更可能導致無法正確追蹤預算承諾或遺漏合約條款。 Oracle Fusion offers four PO types. Choosing the wrong type causes process confusion and may result in incorrect budget tracking or missed contract terms.

BPA 和 Standard PO 的本質差異是什麼？ What's the fundamental difference between BPA and Standard PO? ▶

Standard PO 是「完整採購事件」——你知道買多少、什麼時候交貨。PO 核准後直接發給供應商，收貨後比對發票付款，流程結束。Standard PO is a "complete purchase event" — you know the exact quantity and delivery date. Once approved, it's dispatched to the supplier and closed after receipt and invoice match.

BPA 則是「框架授權」——你只知道這個供應商在這段期間、這個議定價格下可以賣給你，但具體的每批次數量和日期，等需求確定後再透過 Release 發出。Release 才是真正的採購訂單，而 BPA 是授權 Release 的「上層合約」。BPA is a "framework authorization" — you know this supplier can sell to you at this agreed price during this period, but exact quantities and dates are confirmed later via Releases. Each Release is the actual purchase order; the BPA is the parent contract that authorizes releases.

BPA 的最高承諾量用完了怎麼辦？ What happens when a BPA reaches its maximum committed quantity? ▶

系統會根據 BPA 的設定觸發警告或直接拒絕新的 Release。你有兩個選項：(1) 修改 BPA 提高最高承諾量（需要重新核准）；(2) 建立新的 Standard PO 處理超額部分。建議在 BPA 剩餘 10% 時設定預警通知採購人員。The system triggers a warning or blocks new Releases depending on BPA settings. Options: (1) Amend the BPA to increase maximum committed qty (requires re-approval); (2) Create a Standard PO for the overage. Best practice: set an alert when BPA is 90% consumed.

⚠️
常見錯誤：Common Mistake: 把 BPA 當作 Standard PO 使用——在 BPA 上直接設定交貨日期和數量，導致後續無法靈活 Release。BPA 的品項行不應填寫具體的「預計交期」，那是 Release 才要設定的資訊。 Treating BPA like a Standard PO — setting specific delivery dates and quantities on the BPA itself, making it inflexible. BPA line items should NOT have specific need-by dates; those belong on the Release.

🛍️ 深度解析：自助型採購三種模式 🛍️ Deep Dive: Self-Service Procurement — Three Modes

▼

Self-Service Procurement 讓員工像網路購物一樣採購辦公用品，但有三種截然不同的目錄模式。選對模式可以大幅降低採購人員工作量，同時確保合規。 Self-Service Procurement lets employees shop for office supplies like online shopping, but there are three distinct catalog modes. Choosing the right mode dramatically reduces buyer workload while maintaining compliance.

⚠️
常見錯誤：Common Mistake: Punchout 設定後沒有測試 cXML 回傳。最常見的問題是供應商網站的 Price 欄位格式不符 Oracle 預期（應為純數字，不含貨幣符號），導致購物車無法正確帶回金額。上線前務必用測試帳號走完整個 Punchout 流程。 Not testing cXML return after Punchout setup. The most common issue is the supplier's Price field format not matching Oracle's expectation (must be plain number, no currency symbol), causing cart amounts to fail on return. Always do a full Punchout test with a test account before go-live.

🏆 深度解析：RFQ 競標採購流程 🏆 Deep Dive: RFQ Competitive Sourcing Process

▼

GlobalTech 需要採購一台 CNC 精密加工機，預算 NT$3,000,000。採購部決定發起 RFQ 競標，邀請 5 家供應商報價，使用加權評分決定得標廠商。 GlobalTech needs to purchase one CNC precision machining center, budget NT$3,000,000. Procurement initiates an RFQ, inviting 5 suppliers to bid, using weighted scoring to determine the winner.

Oracle 評分設定路徑：Oracle Scoring Setup: Sourcing → Negotiations → Create Negotiation → 在「評分準則」頁簽設定各項目權重，系統在供應商提交報價後自動計算加權分數，採購員只需點擊「分析報價」即可看到排名。 Sourcing → Negotiations → Create Negotiation → Under "Scoring Criteria" tab, set weights for each criterion. System auto-calculates weighted scores after suppliers submit bids. Buyer clicks "Analyze Responses" to see rankings.
可以把 RFQ 決標結果直接轉成 PO 嗎？ Can I directly convert an RFQ award to a PO? ▶

可以。在 Oracle Sourcing 中決標後，系統提供「Create Purchase Order」按鈕，直接將得標供應商的報價資訊帶入 PO 草稿，包含品項、數量、單價、交期。採購員確認後送核准即可，省去重複鍵入的工作。Yes. After awarding in Oracle Sourcing, the system provides a "Create Purchase Order" button that auto-populates a PO draft with the winning supplier's item, quantity, unit price, and delivery date. The buyer reviews and submits for approval — no re-entry needed.

⚠️
常見錯誤：Common Mistake: 評分準則的權重設定為百分比時，總和必須等於 100%。若設定 價格 40% + 品質 30% + 交期 20% = 90%，系統不會報錯，但評分結果會失真。務必在發布 RFQ 前確認所有準則權重合計為 100%。 When setting scoring criteria weights as percentages, they MUST sum to exactly 100%. If Price 40% + Quality 30% + Delivery 20% = 90%, the system may not error but scoring results will be distorted. Always verify weights sum to 100% before publishing the RFQ.

📋 深度解析：合格供應商清單 ASL 設定 📋 Deep Dive: Approved Supplier List (ASL) Setup

▼

ASL（Approved Supplier List）定義了「哪些供應商被授權供應哪些品項」，並記錄每個品項的交貨前置時間和採購分配比例。ASL 不僅影響 PR 轉 PO 時的供應商建議，也是 Touchless Buying 自動化的前提條件。 The ASL defines "which suppliers are authorized to supply which items" and records lead times and sourcing split percentages. The ASL affects supplier suggestions during PR-to-PO conversion and is a prerequisite for Touchless Buying automation.

Item M-STEEL-3MM（3mm 鋼板）的 ASL 設定範例ASL Configuration Example for Item M-STEEL-3MM (3mm Steel Sheet)

Oracle 設定路徑：Oracle Navigation: Procurement → Approved Supplier List → 搜尋品項 M-STEEL-3MM → 新增供應商 → 填寫「採購組織」「供應商」「地點」「分配 %」「前置時間」→ 儲存 Procurement → Approved Supplier List → Search item M-STEEL-3MM → Add Supplier → Fill in Procurement Org, Supplier, Site, Allocation %, Lead Time → Save
ASL 的供應商狀態有哪些？Debarred 和 Approved 的差異？ What ASL supplier statuses exist? Difference between Debarred and Approved? ▶

ASL 供應商狀態分為：
• Approved：正常合格，可接受 PR 建議和 PO 建立
• Conditional：有條件核准，需要額外批准才能採購
• Debarred：停用/黑名單，系統阻止向此供應商發 PO，即使手動嘗試也會警告
• New：新供應商審核中，尚未核准
將供應商設為 Debarred 後，所有現有 BPA Release 和 Standard PO 草稿也會被標示為需要審查。 ASL supplier statuses:
• Approved: Normal qualified status, PR suggestions and PO creation allowed
• Conditional: Conditionally approved, requires additional approval to purchase
• Debarred: Blacklisted, system blocks PO creation to this supplier and warns even on manual attempts
• New: Under review, not yet approved
Setting a supplier to Debarred flags existing BPA Releases and Standard PO drafts for review.

⚠️
常見錯誤：Common Mistake: 在 ASL 中設定採購分配比例時，多個供應商的分配比例總和不需要等於 100%（Oracle 允許非 100% 的設定）。但如果你啟用了「需求分配」功能（Sourcing Rule），則總和必須為 100%，否則系統在建議供應商時會出現計算錯誤。 ASL sourcing percentages across multiple suppliers do NOT need to sum to 100% (Oracle allows non-100% settings). However, if you enable Sourcing Rules with demand allocation, percentages MUST sum to 100% or the system will error when suggesting suppliers.

🤖 深度解析：Touchless Buying 自動化採購規則 🤖 Deep Dive: Touchless Buying Automation Rules

▼

Touchless Buying 讓符合條件的請購單（PR）自動轉換為採購單（PO），無需採購人員手動介入。GlobalTech 設定後，低值辦公耗材的 PR 平均在 8 分鐘內完成採購轉換，採購部門因此每週節省約 15 小時的手動工作。 Touchless Buying auto-converts qualifying Purchase Requisitions to Purchase Orders without buyer intervention. After GlobalTech's setup, low-value office supply PRs convert in an average of 8 minutes, saving the procurement team approximately 15 hours per week of manual work.

自動轉換的觸發條件（AND 邏輯，所有條件需同時滿足）Auto-Conversion Trigger Conditions (AND logic — all must be met)

# 條件Condition GlobalTech 設定值GlobalTech Setting 說明Explanation
1 金額上限Amount Limit NT$5,000 以下 超過此金額仍需採購員處理Above this, buyer intervention required
2 ASL 中唯一合格供應商Single approved supplier in ASL 品項在 ASL 中只有 1 家 Approved 供應商Item has exactly 1 Approved supplier in ASL 多家供應商需人工選擇Multiple suppliers need human selection
3 有效 BPA 可用Active BPA available 供應商有未到期 BPA 且剩餘額度充足Supplier has active BPA with remaining balance 有議定價格才能自動開單Pre-agreed price required for auto-creation
4 PR 已完全核准PR fully approved 所有核准層級通過All approval levels passed 未核准的 PR 不觸發自動轉換Unapproved PRs do not trigger conversion
5 品項屬於目錄採購Item is catalog-based 來自內部目錄或 Punchout 的品項From local catalog or Punchout Smart Form 非目錄品項不適用Non-catalog Smart Form items excluded
💡
設定路徑：Setup Path: Procurement → Procurement Configuration → Configure Procurement Business Function → Automation Rules → 設定「自動轉換 PR」的條件規則 Procurement → Procurement Configuration → Configure Procurement Business Function → Automation Rules → Set "Auto-Create PO from PR" condition rules
如果 PR 符合自動轉換條件，採購員還需要做什麼？ If a PR qualifies for auto-conversion, what does the buyer still do? ▶

理想情況下，採購員什麼都不需要做——系統自動完成 PR→PO 轉換、發出 PO 給供應商。採購員只需定期（如每日）查看「自動建立的 PO」報表，確認沒有異常。如果有任何步驟失敗（如 BPA 額度不足），系統會自動將該 PR 路由回採購員的待辦清單，並附上失敗原因說明。Ideally, the buyer does nothing — the system auto-completes PR→PO conversion and dispatches the PO to the supplier. Buyers only need to periodically (e.g., daily) review "Auto-Created PO" reports to confirm no anomalies. If any step fails (e.g., BPA balance exhausted), the system automatically routes that PR back to the buyer's action list with an explanation.

⚖️ 深度解析：三方比對與 ERS 自動結算 ⚖️ Deep Dive: Three-Way Match & ERS Auto Settlement

▼

三方比對（Three-Way Match）是 AP 付款前的最後防線，確保付出的錢對應真實收到的貨物。Oracle AP 在發票登入時自動比對 PO 數量、收貨數量、發票數量三者是否一致。 Three-Way Match is the final safeguard before AP payment, ensuring money paid corresponds to goods actually received. Oracle AP automatically compares PO quantity, received quantity, and invoice quantity when an invoice is entered.

差異情況與系統處理方式Discrepancy Scenarios and System Handling

情境Scenario PO 數量 收貨數量Received Qty 發票數量Invoice Qty 系統行為System Action AP 處理AP Action
完全匹配 ✅Full Match ✅ 100 100 100 自動核准，進入付款排程Auto-approve, enter payment schedule 無需介入
收貨不足 ⚠️Under-Receipt ⚠️ 100 80 100 發票 Hold（未收到貨的 20 件不能付款）Invoice on Hold (20 unreceived units blocked) 等待補收貨或聯繫供應商
超收 ⚠️Over-Receipt ⚠️ 100 115 115 超過 PO 容差（預設 10%）→ 警告採購員Exceeds PO tolerance (default 10%) → Alert buyer 需 PO 變更單或退貨
價格差異Price Variance NT$100/件 — NT$105/件 Invoice Price Variance，超過容差 → HoldInvoice Price Variance, exceeds tolerance → Hold 需採購員核准價差

ERS（Evaluated Receipt Settlement）—— 免發票自動付款ERS — Invoice-Free Automatic Settlement

ERS 適用於長期穩定合作的供應商。啟用後，倉庫確認收貨即觸發 AP 自動產生發票並排入付款，供應商不需要寄送紙本或電子發票。 ERS suits stable long-term supplier relationships. When enabled, warehouse receipt confirmation triggers AP to auto-generate an invoice and schedule payment — the supplier doesn't need to send any invoice.

✅
ERS 啟用條件與設定：ERS Enablement Conditions & Setup:
  • 在「供應商地點」設定中勾選「Pay on Receipt (ERS)」Check "Pay on Receipt (ERS)" in Supplier Site settings
  • PO 行必須勾選「Match Approval Level = 2-Way Match」（PO + Receipt）PO line must have "Match Approval Level = 2-Way Match" (PO + Receipt)
  • 收貨時必須完整記錄數量（不允許估計收貨）Full quantity must be recorded at receipt (no estimated receiving)
  • 系統在收貨後的下一個排程批次（通常每日夜間）自動產生 InvoiceSystem auto-generates Invoice in the next scheduled batch (usually nightly) after receipt
⚠️
常見錯誤：Common Mistake: 啟用 ERS 後，供應商仍然發來紙本發票，AP 人員手動登入造成「重複發票」（Duplicate Invoice）。應在 ERS 生效前與供應商明確溝通「不再需要發票」，並在供應商入口網站更新設定，或由 AP 設定供應商的「Duplicate Invoice Check」規則。 After enabling ERS, the supplier still sends paper invoices, and AP staff manually enter them causing Duplicate Invoice errors. Before ERS go-live, clearly communicate to suppliers that "no invoice is needed" and update settings in the supplier portal, or configure Duplicate Invoice Check rules in AP.

🎯 端到端案例：GlobalTech 的三條採購策略 🎯 End-to-End Case Study: GlobalTech's Three Buying Strategies

▼

策略 A：辦公椅採購（自助型目錄採購）Strategy A: Office Chair Purchase (Self-Service Catalog)

需求：業務部門採購 5 把人體工學辦公椅，每把 NT$4,200，合計 NT$21,000。
流程：員工登入 Self-Service Procurement → 搜尋「人體工學椅」→ 加入購物車（數量 5）→ 填入成本中心「CC-SALES-01」→ 提交 PR → 主管線上核准（1 小時）→ Touchless 不適用（金額超過 NT$5,000 單筆限制）→ 採購員收到待辦 → 選定 ASL 供應商「辦公家具 A 廠」→ 建立 Standard PO #GT2024-PO-8821 → 核准 → 發出 → 7 天後收貨 → AP 三方比對 → 付款。
耗時：PR 提交到付款約 15 個工作日，其中採購員實際操作時間不超過 20 分鐘。 Need: Sales dept buys 5 ergonomic office chairs at NT$4,200 each, total NT$21,000.
Flow: Employee logs into Self-Service Procurement → searches "ergonomic chair" → adds to cart (qty 5) → enters cost center "CC-SALES-01" → submits PR → manager approves online (1 hour) → Touchless N/A (amount exceeds NT$5,000 per-line limit) → buyer receives action → selects ASL supplier "Office Furniture Vendor A" → creates Standard PO #GT2024-PO-8821 → approves → dispatches → receipt after 7 days → AP three-way match → payment.
Timeline: PR submission to payment ≈15 business days; buyer actual handling time <20 minutes.

策略 B：鋼板採購（BPA 框架合約 Release）Strategy B: Steel Sheet (BPA Release)

需求：MRP 計算出本週需要補充 50 公噸 3mm 鋼板，最晚需貨日 2024-03-15。
流程：MRP 產生 PR（品項 M-STEEL-3MM，數量 50MT，需貨日 03/15）→ PR 核准 → 採購員查看 PR 時，系統自動建議「建立 BPA Release」（因為 Item 有 Active BPA #GT2024-BPA-001，尚有剩餘額度 380MT）→ 採購員點擊「建立 Release」→ BPA Release #GT2024-BPA-001-R07（第 7 次 Release）自動帶入 A 廠、單價 NT$12,000、預計交期 14 天（03/13）→ 核准 → 發出。
效益：不需重新議價；Release 建立時間 <5 分鐘；BPA 已使用額度即時更新為 420MT / 500MT（84%）。 Need: MRP calculates 50 metric tons of 3mm steel sheet needed for replenishment, latest need-by date 2024-03-15.
Flow: MRP generates PR (item M-STEEL-3MM, qty 50MT, need-by 03/15) → PR approved → buyer views PR, system auto-suggests "Create BPA Release" (Active BPA #GT2024-BPA-001 with 380MT remaining balance) → buyer clicks "Create Release" → BPA Release #GT2024-BPA-001-R07 (7th release) auto-populates Vendor A, NT$12,000/MT, 14-day lead time (delivery 03/13) → approved → dispatched.
Benefit: No renegotiation; Release creation <5 minutes; BPA consumed qty instantly updates to 420MT/500MT (84%).

策略 C：CNC 機台採購（RFQ 競標 → Standard PO）Strategy C: CNC Machine (RFQ → Standard PO)

需求：工程部門提出資本支出申請，採購一台 5 軸 CNC 精密加工機台，預算 NT$3,000,000，需 CFO 核准。
流程：工程師建立 PR（品類：資本設備，金額 NT$3,000,000）→ 觸發三層核准（部門主管 → 財務總監 → CFO）→ 核准後採購員建立 Sourcing Negotiation（RFQ）→ 邀請 5 家供應商 → 供應商 10 天內提交報價 → 系統加權評分（A 廠 88.7 分最高）→ 採購員選擇 A 廠決標 → 系統一鍵建立 Standard PO #GT2024-PO-9001（NT$2,650,000）→ 再次核准（CFO）→ 發出 → 90 天後交機 → 驗收 → 付款。
節省：原預算 NT$3,000,000，實際採購 NT$2,650,000，節省 NT$350,000（11.7%）。 Need: Engineering capex request for one 5-axis CNC precision machining center, budget NT$3,000,000, requires CFO approval.
Flow: Engineer creates PR (category: Capital Equipment, amount NT$3,000,000) → triggers 3-tier approval (Dept Manager → CFO Controller → CFO) → after approval, buyer creates Sourcing Negotiation (RFQ) → invites 5 suppliers → suppliers submit bids within 10 days → system weighted scoring (Vendor A scores highest at 88.7) → buyer awards to Vendor A → one-click creates Standard PO #GT2024-PO-9001 (NT$2,650,000) → re-approved (CFO) → dispatched → machine delivered in 90 days → acceptance → payment.
Savings: Budget NT$3,000,000, actual NT$2,650,000, saved NT$350,000 (11.7%).
