❓ 常見問題解答

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

PO Hold 和 Cancel 的差異是什麼？什麼時候用哪個？ What is the difference between PO Hold and Cancel? When to use each? ▶
PO Hold（暫緩）PO Cancel（取消）
狀態Status暫時停止，可恢復Temporarily paused, reversible永久終止，不可恢復Permanently terminated, irreversible
使用時機When to use正在協商修改條款、等待供應商確認、臨時凍結支出Negotiating changes, awaiting supplier confirmation, temporary spending freeze需求已取消、供應商無法履約、採購決策改變Need cancelled, supplier cannot fulfill, procurement decision changed
對 Invoice 影響Invoice ImpactHold 期間 Invoice 無法匹配付款Invoices cannot match/pay during Hold取消後任何新 Invoice 均被拒絕All new invoices rejected after Cancel
已收貨部分Received Qty不受影響Unaffected已收貨部分仍可付款（需手動處理）Received qty can still be paid (manual handling)

實務建議：如果只是不確定是否要取消，先用 Hold；確認不需要了再 Cancel。Cancel 後若有未付款的已收貨，需建立獨立 Invoice 處理。Practical tip: If unsure whether to cancel, use Hold first; Cancel only when confirmed. If cancelled PO has received but unpaid items, create a standalone Invoice to handle them.

一張 PR 可以轉成多張 PO 嗎？ Can one Purchase Requisition become multiple Purchase Orders? ▶

可以，而且這是實務中很常見的情況。一張 PR 的不同行（Line）可以因為以下原因分拆成多張 PO：Yes, and it's very common in practice. Different lines on one PR can be split into multiple POs because:

  • 不同行對應不同的合格供應商（ASL 中指定了不同供應商）Different lines map to different approved suppliers (ASL specifies different vendors)
  • 不同行來自不同採購品類，由不同採購員負責Different lines belong to different categories handled by different buyers
  • 部分行有 BPA 可用（建立 BPA Release），其他行需建立 Standard POSome lines have active BPA (create Release), others need Standard PO
  • 採購員手動選擇將某幾行合併或拆分Buyer manually chooses to consolidate or split lines

Oracle 在「處理請購單」介面（Process Requisitions）中，採購員可以選擇多個 PR 行，選擇「建立採購單」，系統自動根據供應商分組。同一供應商的行合併為一張 PO，不同供應商的行各自獨立建立 PO。In Oracle's "Process Requisitions" screen, buyers select multiple PR lines and click "Create Purchase Order." The system auto-groups by supplier — same supplier lines merge into one PO, different supplier lines create separate POs.

收貨數量超過 PO 數量（Over-Receipt）怎麼處理？ What happens if goods received exceed the PO quantity (over-receipt)? ▶

Oracle 有「Over-Receipt Tolerance」設定（預設 10%）。以 PO 100 件為例：Oracle has an "Over-Receipt Tolerance" setting (default 10%). For PO qty = 100:

  • 收貨 ≤110 件（10% 容差內）：系統允許收貨，但會記錄超收數量，AP 需注意發票比對。Receipt ≤110 units (within 10% tolerance): System allows receipt but flags the overage; AP should note invoice matching.
  • 收貨 >110 件（超過容差）：系統根據設定選擇：(a) 警告並允許收貨（Warn Only）、(b) 阻止收貨（Reject）。倉庫需要聯繫採購員，採購員建立「PO 變更單」（Change Order）提高 PO 數量，或安排退貨（Return to Supplier）。Receipt >110 units (exceeds tolerance): System either (a) warns and allows (Warn Only) or (b) rejects receipt. Warehouse contacts buyer, who creates a PO Change Order to increase qty, or arranges Return to Supplier.

建議：在高精度採購（如特殊規格零件）中，將 Over-Receipt Tolerance 設為 0，避免任何超收。在原物料採購中，考慮設為 5% 以容納量測誤差。Recommendation: For precision procurement (custom-spec parts), set Over-Receipt Tolerance to 0. For raw materials, consider 5% to accommodate measurement variance.

高金額 PO 的核准層級如何設定？可以自動轉交代理嗎？ How do approval hierarchies work for high-value POs? Can they be auto-delegated? ▶

Oracle 使用「核准管理（AME，Approval Management Engine）」設定採購核准規則。核准層級典型設定如下：Oracle uses AME (Approval Management Engine) to configure procurement approval rules. Typical tier setup:

金額範圍Amount Range核准人Approver系統角色System Role
NT$0 ~ NT$50,000採購主管Procurement SupervisorProcurement Manager
NT$50,001 ~ NT$500,000財務主管Finance ManagerFinance Director
NT$500,001 ~ NT$3,000,000財務總監CFO ControllerVP Finance
>NT$3,000,000執行長 CEOCEOChief Executive

代理核准（Delegation）：在 Oracle 中，核准人可在個人設定中設定「核准代理人」和代理期間（如出差期間）。代理期間，所有核准通知自動轉發至代理人。設定路徑：My Account → Worklist → Vacation Rules。Delegation: In Oracle, approvers can configure "approval delegates" and delegation periods (e.g., during travel) in personal settings. During delegation, all approval notifications auto-forward to the delegate. Path: My Account → Worklist → Vacation Rules.

模組 3：製造管理 Module 3: Manufacturing

從工作定義到工單執行，管理產品生產的全過程，包含資源調度、物料消耗和品質控制

From work definition to work order execution — managing the complete production process including scheduling, consumption, and quality

Work Definition Work Order Supply Types Backflush Outside Processing OEE

為什麼製造管理很重要？

Why Does Manufacturing Management Matter?

SmarTech 是一家生產高階筆記型電腦的組裝廠，每台筆電有超過 50 種零件。在導入 Oracle Manufacturing 之前，生產部門每天早上要花兩個小時手動整理「今天要做什麼」：倉庫主管打電話確認料件有沒有到、機台操作員等 Excel 排程表、品管人員紙本記錄每一道工序的合格率。一旦某個零件少了，整條線就停下來，而沒有人第一時間知道螢幕組件已經外包給哪個合約廠商、現在到了哪個工序。 SmarTech assembles high-end laptops with 50+ components per unit. Before implementing Oracle Manufacturing, the production team spent two hours every morning manually piecing together "what to build today": the warehouse supervisor called around to confirm parts had arrived, machine operators waited for an Excel schedule, and QC staff recorded pass rates on paper for each step. The moment a part was short, the entire line stopped — and nobody knew in real time which contract manufacturer was handling the screen assembly or what stage it had reached.

導入 Oracle Manufacturing Cloud 後，SmarTech 建立了一套「Work Definition」（工作定義），把筆電組裝拆成三道工序：底盤組裝（Operation 10）、主機板安裝（Operation 20）、螢幕組裝（Operation 30，外包）。系統根據每道工序的 Supply Type 自動決定物料如何補充：高價 CPU 晶片採 Push（預先發料），螺絲採 Assembly Pull（完工後自動扣帳），外包螢幕則自動觸發採購單到合約廠商。每張工單從「Unreleased → Released → In Progress → Complete → Closed」全程可追蹤。 After deploying Oracle Manufacturing Cloud, SmarTech built a "Work Definition" that breaks laptop assembly into three operations: Chassis Assembly (Op 10), Motherboard Install (Op 20), and Screen Assembly (Op 30 — outsourced). The system automatically determines how each component is replenished based on its Supply Type: high-value CPU chips use Push (pre-issued), screws use Assembly Pull (auto-deducted at completion), and the outsourced screen automatically generates a purchase order to the contract manufacturer. Every work order is tracked through its full lifecycle: Unreleased → Released → In Progress → Complete → Closed.

這個模組將帶你走過製造管理的每一個核心環節：從如何設計 Work Definition、選擇正確的 Supply Type、理解 Backflush 的庫存影響、到外包工序的採購整合，最後用 OEE（整體設備效能）量化你的生產效率。學完這個模組，你將能夠在 Oracle Cloud 中設定並執行一條完整的生產線。 This module walks you through every core element of manufacturing management: designing a Work Definition, choosing the right Supply Type, understanding Backflush inventory impact, integrating outside processing with procurement, and finally quantifying production efficiency with OEE. By the end, you'll be able to configure and execute a complete production line in Oracle Cloud.

🔑
核心洞察Core Insight
製造管理的本質是「資源排程 + 物料消耗 + 品質確認」三者的即時協調。Oracle Manufacturing 的價值在於讓這三件事在同一個系統裡自動化，消除紙本、電話和 Excel 的延遲。 Manufacturing management is fundamentally real-time coordination of three things: resource scheduling + material consumption + quality confirmation. Oracle Manufacturing's value is automating all three in one system, eliminating the lag of paper, phone calls, and spreadsheets.

⚠️
常見錯誤：過早關閉工單Common Mistake: Closing Too Early
工單一旦 Closed，所有成本差異即刻轉帳至 GL，無法再修改。如果有遺漏的發料或工時未回報，必須先在 Complete 狀態補齊，再執行 Close。 Once a Work Order is Closed, all cost variances are immediately posted to GL and cannot be reversed. If any material issues or labor hours are missing, complete them while the order is still in Complete status before running Close.

⭐ 核心功能一覽 ⭐ Key Features Overview

▼
📋

工作定義Work Definition

整合 BOM 與途程的生產模板。SmarTech 筆電工作定義包含 3 道工序、52 種物料、2 個工作中心，一次設定後所有工單自動繼承。Production template integrating BOM and routing. SmarTech's laptop Work Definition has 3 operations, 52 components, 2 work centers — set once and inherited by all work orders.

📦

Supply Type 物料補充Supply Type Control

6 種補充類型決定物料何時、如何計入工單。CPU（Push 預先發料）vs 螺絲（Assembly Pull 完工扣帳）vs 螢幕（Supplier 外包）三種截然不同的處理邏輯。6 replenishment types control when and how materials are charged. CPU (Push — pre-issued), screws (Assembly Pull — deducted at completion), screen (Supplier — outsourced) each follow completely different logic.

🔄

Backflush 自動扣料Backflush Auto-Deduction

完工回報時系統自動計算並扣除物料，無需手動發料。100 台筆電完工 → 系統自動扣 800 顆螺絲（每台 8 顆），零手工介入。System auto-calculates and deducts materials upon completion reporting. 100 laptops complete → system auto-deducts 800 screws (8 per unit), zero manual intervention.

🏢

Outside Processing 外包工序Outside Processing

工序設為外包時，系統自動建立 Purchase Requisition → Purchase Order。螢幕廠商收貨確認後，Oracle 自動更新工單進度，無需人工觸發。When an operation is flagged as outsourced, the system auto-creates a PR → PO. When the screen vendor confirms receipt, Oracle automatically updates work order progress — no manual trigger needed.

📅

排程：前排 / 後排Scheduling: Forward / Backward

前排（Forward）從開始日計算最早完工日；後排（Backward）從需求日倒推最晚開工日。SmarTech 用後排確保「6/30 出貨」的訂單不會延遲。Forward scheduling calculates earliest completion from start date; Backward scheduling calculates latest start from due date. SmarTech uses backward to ensure orders due 6/30 never slip.

📊

OEE 整體設備效能OEE Overall Equipment Effectiveness

可用率 × 效率 × 品質率 = OEE。SmarTech 主機板線：87% × 90% × 88% = 68.8%，系統自動計算並預警低效機台，協助找出瓶頸。Availability × Performance × Quality = OEE. SmarTech motherboard line: 87% × 90% × 88% = 68.8%. System auto-calculates and alerts on underperforming machines to identify bottlenecks.

📋 深入探討 1：工作定義 (Work Definition) 📋 Deep Dive 1: Work Definition

▼

Work Definition 是 Oracle Manufacturing 的生產模板，相當於傳統 ERP 中「BOM + Routing」的合體。它定義了：生產什麼（成品 Item）、分幾道工序（Operations）、每道工序用哪些物料（Components）、在哪個機台做（Work Center）、花多少時間（Resource Requirements）。工作定義本身不消耗庫存，只有建立工單後才會實際發生物料與資源的移動。 A Work Definition is Oracle Manufacturing's production template — equivalent to a traditional ERP "BOM + Routing" combined. It defines: what to build (finished item), how many operations, which components at each step, which work center, and how long each resource takes. The Work Definition itself doesn't consume inventory — actual material and resource movements only happen once a Work Order is created from it.

💡
Navigation： Manufacturing → Product Management → Work Definitions → Manage Work Definitions Navigation: Manufacturing → Product Management → Work Definitions → Manage Work Definitions

SmarTech 筆電工作定義：三道工序詳解SmarTech Laptop Work Definition: Three Operations in Detail

工序Operation 名稱Name 工作中心Work Center 標準工時Std Time 關鍵物料 (Supply Type)Key Components (Supply Type)
Op 10 底盤組裝Chassis Assembly WC-MECH-01 45 min/unit 底盤 (Push)、螺絲×8 (Assembly Pull)、散熱膏 (Bulk) Chassis (Push), Screws ×8 (Assembly Pull), Thermal Paste (Bulk)
Op 20 主機板安裝Motherboard Install WC-ELEC-02 60 min/unit 主機板 (Push)、CPU (Push)、RAM 16GB×2 (Operation Pull)、連接線組 (Phantom) Motherboard (Push), CPU (Push), RAM 16GB×2 (Operation Pull), Cable Harness (Phantom)
Op 30 螢幕組裝 (外包)Screen Assembly (Outsourced) WC-OSP-EXT 72 hr lead time 螢幕模組 (Supplier — 外包觸發 PO) Screen Module (Supplier — triggers outsourcing PO)
Work Definition 和 Work Order 的差別是什麼？ What's the difference between Work Definition and Work Order? ▶
Work Definition 是「模板」（藍圖），Work Order 是「執行實例」（實際訂單）。一個 Work Definition 可以產生無數個 Work Order。類比：Work Definition 像食譜，Work Order 像今天餐廳開的訂單。修改食譜不影響已在執行中的訂單。 A Work Definition is the "template" (blueprint); a Work Order is an "execution instance" (actual order). One Work Definition can generate unlimited Work Orders. Analogy: Work Definition is like a recipe, Work Order is like today's restaurant ticket. Changing the recipe doesn't affect tickets already in the kitchen.
可以針對單一工單修改 BOM 嗎？ Can I change the BOM after a Work Order is released? ▶
可以，但有限制。在 Released 或 In Progress 狀態下，你可以在工單層級新增或修改零件（稱為工單層級的 BOM 替代），但不能修改 Work Definition 本身去影響此訂單。常見情境：某零件缺貨，臨時替換為 RAM-16B 替代品，只需在工單上修改該筆零件，不影響其他工單或 Work Definition。 Yes, with limitations. In Released or In Progress status, you can add or modify components at the work order level (a work-order-level BOM substitution), but you cannot modify the Work Definition itself to affect this order. Common scenario: a component is out of stock, so you substitute RAM-16B as an alternative — change only that line on the work order without affecting other orders or the Work Definition.
⚠️
常見錯誤：忘記設定版本 (Version)Common Mistake: Forgetting to Set Version
Oracle 允許一個 Item 有多個 Work Definition 版本（例如舊版筆電用 V1，新款用 V2）。如果不設定有效日期範圍，系統可能拉取到錯誤版本，導致工單用錯 BOM。建議：每個版本務必設定「Effective From」和「Effective To」日期。 Oracle allows multiple Work Definition versions per item (e.g., old laptop uses V1, new model uses V2). Without proper effective date ranges, the system may pull the wrong version and generate work orders with the wrong BOM. Best practice: always set "Effective From" and "Effective To" dates on every version.

📦 深入探討 2：Supply Type 物料補充類型 📦 Deep Dive 2: Supply Types

▼

Supply Type 決定了每種零件「何時」以及「如何」從庫存移轉到工單。選錯 Supply Type 是製造系統最常見也最危險的設定錯誤之一——輕則庫存帳不準，重則成本核算錯誤。以下是六種類型的完整說明與 SmarTech 的實際應用。 Supply Type determines "when" and "how" each component moves from inventory to the work order. Choosing the wrong Supply Type is one of the most common and dangerous configuration errors in manufacturing systems — at best it causes inventory inaccuracies, at worst it corrupts cost accounting. Here are all six types with SmarTech's real-world usage.

Supply TypeSupply Type 扣料時機When Deducted 需要手動發料？Manual Issue? SmarTech 使用場景SmarTech Use Case 適用零件特性Best For
Push 工單 Released 時手動發料Manual issue after Release ✅ 是✅ Yes CPU Intel i9 ($450/ea) 高價值、需嚴格管控High-value, strict control needed
Operation Pull 該工序完成時自動扣帳Auto at operation completion ❌ 否（系統自動）❌ No (system auto) RAM 16GB (Op 20 完成時) 中價值、與特定工序綁定Mid-value, tied to specific operation
Assembly Pull 整張工單完工時自動扣帳Auto at full work order completion ❌ 否（系統自動）❌ No (system auto) 螺絲、墊片（完工後一次扣）Screws, washers (bulk deduct at completion) 低價值、高頻使用Low-value, high-frequency use
Bulk 不扣帳（週期盤點調整）Never deducted (cycle count) ❌ 否❌ No 散熱膏（按管使用）Thermal paste (tube-based usage) 極低價值、難以精確追蹤Very low-value, hard to track precisely
Phantom 展開子件，不扣帳本身Explodes to sub-components, itself not deducted ❌ 否（展開後子件各自管）❌ No (sub-items managed individually) 連接線組（包含 5 種線材）Cable harness (contains 5 wire types) 中間組件，只在 BOM 中存在Intermediate assembly that only exists in BOM
Supplier 外包廠商收料後觸發 PO 接收PO receipt from supplier ❌ 否（PO 自動觸發）❌ No (PO auto-triggered) 螢幕模組（Op 30 外包）Screen module (Op 30 outsourced) 外購或外包零件Bought-out or outsourced components

Phantom 展開邏輯：連接線組範例Phantom Explosion Logic: Cable Harness Example

SmarTech 的「連接線組 (CABLE-HARN-001)」在 Work Definition 中是 Phantom 類型。當工單建立時，系統「穿透」這個 Phantom 項目，直接將其下的 5 種子件加入工單 BOM：電源線 ×1、資料線 ×2、天線線 ×2、接地線 ×1、FFC 排線 ×3。倉庫中不存放「連接線組」這個半成品，倉庫員看到的只有這 5 種子件各自的庫存。 SmarTech's "Cable Harness (CABLE-HARN-001)" is set as Phantom in the Work Definition. When a work order is created, the system "passes through" this Phantom item and explodes its 5 sub-components directly onto the work order BOM: Power Cable ×1, Data Cable ×2, Antenna Wire ×2, Ground Cable ×1, FFC Ribbon ×3. The warehouse never stocks a "Cable Harness" sub-assembly — workers see only the 5 individual sub-components in inventory.

⚠️
Supply Type 錯選的後果Consequences of Wrong Supply Type
若把 CPU（Push）誤設為 Assembly Pull：CPU 不會在發料時扣帳，而是等到完工才扣。若在途中工單被取消，CPU 庫存帳和實物將出現落差。若把螺絲（Assembly Pull）誤設為 Push：每次發料都要手動操作，每台筆電 8 顆螺絲 × 1000 台 = 8000 筆手動交易，人工成本直線上升。 If CPU (should be Push) is set to Assembly Pull: the CPU isn't deducted at issue time — it waits until completion. If the work order is cancelled mid-run, physical CPU and book inventory diverge. If screws (should be Assembly Pull) are set to Push: every issue requires manual transaction — 8 screws × 1,000 laptops = 8,000 manual transactions, labor costs skyrocket.
Operation Pull 和 Assembly Pull 有什麼具體差異？什麼時候選哪個？ What's the concrete difference between Operation Pull and Assembly Pull? When to use which? ▶
Operation Pull：在特定工序（Operation）完工時扣帳。適用於與某道工序強綁定的零件。例如：RAM 只在 Op 20（主機板安裝）完成後才扣帳。如果工單做到 Op 20 就中止，RAM 會被扣帳但底盤不會（因為底盤在 Op 10）。

Assembly Pull：在整張工單的最後一道工序完工後才扣帳。適用於貫穿所有工序使用、難以歸屬到特定工序的低值零件（如螺絲）。若工單在 Op 20 中止，螺絲不會被扣帳（即使底盤組裝時已實際用掉螺絲）。 Operation Pull: deducts at the completion of a specific operation. Use for components tightly bound to one operation. Example: RAM deducts only when Op 20 (Motherboard Install) completes. If the work order stops at Op 20, RAM is deducted but the chassis is not (chassis belongs to Op 10).

Assembly Pull: deducts when the final operation of the entire work order completes. Use for low-value items used throughout all operations that can't be cleanly attributed to one step (like screws). If the work order stops at Op 20, screws are NOT deducted — even if physically used during chassis assembly.

🔄 深入探討 3：Backflush 自動扣料邏輯 🔄 Deep Dive 3: Backflush Logic — Step by Step

▼

Backflush（逆沖扣料）是指在生產完工時，系統「往回」自動計算並扣除應消耗的物料，而不是在生產前手動一一發料。Operation Pull 和 Assembly Pull 都是 Backflush 的形式，只是觸發時機不同。以下用 SmarTech 100 台筆電的工單，逐步展示庫存帳的變化。 Backflush means the system automatically calculates and deducts consumed materials "backward" at completion time, rather than requiring manual pre-issue transactions. Both Operation Pull and Assembly Pull are forms of backflush — they just trigger at different moments. Below is a step-by-step inventory walkthrough for SmarTech's 100-laptop work order.

情境：100 台筆電工單，逐步庫存影響Scenario: 100-Laptop Work Order — Step-by-Step Inventory Impact

時間點Timing 事件Event CPU 庫存CPU Stock RAM 庫存RAM Stock 螺絲庫存Screw Stock 觸發原因Trigger
工單建立前Before WO — 500 ea 1,000 ea 5,000 ea —
工單 ReleasedWO Released 手動發料 CPU ×100Manual issue CPU ×100 400 ea 1,000 ea 5,000 ea Push
Op 20 完工回報Op 20 Complete 系統自動扣 RAM ×200System auto-deducts RAM ×200 400 ea 800 ea 5,000 ea Operation Pull
工單完工 (Complete)WO Complete 系統自動扣螺絲 ×800System auto-deducts screws ×800 400 ea 800 ea 4,200 ea Assembly Pull
成品入庫FG Receipt 筆電 ×100 入成品倉Laptops ×100 into FG warehouse 400 ea 800 ea 4,200 ea 完工入庫Completion receipt
✅
Backflush 的效益：100 台筆電，如果所有零件都用 Push，需要 52 種零件 × 100 台 = 5,200 筆發料交易。改用 Backflush 後，倉庫只需執行 CPU ×100 這 1 筆 Push 交易，其他 51 種零件由系統自動處理，交易量減少 98%。 Backflush benefit: For 100 laptops, if all components used Push, you'd need 52 components × 100 laptops = 5,200 manual issue transactions. With backflush, the warehouse only executes 1 Push transaction (CPU ×100); the other 51 components are handled automatically — a 98% reduction in transactions.
如果工單取消，WIP 物料怎麼處理？ What happens to WIP materials if a Work Order is cancelled? ▶
取消工單前，必須先將已發出的物料「退回」庫存（Material Return 交易）。以 SmarTech 為例：如果工單在 Op 20 完成後取消，CPU ×100 已發料（Push 已扣帳），必須手動執行 Return to Inventory，將 CPU 退回。RAM 已被 Operation Pull 扣帳，同樣需要退料。螺絲尚未扣帳（Assembly Pull 未觸發），無需處理。系統提供「Return All Issued Components」快捷功能，可一鍵退回所有已發料項目。 Before cancelling a work order, you must "return" all issued materials to inventory (Material Return transaction). In SmarTech's case: if the work order is cancelled after Op 20 completes, CPU ×100 was Push-issued and must be manually returned via Return to Inventory. RAM was deducted by Operation Pull and also needs a return transaction. Screws were never deducted (Assembly Pull not yet triggered) — no action needed. Oracle provides a "Return All Issued Components" shortcut to return all issued items in one step.

🏢 深入探討 4：Outside Processing 外包工序 🏢 Deep Dive 4: Outside Processing

▼

Outside Processing（外包工序）是指將某道工序委託給外部廠商執行。Oracle 的強大之處在於：當工單執行到外包工序時，系統自動建立採購申請（PR）→ 採購單（PO），並在外包廠商完成後透過收貨（Receipt）自動更新工單進度。整個流程跨越 Manufacturing、Procurement 和 Inventory 三個模組，但使用者只需在製造端操作。 Outside Processing means delegating a specific operation to an external supplier. Oracle's strength: when a work order reaches an outsourced operation, the system automatically creates a Purchase Requisition (PR) → Purchase Order (PO), and when the supplier completes the work, a Receipt automatically updates the work order progress. The flow spans Manufacturing, Procurement, and Inventory — but the user only needs to work in the Manufacturing module.

SmarTech 螢幕外包完整流程SmarTech Screen Outsourcing: Complete Flow

Op 20 完工Op 20 Complete
主機板安裝完成Motherboard installed
▶

▶

💡
設定要點：Outside Processing 工序的 3 個必填項Setup Keys: 3 Required Fields for OSP Operation
  1. Outside Processing Item：設定外包服務的採購品項（例如 OSP-SCREEN-SVC），這是 PO 上的品項Outside Processing Item: The purchased service item used on the PO (e.g., OSP-SCREEN-SVC)
  2. Supplier：指定外包廠商（ScreenTech Ltd）及採購單位價格Supplier: Assign the outsource vendor (ScreenTech Ltd) and unit price
  3. Count Point：勾選此工序為計數點，收貨後才觸發工單進度更新Count Point: Mark this operation as a count point — progress only updates upon receipt
⚠️
常見錯誤：OSP Item 未設為 Outside Processing 類型Common Mistake: OSP Item Not Flagged as Outside Processing Type
採購品項（如 OSP-SCREEN-SVC）必須在 Item Master 中將 Item Type 設為「Outside Processing」，否則系統不會在工單執行到該工序時自動建立 PR。若忘記設定，採購員將無法看到自動產生的 PR，整個外包流程斷鏈。 The purchase item (e.g., OSP-SCREEN-SVC) must have its Item Type set to "Outside Processing" in the Item Master — otherwise the system won't auto-create a PR when the work order reaches that operation. If forgotten, the purchasing team will never see an auto-generated PR and the outsourcing chain breaks entirely.

📅 深入探討 5：排程 — 前排與後排 📅 Deep Dive 5: Scheduling — Forward and Backward

▼

Oracle Manufacturing 支援兩種排程方式。前排（Forward Scheduling）從已知的開工日往後計算，得出最早可完工日——適合回答「這批貨最快什麼時候可以交？」。後排（Backward Scheduling）從客戶要求的交貨日往前倒推，得出必須開工的最晚日期——適合回答「為了 6/30 出貨，我們最晚哪天要開始生產？」 Oracle Manufacturing supports two scheduling directions. Forward Scheduling calculates the earliest possible completion date starting from a known start date — answers "what's the soonest we can deliver this batch?" Backward Scheduling works from the customer's required date backward to find the latest allowable start date — answers "to ship by 6/30, what's the latest we can start production?"

SmarTech 排程計算範例SmarTech Scheduling Calculation Example

前排 (Forward)Forward 後排 (Backward)Backward
已知條件Given 開工日 6/16（週一）Start date: 6/16 (Mon) 需求日 6/30（週一）Due date: 6/30 (Mon)
Op 10 (45 min × 100 units) 6/16 08:00 → 6/17 09:30 ← 1.9 days
Op 20 (60 min × 100 units) 6/17 09:30 → 6/19 09:30 ← 2.5 days
Op 30 OSP (72 hr lead time) 6/19 → 6/22 (3 days) ← 3 days
結論Result 最早完工：6/22Earliest completion: 6/22 最晚開工：6/22 → 6/23 開工Latest start: must begin by 6/23
✅
工作中心日曆很關鍵：排程計算必須考量工作中心的可用時間（Work Center Calendar）。若 WC-ELEC-02 週末不開機，Op 20 不能排在週六/日，系統會自動跳過。SmarTech 的電子工作中心採用 5天8小時 日曆，OSP 外包工序使用 7天24小時 日曆（供應商不停工）。 Work Center Calendar is critical: Scheduling must respect each work center's available hours. If WC-ELEC-02 doesn't run weekends, Op 20 won't be scheduled on Saturday or Sunday — the system skips automatically. SmarTech's electronic work center uses a 5-day/8-hour calendar; the OSP operation uses a 7-day/24-hour calendar (the supplier runs non-stop).

📊 深入探討 6：OEE 整體設備效能 📊 Deep Dive 6: OEE — Overall Equipment Effectiveness

▼

OEE（Overall Equipment Effectiveness，整體設備效能）是衡量製造設備實際產能利用率的黃金指標，由三個維度相乘得出。OEE = 可用率（Availability）× 效率（Performance）× 品質率（Quality）。Oracle Manufacturing 的 OEE Dashboard 可以即時顯示每台機台的三項指標，並預警低效設備。 OEE (Overall Equipment Effectiveness) is the gold standard metric for measuring how effectively manufacturing equipment is utilized. OEE = Availability × Performance × Quality. Oracle Manufacturing's OEE Dashboard displays all three metrics in real time for each machine and alerts on underperforming equipment.

SmarTech 主機板安裝線 OEE 計算SmarTech Motherboard Line OEE Calculation

指標Metric 公式Formula SmarTech 數據SmarTech Data 計算結果Result
可用率 AvailabilityAvailability 實際運行時間 ÷ 計畫可用時間Actual Run Time ÷ Planned Time 7 小時 ÷ 8 小時（1 小時故障停機）7 hrs ÷ 8 hrs (1 hr breakdown) 87.5%
效率 PerformancePerformance 實際產量 ÷ 理論產量Actual Output ÷ Ideal Output 90 台 ÷（100 台/hr × 7hr → 理論 100）90 units vs. 100 unit/hr target 90%
品質率 QualityQuality 良品數 ÷ 總產出數Good Units ÷ Total Units 88 台合格 ÷ 100 台產出88 good ÷ 100 produced 88%
OEE 87.5% × 90% × 88% 低於世界級標準 (85%)Below world-class standard (85%) 69.3%
⚠️
OEE 69.3% 意味著什麼？What Does OEE 69.3% Mean?
這台機台僅發揮了 69.3% 的潛在產能。每天 8 小時中，有效生產良品的時間只有 5.5 小時。損失分析：可用率損失（1小時停機）= 消除目標；效率損失（速度慢 10%）= 查原因（操作員技能？換料？）；品質損失（12 台不良）= 找根本原因（錫膏量不足？）。世界級 OEE 目標通常設在 85% 以上。 This machine uses only 69.3% of its potential capacity. Of 8 available hours, only 5.5 hours produce good parts. Loss breakdown: Availability loss (1 hr downtime) — fix the breakdown root cause; Performance loss (10% speed gap) — investigate (operator skill? material change?); Quality loss (12 defects) — find root cause (solder paste volume?). World-class OEE target is typically 85% or above.
Product Genealogy（產品族譜）在 OEE 之外還能做什麼？ What can Product Genealogy do beyond OEE tracking? ▶
Product Genealogy 記錄每個序號產品從原料到成品的完整追蹤鏈。對 SmarTech 而言，每台筆電的序號對應到：使用了哪批次的 CPU（Lot ABC-2025-06）、哪台機台組裝（WC-ELEC-02, Machine #3）、哪個作業員操作、在哪個工序發現不良品。當客戶回報筆電故障時，可立即追查「同批 CPU 還裝在哪些其他台筆電上」，縮短召回範圍。Navigation: Manufacturing → Quality → Product Genealogy → Search by Serial Number Product Genealogy records the complete traceability chain from raw material to finished product for every serialized item. For SmarTech, each laptop serial number is linked to: which CPU lot was used (Lot ABC-2025-06), which machine assembled it (WC-ELEC-02, Machine #3), which operator, and at which operation a defect was found. When a customer reports a failure, you can instantly find all other laptops built with the same CPU lot and narrow any recall scope. Navigation: Manufacturing → Quality → Product Genealogy → Search by Serial Number

案例總結：製造模組的整合價值Case Summary: Integration Value of the Manufacturing Module
整個流程中，Manufacturing 模組自動觸發了 Procurement（OSP PO）、Inventory（Backflush 扣料、成品入庫）、和 Cost Accounting（差異轉帳）。計畫員全程只需執行 2 個關鍵操作：Release 工單 + Report Complete。其他 90% 的事務由系統自動完成。 Throughout this flow, the Manufacturing module automatically triggered Procurement (OSP PO), Inventory (backflush deductions, FG receipt), and Cost Accounting (variance posting). The planner needed to manually perform just 2 key actions: Release the WO + Report Complete. The other 90% of transactions were handled automatically by the system.

❓ 常見問題 FAQ ❓ Frequently Asked Questions

▼
Work Order 和 Flow Schedule 有什麼差別？什麼時候用哪個？ What is the difference between a Work Order and a Flow Schedule? When to use each? ▶

Work Order（離散製造）：適合每批次數量不固定、每張單獨立追蹤成本和進度的生產模式。SmarTech 的筆電每次生產批量不同（50 台、100 台、200 台），每張工單都需要獨立的成本核算和生產追蹤，所以用 Work Order。Work Order (Discrete Manufacturing): Best for production where batch size varies and each order needs independent cost and progress tracking. SmarTech's laptop batches vary (50, 100, 200 units) and each needs separate cost accounting — Work Order is the right choice.

Flow Schedule（流線製造）：適合連續生產、固定節拍（Takt Time）的流水線，例如每分鐘生產 10 個瓶蓋。Flow Schedule 不追蹤個別批次成本，強調產線平衡和節拍控制。若 SmarTech 改為 24 小時連續組裝、每 6 分鐘一台的流水線，Flow Schedule 更合適。Flow Schedule (Flow/Lean Manufacturing): Best for continuous production with fixed takt time, like 10 bottle caps per minute. Flow Schedules don't track individual batch costs — they focus on line balancing and rhythm. If SmarTech shifted to a 24/7 line producing one laptop every 6 minutes, Flow Schedule would be more appropriate.

工單 Released 後可以修改 BOM 嗎？ Can I change the BOM after a Work Order is released? ▶
可以，在工單層級（不是 Work Definition 層級）可以修改。操作路徑：Manufacturing → Work Orders → 選取工單 → Components 頁籤 → 新增/修改/刪除零件。限制：已 Backflush 扣帳的零件（Operation Pull 或 Assembly Pull 已執行）無法被刪除；已 Push 發料完成的零件需先退料才能修改數量。建議：所有工單層級的 BOM 修改都應記錄原因（備注欄），以便後續稽核和成本差異分析。 Yes, at the work order level (not the Work Definition level). Navigation: Manufacturing → Work Orders → select WO → Components tab → Add/Modify/Delete components. Restrictions: components already deducted by backflush (Operation Pull or Assembly Pull already executed) cannot be deleted; Push-issued components require a return transaction before you can change the quantity. Best practice: always document the reason for any WO-level BOM change in the notes field for audit trails and variance analysis.
工單取消後，WIP 物料怎麼辦？庫存會自動回補嗎？ What happens to WIP materials if a Work Order is cancelled? Does inventory auto-restore? ▶
不會自動回補。取消工單前，系統會警告你有未退料的零件。你必須手動執行 Material Return 交易，將已發料的物料退回倉庫。操作路徑：Manufacturing → Work Orders → 選取工單 → Actions → Return All Components。系統會顯示所有已發料項目及數量，你可以全部退回或部分退回（若有部分已實際消耗）。退料完成後才能執行 Cancel。注意：已被 Backflush 扣帳的零件同樣需要退料，系統不會因為取消工單而自動反轉 Backflush 交易。 Inventory is NOT automatically restored. Before you can cancel, the system warns you of any unreturned components. You must manually execute Material Return transactions to return issued materials to the warehouse. Navigation: Manufacturing → Work Orders → select WO → Actions → Return All Components. The system lists all issued items and quantities; you can return all or partial amounts (if some were actually consumed). Only after all returns are complete can you execute Cancel. Important: components deducted by backflush also require return transactions — cancelling the work order does NOT automatically reverse backflush transactions.
Phantom 品項在 Work Definition 中怎麼展開？工單上會看到 Phantom 本身嗎？ How does a Phantom item explode in a Work Definition? Does the Phantom itself appear on the Work Order? ▶
Phantom 品項在工單建立時被「穿透展開」：工單的零件清單只顯示 Phantom 的子件，不顯示 Phantom 本身。這是刻意設計的——Phantom 只是 BOM 的邏輯分組工具，倉庫中不存在這個半成品的庫存。

SmarTech 範例：Work Definition 中有「連接線組 CABLE-HARN-001」(Phantom)，其下有 5 種子件。工單建立後，零件清單顯示：電源線 ×1、資料線 ×2、天線線 ×2、接地線 ×1、FFC 排線 ×3。連接線組本身不出現。倉管直接對這 5 種子件進行發料和盤點，不需要「組裝連接線組」這個動作。 Phantom items are "explosion-passed through" at work order creation time: only the Phantom's sub-components appear on the work order component list — the Phantom itself does not appear. This is by design — Phantoms are purely logical BOM grouping tools; no physical inventory of the phantom sub-assembly exists in the warehouse.

SmarTech example: the Work Definition contains "Cable Harness CABLE-HARN-001" (Phantom) with 5 sub-components. After work order creation, the component list shows: Power Cable ×1, Data Cable ×2, Antenna Wire ×2, Ground Cable ×1, FFC Ribbon ×3. The Cable Harness itself never appears. Warehouse staff issue and count these 5 individual items directly — there's no "assemble the harness" step.

模組 4：訂單管理 Module 4: Order Management

從客戶下單到出貨開票的 Order-to-Cash 流程，核心是 Orchestration 設計和全球訂單承諾 Order-to-Cash from customer order to invoice — centered on Orchestration design and Global Order Promising

Order-to-Cash Orchestration GOP/ATP Pricing Jeopardy
🔑
真實場景：MegaRetail 的訂單管理挑戰Real Scenario: MegaRetail's Order Management Challenge

MegaRetail 是一家中型零售商，每天接到 500 筆訂單。導入 Oracle Fusion 前，業務人員在 Excel 上手動跟單，承諾交期靠「感覺」，常常承諾了客戶 3 天交貨，結果發現庫存根本不夠，倉管收到紙本揀貨單又看不清楚，出貨後還要再手動輸入 AR 系統開票。整個 Order-to-Cash 流程像一條破爛的傳送帶——每個環節都靠人工，錯誤率居高不下，VIP 客戶的優惠價格也常常搞錯。 MegaRetail is a mid-size retailer processing 500 orders daily. Before Oracle Fusion, sales reps tracked orders manually in Excel, delivery promises were based on gut feel, and they routinely committed to 3-day delivery only to discover insufficient stock. Warehouse staff received illegible paper pick tickets, and after shipping, AR invoices had to be re-keyed into a separate system. The entire Order-to-Cash process resembled a broken conveyor belt — every step was manual, error rates were high, and VIP customer discount pricing was frequently applied incorrectly.

導入 Oracle Order Management 後，MegaRetail 設計了三條 Orchestration Process：標準訂單走 ATP 庫存確認後直接出貨，Back-to-Back 訂單自動觸發採購，Drop Shipment 則直接通知供應商出貨給客戶。VIP 客戶憑 Customer Class = GOLD 自動路由到專屬流程，同時套用含 15% 折扣的 Pricing Strategy，整個過程完全自動化，人工介入點僅剩例外管理。 After implementing Oracle Order Management, MegaRetail designed three Orchestration Processes: standard orders follow ATP inventory confirmation then ship directly; Back-to-Back orders automatically trigger purchase orders; Drop Shipment notifies suppliers to ship directly to customers. VIP customers with Customer Class = GOLD are automatically routed to a dedicated process with a 15% discount Pricing Strategy applied — the entire flow is fully automated, with human intervention only at exception points.

本模組將帶你深入理解這套架構：如何設計 Orchestration Process、如何讓 GOP 即時計算 ATP 日期、如何設定三層 Pricing 讓折扣自動疊加、如何用 Jeopardy 機制提早預警訂單風險。每個概念都會配合 MegaRetail 的具體數字說明，讓你學完就能直接在專案中應用。 This module takes you deep into this architecture: how to design Orchestration Processes, how GOP calculates ATP dates in real time, how to configure three-tier Pricing so discounts stack automatically, and how Jeopardy flags order risks early. Every concept is grounded in MegaRetail's specific numbers so you can apply what you learn directly to your own project.

Order-to-Cash 全流程概覽

Order-to-Cash End-to-End Overview

Oracle Order Management 的訂單生命週期由 Orchestration Process 驅動，每一個 Task（任務）對應一個業務動作，系統依序執行，直到訂單完成結案。以下是標準 O2C 流程的八個核心步驟： Oracle Order Management's order lifecycle is driven by Orchestration Processes. Each Task maps to a business action, and the system executes them in sequence until the order is closed. Below are the eight core steps of a standard O2C flow:

核心功能概覽

Key Features Overview

🎼

Orchestration ProcessOrchestration Process

定義訂單從建立到結案的完整任務序列。MegaRetail 標準訂單的 Orchestration 包含 8 個 Task，Back-to-Back 訂單多出「Create PO」和「Wait for PO Receipt」兩個任務，讓供應鏈動作自動串聯。 Defines the complete task sequence from order creation to closure. MegaRetail's standard Orchestration has 8 Tasks; Back-to-Back adds "Create PO" and "Wait for PO Receipt," automatically chaining supply chain actions.

🌐

Global Order Promising (GOP)Global Order Promising (GOP)

即時計算能否在要求日期前交貨。庫存 1000 件、已確認供應 500 件、需求 1200 件，ATP = 300 件，系統自動告知客戶可承諾數量和最早交期，避免過度承諾。 Real-time calculation of whether requested delivery dates are achievable. With 1,000 units on hand, 500 confirmed supply, and 1,200 demand, ATP = 300 units — the system tells customers what can be promised and when, preventing over-commitment.

💰

三層 Pricing 架構Three-Tier Pricing

Base Price List → Pricing Strategy → Promotion 三層疊加。MegaRetail Widget-A 定價 $1,000，合作夥伴策略折扣 10% = $900，促銷再折 5% = $855，全程自動計算，不需業務手動改價。 Base Price List → Pricing Strategy → Promotion stacking. MegaRetail Widget-A at $1,000, partner strategy 10% discount = $900, promotion -5% = $855, calculated automatically without manual rep adjustments.

🔗

Back-to-Back 訂單Back-to-Back Orders

客戶訂單自動觸發採購訂單，料號一對一連結。當 PO 收料完成，系統自動更新 SO 的履約狀態，不需人工介入。適合不庫存的客製品或進口品。 Customer orders automatically trigger purchase orders with one-to-one item linkage. When the PO is received, the system auto-updates the SO fulfillment status — no manual action needed. Ideal for custom or imported items not held in stock.

⚠️

Jeopardy 預警Jeopardy Alerting

系統持續監控每筆訂單是否可能延誤，依風險評分分為 Low / Medium / High。High Jeopardy 自動發信給客服主管，讓客服在客戶投訴前主動聯絡，提升客戶滿意度。 Continuously monitors each order for potential delays, scoring risk as Low / Medium / High. High Jeopardy triggers automatic email to CS managers, enabling proactive customer contact before complaints arise.

🚫

Hold & Processing ConstraintsHold & Processing Constraints

Hold 可暫停整張訂單或特定訂單行，Processing Constraints 則防止不當欄位修改（例如出貨後不得改品項）。兩者共同構成訂單管控防線，減少人為錯誤。 Holds pause entire orders or specific lines; Processing Constraints prevent inappropriate field changes (e.g., no item changes after shipping). Together they form the order control layer, reducing human error.

🎼 深入解析：Orchestration Process 設計 🎼 Deep Dive: Orchestration Process Design

▼

Orchestration Process 是 Oracle Order Management 的「大腦」，定義每筆訂單必須依序完成哪些任務（Task）。每個 Task 可以是同步（Synchronous，等待完成再往下）或非同步（Asynchronous，發出指令後繼續）。設計時需考慮：哪些任務可以並行、哪些必須等待外部系統回應、哪些情況需要人工干預。 Orchestration Process is the "brain" of Oracle Order Management, defining which Tasks must be completed in sequence for each order. Each Task can be Synchronous (wait for completion before proceeding) or Asynchronous (issue instruction and continue). Design considerations: which tasks can run in parallel, which need to wait for external system responses, and which scenarios require human intervention.

三種流程範例：MegaRetail 實際配置 Three Process Examples: MegaRetail's Actual Configuration

流程名稱Process Name 適用場景Use Case Task 序列（簡化）Task Sequence (simplified) 關鍵差異Key Difference
MR_STANDARD 一般庫存品Standard stock items Credit Check → ATP → Reserve → Pick Wave → Ship Confirm → Invoice 最快 1 天完成Can complete in 1 day
MR_B2B 客製品、不庫存品Custom/non-stock items Credit Check → ATP → Create PO → Wait PO Receipt → Reserve → Pick Wave → Ship Confirm → Invoice 多兩個 PO 任務Two additional PO tasks
MR_DROP_SHIP 供應商直寄客戶Supplier ships to customer Credit Check → Create PO (ship-to=customer) → Receive PO (logical) → Invoice 無需實際入庫No physical warehouse receipt

Process Assignment 規則：VIP 路由邏輯 Process Assignment Rules: VIP Routing Logic

Process Assignment 決定哪張訂單走哪條流程。MegaRetail 的路由邏輯： Process Assignment determines which order follows which process. MegaRetail's routing logic:

條件Condition 分配流程Assigned Process 優先序Priority
Order Type = VIP Sales Order AND Customer Class = GOLD MR_STANDARD (高優先批次) 1
Item.Source Type = Buy AND Item.Shippable = No MR_DROP_SHIP 2
Item.Source Type = Buy MR_B2B 3
其他Default MR_STANDARD 99
✅
設定路徑：Setup → Order Management → Orchestration Processes → Process Assignment Rules。優先序數字越小越優先，建議每條 Rule 間距留 10（10, 20, 30...），方便日後插入新規則。 Setup path: Setup → Order Management → Orchestration Processes → Process Assignment Rules. Lower priority numbers take precedence. Leave gaps of 10 between rules (10, 20, 30...) to allow future insertions.
Q：同一張訂單不同行可以走不同 Orchestration Process 嗎？Q: Can different lines on the same order follow different Orchestration Processes?▶
可以。Process Assignment 是以訂單行（Order Line）為單位評估的，不是以整張訂單為單位。例如同一張 SO，第 1 行是庫存品走 MR_STANDARD，第 2 行是客製品走 MR_B2B。系統會分別管理各行的 Orchestration 狀態，互不干擾。 Yes. Process Assignment is evaluated at the Order Line level, not the order header level. For example, on the same SO, Line 1 (stock item) follows MR_STANDARD while Line 2 (custom item) follows MR_B2B. The system manages each line's Orchestration status independently.
Q：Orchestration Process 設好後可以修改嗎？Q: Can an Orchestration Process be modified after it's been set up?▶
已有訂單在執行中的 Process 不建議直接修改，因為現有訂單行的 Task 狀態已固定。正確做法是建一個新版本的 Process（版本號遞增），新訂單自動套用新版本，舊訂單繼續走舊版本。Oracle 系統也允許對進行中訂單手動切換流程，但需要適當的職能授權。 Directly modifying a Process with active orders is not recommended, as existing order line task states are already fixed. The correct approach is to create a new version of the Process (incremented version number) — new orders automatically use the new version while existing orders continue on the old version. Oracle also allows manually switching processes for in-progress orders, but this requires appropriate role authorization.
⚠️
常見錯誤：Process Assignment Rules 的條件設太寬泛，導致所有訂單都落入同一條流程。建議用「Order Type + Item Source Type」雙條件組合，確保分流精準。另外，忘記設「Default」兜底規則會導致系統報錯無法找到對應 Process。 Common mistake: Overly broad Process Assignment Rule conditions cause all orders to fall into the same process. Recommended to use "Order Type + Item Source Type" dual-condition combinations for precise routing. Also, forgetting to set a "Default" catch-all rule will cause system errors when no matching process is found.

🌐 深入解析：Global Order Promising (GOP) / ATP 計算 🌐 Deep Dive: Global Order Promising (GOP) / ATP Calculation

▼

Global Order Promising (GOP) 是 Oracle Supply Chain Planning 的子功能，與 Order Management 整合，在訂單建立或修改時即時計算「最早可承諾交期」和「可承諾數量」。GOP 支援三種計算模式：ATP、CTP、PTP，各適用不同業務場景。 Global Order Promising (GOP) is a sub-function of Oracle Supply Chain Planning, integrated with Order Management to calculate "earliest promising date" and "available-to-promise quantity" in real time when orders are created or modified. GOP supports three calculation modes: ATP, CTP, and PTP, each suited to different business scenarios.

ATP 計算範例：Widget-A 的數字 ATP Calculation Example: Widget-A Numbers

項目Item 數量（件）Quantity (units) 說明Description
現有庫存（On Hand）On-Hand Inventory 1,000 倉庫實際可用庫存Physically available in warehouse
已確認入庫（Confirmed Supply）Confirmed Supply +500 在途 PO，預計 5 天後到In-transit PO, expected in 5 days
已承諾需求（Demand）Committed Demand -1,200 已承諾給其他訂單的數量Quantity already committed to other orders
ATP（可承諾數量）ATP (Available to Promise) 300 = 1,000 + 500 - 1,200= 1,000 + 500 - 1,200

當 MegaRetail 的業務輸入新訂單要求 400 件 Widget-A 時，ATP=300，系統有兩個回應：(a) 承諾 300 件可立即出貨，100 件需等下一批 PO 到貨（分批交貨模式），或 (b) 計算最早何時能湊齊 400 件並承諾一個完整交期。業務可在 Order Management 介面即時看到這個計算結果。 When MegaRetail's sales rep enters a new order requesting 400 units of Widget-A with ATP=300, the system has two responses: (a) promise 300 units for immediate shipment and 100 units pending the next PO arrival (split shipment mode), or (b) calculate the earliest date when all 400 units can be fulfilled and promise a single delivery date. The sales rep sees this calculation in real time in the Order Management interface.

ATP vs CTP vs PTP：何時用哪種？ ATP vs CTP vs PTP: When to Use Each?

模式Mode 全稱Full Name 檢查項目Checks 適用場景Best For MegaRetail 使用MegaRetail Usage
ATP Available to Promise 庫存 + 已確認供應On-hand + confirmed supply 標準庫存品Standard stock items 標準訂單流程Standard order process
CTP Capable to Promise ATP + 產能 + 物料ATP + capacity + materials 製造型企業、MTO 產品Manufacturers, MTO products 客製品訂單Custom item orders
PTP Profitable to Promise ATP + 利潤分析ATP + profitability analysis 資源有限、需優先高利潤訂單Limited resources, prioritize high-margin orders 季末大促衝刺時Year-end sales pushes
💡
CTP 觸發時機：當 ATP 數量不足但客戶要求仍需滿足時，系統觸發 CTP，進一步檢查工廠產能（Work Center 可用時數）和物料（BOM 展開後各物料的 ATP），計算是否能臨時製造出所需數量及最早完工日。CTP 需要 Manufacturing + Supply Chain Planning 模組同時啟用才能運作。 When CTP fires: When ATP quantity is insufficient but the customer's requirement must still be met, the system triggers CTP to further check factory capacity (Work Center available hours) and materials (ATP of each material after BOM explosion), calculating whether temporary production is feasible and the earliest completion date. CTP requires both Manufacturing and Supply Chain Planning modules to be active.
Q：供應計畫改變後，GOP 承諾日期會自動更新嗎？Q: When supply plans change, do GOP promise dates auto-update?▶
GOP 會定期重新計算（通常是每日批次）或由事件觸發（如 PO 延期、庫存調整）。當重算發現某訂單的承諾日期無法維持時，系統會觸發 Jeopardy 警示，提醒客服人員主動聯絡客戶協商新的交期。業務也可在訂單詳情頁手動點擊「重新承諾」（Re-Promise）來即時取得最新 ATP 計算結果。 GOP recalculates periodically (usually daily batch) or is event-triggered (e.g., PO delays, inventory adjustments). When recalculation finds a promise date can no longer be met, the system triggers a Jeopardy alert, prompting CS reps to proactively contact the customer to negotiate a new date. Sales reps can also manually click "Re-Promise" on the order detail page to get an instant updated ATP calculation.
⚠️
常見錯誤：ATP 計算未包含所有供應來源（如部分倉庫未納入 GOP 範圍），導致實際可用量低於系統顯示。設定時務必在 Setup → Supply Chain Planning → Organizations 確認所有相關倉庫都已加入 GOP 的 Supply Network。 Common mistake: ATP calculation doesn't include all supply sources (e.g., some warehouses excluded from GOP scope), causing actual available quantity to appear lower than what the system shows. Always verify in Setup → Supply Chain Planning → Organizations that all relevant warehouses are included in the GOP Supply Network.

💰 深入解析：三層 Pricing 架構 💰 Deep Dive: Three-Tier Pricing Architecture

▼

Oracle Order Management 的定價採用三層結構：Price List（基礎定價）→ Pricing Strategy（策略折扣）→ Promotion（促銷活動）。每一層都有自己的生效條件，系統依優先序套疊計算最終售價。這個架構的優點是：業務人員不需要手動改價，所有折扣邏輯都在設定層管理。 Oracle Order Management uses a three-tier pricing structure: Price List (base pricing) → Pricing Strategy (strategy discounts) → Promotion (promotional activities). Each tier has its own activation conditions, and the system stacks them in priority order to calculate the final selling price. The advantage: sales reps never manually adjust prices — all discount logic is managed at the configuration level.

具體範例：Widget-A 的定價計算 Concrete Example: Widget-A Pricing Calculation

Price ListPrice List
Widget-A 基準Widget-A base
$1,000
▶
Pricing StrategyPricing Strategy
合作夥伴 -10%Partner -10%
$900
▶
PromotionPromotion
夏季促銷 -5%Summer Promo -5%
$855
▶
最終售價Final Price
客戶帳單金額Invoiced amount
$855
定價層Pricing Tier 設定物件Configuration Object 套用條件Applied When MegaRetail 範例MegaRetail Example
第一層 Price List 品號 + 貨幣Item + Currency MR_USD_PRICELIST: Widget-A = $1,000
第二層 Pricing Strategy 客戶區段 (Customer Segment) = PARTNERCustomer Segment = PARTNER PARTNER_STRATEGY: 套用 Price List + 10% 折扣
第三層 Promotion 訂單日期在促銷期間內Order date within promotion period SUMMER2025: 2025-06-01 ~ 2025-08-31，再折 5%
✅
設定路徑：
• Price List：Pricing → Price Lists → Manage Price Lists
• Pricing Strategy：Pricing → Pricing Strategies → Manage Pricing Strategies
• Segment：Pricing → Customer Pricing Profiles → Manage Customer Segments
• Promotion：Pricing → Promotions → Manage Promotions Setup paths:
• Price List: Pricing → Price Lists → Manage Price Lists
• Pricing Strategy: Pricing → Pricing Strategies → Manage Pricing Strategies
• Segment: Pricing → Customer Pricing Profiles → Manage Customer Segments
• Promotion: Pricing → Promotions → Manage Promotions
Q：Promotion 折扣是疊加在 Strategy 之後，還是各自獨立計算後取最低？Q: Do Promotion discounts stack on top of Strategy discounts, or do they each calculate independently and take the lowest?▶
預設是「疊加（Stacking）」。即 Strategy 先算完得到中間價，再由 Promotion 對中間價套折扣。上例：$1,000 × (1-10%) = $900，再 × (1-5%) = $855。你也可以在 Pricing Strategy 中設定 Promotion 的「互斥性」，讓系統在多個 Promotion 同時符合時只取最優一個，避免過度折扣。 The default is "Stacking." Strategy calculates first to get an intermediate price, then Promotion discounts the intermediate price. In our example: $1,000 × (1-10%) = $900, then × (1-5%) = $855. You can also configure "Promotion Exclusivity" in the Pricing Strategy so the system takes only the best single Promotion when multiple qualify, preventing excessive discounting.
⚠️
常見錯誤：Pricing Strategy 與客戶的關聯設錯。Strategy 是透過「Customer Pricing Profile」→「Customer Segment」→「Pricing Strategy」的鏈結套用到客戶，如果客戶未指派到正確 Segment，就會沿用預設的 Price List，折扣不會生效。每次有 VIP 客戶反映價格問題，先檢查客戶的 Customer Pricing Profile 是否正確。 Common mistake: Incorrect linkage between Pricing Strategy and customers. Strategies are applied through "Customer Pricing Profile" → "Customer Segment" → "Pricing Strategy." If a customer isn't assigned to the correct Segment, the default Price List is used and discounts won't apply. When a VIP customer reports a pricing issue, first check whether their Customer Pricing Profile is correctly configured.

⚠️ 深入解析：Jeopardy 預警機制 ⚠️ Deep Dive: Jeopardy Alerting Mechanism

▼

Jeopardy 是 Oracle Order Management 的訂單風險預警系統。系統根據當前 Task 完成狀態、承諾交期與實際進度差距，計算每筆訂單的風險分數，分為三個等級：Low（低風險）、Medium（中風險）、High（高風險），讓客服人員提前介入，不必等客戶投訴才知道訂單出問題。 Jeopardy is Oracle Order Management's order risk alerting system. Based on current Task completion status and the gap between promised and actual delivery timelines, the system calculates a risk score for each order at three levels: Low, Medium, and High — enabling CS reps to intervene proactively rather than waiting for customer complaints.

風險等級Risk Level 觸發條件範例Example Trigger Conditions 建議動作Recommended Action
Low Task 進度略慢，承諾日期仍可達成Task progress slightly slow but promise date still achievable 系統記錄，不主動通知System logs, no proactive notification
Medium Pick Wave 未在承諾前 2 天完成；PO 收料延誤 1 天Pick Wave not completed 2 days before promise; PO receipt delayed 1 day 在 Jeopardy Dashboard 顯示，客服人員需在 24 小時內處理Displayed in Jeopardy Dashboard, CS rep must action within 24 hours
High 承諾日期確定無法達成；關鍵 Task 卡住超過閾值；Hold 未解除Promise date confirmed unachievable; critical Task blocked beyond threshold; Hold not released 自動發 Email 給客服主管 + 客戶，要求立即聯絡客戶協商Auto-email CS manager + customer, requiring immediate contact to negotiate
💡
Jeopardy Dashboard 路徑：Order Management → Overview → Jeopardy。可按客戶、業務代表、產品類別篩選，也可設定自動排程通知。Jeopardy 閾值（觸發 Medium/High 的天數差距）在 Setup → Order Management → Jeopardy Rules 中設定。 Jeopardy Dashboard path: Order Management → Overview → Jeopardy. Filterable by customer, sales rep, and product category; automatic scheduled notifications can also be configured. Jeopardy thresholds (day gaps that trigger Medium/High) are configured in Setup → Order Management → Jeopardy Rules.
Q：Jeopardy 只看承諾日期，還是會考慮客戶的重要性？Q: Does Jeopardy only look at promise dates, or does it consider customer importance?▶
Jeopardy Rules 可以設定額外的加權條件，例如 VIP 客戶（Customer Class = GOLD）訂單的閾值收緊為 1 天（一般客戶是 3 天），這樣 VIP 訂單稍有延誤就立即升為 High Jeopardy，確保 VIP 客戶的訂單得到最高優先的關注。MegaRetail 就採用這個設定，讓客服主管每天早上看到的 High Jeopardy 清單優先都是 GOLD 客戶的問題。 Jeopardy Rules can include additional weighting conditions. For example, VIP customer (Customer Class = GOLD) orders can have a tighter threshold of 1 day (vs. 3 days for regular customers), so any delay immediately escalates to High Jeopardy, ensuring VIP orders receive highest-priority attention. MegaRetail uses this configuration, so the CS manager's morning High Jeopardy list is dominated by GOLD customer issues.
⚠️
常見錯誤：Jeopardy Email 通知設定了但沒人看。建議在上線初期指定專人每天早上 9 點檢視 Jeopardy Dashboard，並把 High Jeopardy 的 Email 發給 CS Team 的 Group Mailbox 而非個人信箱，避免人員請假時漏看。 Common mistake: Jeopardy email notifications are configured but nobody reads them. Recommend designating a specific person to review the Jeopardy Dashboard every morning at 9am during go-live, and send High Jeopardy emails to a CS Team Group Mailbox rather than individual inboxes, preventing missed alerts during staff absences.

🔗 深入解析：Back-to-Back 訂單與 Drop Shipment 🔗 Deep Dive: Back-to-Back Orders & Drop Shipment

▼

Back-to-Back (B2B) 訂單是指：客戶銷售訂單（SO）建立後，系統自動產生一張對應的採購訂單（PO），SO 行與 PO 行之間有明確的一對一連結。當 PO 收料入庫後，相關 SO 行的庫存即自動預留並推進出貨流程。這個機制適合「不庫存但需要從供應商採購後出給客戶」的品項。 Back-to-Back (B2B) orders work as follows: after a customer Sales Order (SO) is created, the system automatically generates a corresponding Purchase Order (PO) with a clear one-to-one linkage between SO line and PO line. When the PO receipt arrives, inventory is automatically reserved for the SO line and the shipment process advances. This mechanism suits items that aren't stocked but must be procured from suppliers before delivery to customers.

B2B vs Drop Shipment vs 標準訂單：如何選擇？ B2B vs Drop Shipment vs Standard: How to Choose?

情境Scenario 標準訂單Standard Back-to-BackBack-to-Back Drop ShipmentDrop Shipment
庫存來源Inventory source 自有庫存Own stock 採購後入庫再出貨Buy, receive, then ship 供應商直接寄客戶Supplier ships direct
實體入庫Physical receipt 已有庫存Already in stock ✅ 需要Required ❌ 邏輯入庫Logical receipt only
適用品項Best for 庫存品Stock items 進口品、客製品、高值品Imported, custom, high-value 大型設備、直送品Large equipment, direct-delivery
發票Invoice 出貨後開票After shipment 出貨後開票After shipment 邏輯收貨後開票After logical receipt

B2B 訂單的自動連結與結案邏輯 B2B Order Auto-Linking and Closure Logic

MegaRetail 的客製品訂單流程：客戶訂購 Widget-C（客製品）100 件 → SO 行建立，Orchestration 任務「Create PO」執行 → 系統自動產生 PO-1001，供應商：ABC製造，數量 100 件，交貨地：MegaRetail 台北倉 → 供應商交貨，倉庫執行 PO 收料（PO-1001 收料 100 件）→ Orchestration 任務「Wait for PO Receipt」完成，SO 行自動預留庫存 → 揀貨出貨 → SO 行結案，系統自動關閉 PO-1001 相關的 B2B 連結。 MegaRetail's custom item order flow: Customer orders Widget-C (custom item), 100 units → SO line created, Orchestration task "Create PO" executes → system auto-generates PO-1001, Supplier: ABC Manufacturing, Qty 100, Deliver-to: MegaRetail Taipei Warehouse → Supplier delivers, warehouse receives PO (PO-1001 receipt: 100 units) → Orchestration task "Wait for PO Receipt" completes, SO line auto-reserves inventory → Pick and ship → SO line closes, system automatically closes the B2B linkage for PO-1001.

Q：B2B PO 數量和 SO 數量可以不一樣嗎？Q: Can the B2B PO quantity differ from the SO quantity?▶
通常系統預設 PO 數量等於 SO 行需求量。但你可以在 Orchestration Task 設定中允許數量不一致，例如供應商最小採購量（MOQ）比客戶訂量大。多採購的部分可以轉入一般庫存。建議在 Processing Constraints 中設定：B2B SO 行出貨後不得修改數量，避免 SO 減量但 PO 已收料完成的矛盾。 By default the system sets PO quantity equal to SO line demand. However, you can configure the Orchestration Task to allow quantity mismatches — for example, when the supplier's Minimum Order Quantity (MOQ) exceeds the customer's order. Excess-purchased quantities can be transferred to general inventory. Recommend setting Processing Constraints so B2B SO line quantities cannot be modified after shipment, preventing the contradiction of SO reduction after PO receipt is complete.
⚠️
常見錯誤：B2B PO 已收料但 SO 行被取消，導致庫存無處去。應在 Orchestration 設計時加入「PO 收料後不允許取消 SO 行」的 Processing Constraint，或設定取消 SO 行時自動觸發退貨流程給供應商（Return to Supplier）。 Common mistake: B2B PO receipt is complete but the SO line gets cancelled, leaving inventory stranded. When designing the Orchestration, add a Processing Constraint preventing SO line cancellation after PO receipt, or configure automatic Return to Supplier when an SO line is cancelled post-receipt.

🚚 深入解析：Pick Wave → Ship Confirm 倉庫作業 🚚 Deep Dive: Pick Wave → Ship Confirm Warehouse Operations

▼

Pick Wave 是 Oracle Inventory Management 的出貨準備功能，將多張 SO 的揀貨需求合並成一波次（Wave），讓倉管人員一次掃描、批量完成揀貨。完成後依序進行 Pick Confirm（確認揀貨完成）和 Ship Confirm（確認出貨），庫存才會從「已預留」變成「實際扣減」。 Pick Wave is Oracle Inventory Management's shipment preparation feature, consolidating pick requirements from multiple SOs into a single wave, allowing warehouse staff to scan and complete picks in batch. After completion, Pick Confirm (confirm picking done) and Ship Confirm (confirm shipped) are executed sequentially — only then does inventory shift from "reserved" to "actually decremented."

逐步操作與庫存影響時間點 Step-by-Step Operations and Inventory Impact Timing

步驟Step 操作Action 庫存狀態變化Inventory Status Change Oracle 路徑Oracle Path
1 ATP 確認 / 預留ATP Confirm / Reserve Soft Reserve → 庫存仍在帳，標記為已承諾Soft Reserve → inventory still on books, marked committed GOP → Reserve Inventory
2 建立 Pick WaveCreate Pick Wave 無庫存異動，產生揀貨清單No inventory change, generates pick list Inventory → Pick Wave → Create Wave
3 Pick ConfirmPick Confirm 庫存移至「已揀貨」次狀態（Sub-inventory 轉移）Inventory moves to "Picked" sub-status (sub-inventory transfer) Inventory → Picks → Confirm Picks
4 Ship ConfirmShip Confirm 庫存正式扣減，SO 行狀態 → ShippedInventory formally decremented, SO line status → Shipped Shipping → Trips/Stops → Confirm Shipment
5 AutoInvoice 開票AutoInvoice AR 開票（帳務事件）AR invoice created (accounting event) AR → AutoInvoice → Run AutoInvoice
💡
Ship Confirm 是庫存扣減的關鍵時點。在此之前取消或修改出貨數量都是允許的。一旦 Ship Confirm 完成，要修改數量必須走「退貨→重新出貨」流程。確認出貨時，系統同步觸發 Oracle Logistics 的裝運紀錄和 Shipping Integration 通知（如貨運追蹤）。 Ship Confirm is the critical point for inventory decrement. Cancelling or modifying shipment quantities is permitted before this point. Once Ship Confirm is complete, modifying quantities requires a "Return → Re-ship" process. When confirming shipment, the system simultaneously triggers Oracle Logistics shipment records and Shipping Integration notifications (e.g., tracking updates).
⚠️
常見錯誤：Pick Wave 設計時把所有訂單合為一個大 Wave，導致部分訂單因缺貨而整個 Wave 卡住。建議 Wave 規則依「預計出貨日 + 承運商 + 倉庫區域」分組，讓問題訂單只影響同批次的小 Wave，不拖累全倉作業。 Common mistake: Designing Pick Waves that consolidate all orders into one large wave, causing the entire wave to stall when any order has a stockout. Recommend grouping Wave rules by "scheduled ship date + carrier + warehouse zone" so problem orders only affect a small wave, not the entire warehouse operation.

🚫 深入解析：Hold 管理與 Processing Constraints 🚫 Deep Dive: Hold Management & Processing Constraints

▼

Hold 用於暫停訂單的後續處理，可以套用在整張訂單（Order Level Hold）或特定訂單行（Line Level Hold）。Processing Constraints 則是欄位層級的保護規則，防止在不適當的時機修改關鍵欄位，兩者相輔相成構成訂單管控體系。 Holds pause order processing and can be applied at the entire order level (Order Level Hold) or to specific order lines (Line Level Hold). Processing Constraints are field-level protection rules that prevent modifications to critical fields at inappropriate times — together they form the order control framework.

Hold 類型Hold Type 套用層級Applied At MegaRetail 使用場景MegaRetail Use Case 解除方式Release Method
Credit Hold 訂單 / 客戶Order / Customer 客戶超出信用額度時自動套用Auto-applied when customer exceeds credit limit 財務主管手動放行Finance manager manual release
Shipping Hold 訂單行Order Line 等待客戶確認出貨地址時Awaiting customer address confirmation 客服人員確認後放行CS rep releases after confirmation
Price Hold 訂單行Order Line 單價異常低時（可能輸入錯誤）When unit price is unusually low (possible input error) 業務主管核准後放行Sales manager approves release
Export Compliance Hold 訂單Order 出口管制品項出口特定國家Export-controlled items to specific countries 法遵部門審核放行Compliance team review and release

Processing Constraints 範例：出貨後防改品項 Processing Constraints Example: Prevent Item Change After Shipment

MegaRetail 設定的 Processing Constraint：
• Entity：Order Line，Attribute：Ordered Item
• Condition：Fulfillment Set Status = Shipped 或 Closed
• Action：Prevent Update（禁止修改）+ 顯示錯誤訊息「此訂單行已出貨，不可修改品項」
這樣即使業務誤操作，系統也不會允許變更，確保出貨紀錄的完整性。 MegaRetail's Processing Constraint configuration:
• Entity: Order Line, Attribute: Ordered Item
• Condition: Fulfillment Set Status = Shipped or Closed
• Action: Prevent Update + display error message "This order line has been shipped and the item cannot be changed"
Even if a sales rep makes an accidental change, the system won't allow it, ensuring shipment record integrity.

Q：Hold 可以套用到特定訂單行，還是只能整張訂單？Q: Can Holds be applied to specific order lines, or only the entire order?▶
Hold 可以套用到訂單行層級（Line Level）。例如同一張 SO 中，第 1 行庫存充足可以正常出貨，但第 2 行需要等客戶確認規格，就可以只對第 2 行套 Shipping Hold。系統會讓第 1 行繼續推進 Orchestration，第 2 行則暫停在 Hold 步驟。放行時也只需放行第 2 行，不影響第 1 行已完成的出貨。 Holds can be applied at the Line Level. For example, on the same SO, Line 1 has sufficient stock and can ship normally, but Line 2 needs customer specification confirmation — you can apply a Shipping Hold to Line 2 only. The system lets Line 1 continue its Orchestration while Line 2 pauses at the Hold step. Releasing only requires releasing Line 2, without affecting Line 1's completed shipment.

❓ 常見問題解答

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

Q1：什麼時候用 Back-to-Back，什麼時候用 Drop Shipment，什麼時候用一般訂單？ Q1: When should I use Back-to-Back vs Drop Shipment vs regular orders? ▶

一般訂單（Standard）：當你有充足的自有庫存，可以從倉庫直接揀貨出貨。例如 Widget-A 有 1,000 件庫存，客戶訂 300 件，直接走標準流程最快。 Standard Orders: When you have sufficient own stock and can pick and ship directly from your warehouse. E.g., Widget-A has 1,000 units on hand, customer orders 300 — standard flow is fastest.

Back-to-Back：需要從供應商採購，採購品到你的倉庫後再出給客戶。適合進口品、客製品、或你不想長期庫存的品項。貨會實際通過你的倉庫，你可以做品質檢驗。 Back-to-Back: Must procure from a supplier, then receive at your warehouse before shipping to the customer. Good for imported items, custom items, or items you don't want to stock long-term. Goods physically pass through your warehouse so you can perform quality inspection.

Drop Shipment：供應商直接把貨寄給客戶，你的倉庫不見到實體貨。適合大型設備、超重物品、或供應商在客戶附近有倉庫可加速交期的情況。你仍然是銷售方（發票給客戶），供應商對你開發票，中間有兩個交易。 Drop Shipment: Supplier ships directly to your customer; your warehouse never sees the physical goods. Good for large equipment, heavy items, or when the supplier has a warehouse near the customer for faster delivery. You remain the seller (invoice to customer), supplier invoices you — there are two separate transactions in the middle.

Q2：Hold 可以只套用在特定訂單行，還是一定要整張訂單？ Q2: Can a Hold be applied to a specific order line vs the whole order? ▶
Hold 同時支援訂單層級（Order Level）和訂單行層級（Line Level）。設定 Hold Type 時，可以指定「Applies To」= Order 或 Line。Line Level Hold 讓你精確控制：同一張訂單中，有問題的行暫停，沒問題的行繼續推進出貨。例如 5 行訂單中第 3 行有信用疑慮，只需 Hold Line 3，其他 4 行照常出貨，不影響客戶整體收貨時間表。 Holds support both Order Level and Line Level. When configuring a Hold Type, you specify "Applies To" = Order or Line. Line Level Hold gives precise control: within the same order, problematic lines pause while others continue to shipment. For example, if Line 3 of a 5-line order has a credit concern, only Hold Line 3 — the other 4 lines ship normally, preserving the customer's overall delivery schedule.
Q3：供應計畫改變後，GOP 的承諾日期會自動更新嗎？客戶怎麼知道？ Q3: When supply plans change, do GOP promise dates auto-update? How does the customer know? ▶
GOP 承諾日期不會自動重新推送給客戶，但系統會透過 Jeopardy 機制提醒客服人員。當 ATP 重新計算發現當前承諾日期無法達成時，訂單的 Jeopardy Score 升高，系統發送警示給客服。客服人員需手動聯絡客戶協商新交期，或在訂單上點選「Re-Promise」讓系統提供新的 ATP 日期選項，確認後更新訂單的承諾日期。Oracle 本身不自動發 Email 給客戶通知交期變更，這部分通常需要客製化通知流程或整合 CRM 系統。 GOP promise dates are not automatically pushed to customers, but the Jeopardy mechanism alerts CS reps. When ATP recalculation finds the current promise date is unachievable, the order's Jeopardy Score rises and the system sends an alert to CS. CS reps must manually contact the customer to negotiate a new date, or click "Re-Promise" on the order to have the system offer new ATP date options, then update the order's promise date upon confirmation. Oracle does not automatically email customers about delivery date changes — this typically requires custom notification workflows or CRM integration.
Q4：Processing Constraints 如何防止出貨後誤改欄位？ Q4: How does Processing Constraints prevent accidental field changes after shipping? ▶
Processing Constraints 的工作原理：你定義一個規則，包含「實體（Entity）」（如 Order Line）、「屬性（Attribute）」（如 Ordered Quantity）、「條件（Condition）」（如 Line Status = Shipped）、「動作（Action）」（如 Prevent Update）。當使用者嘗試在滿足 Condition 的狀態下修改指定 Attribute，系統顯示自訂錯誤訊息並拒絕儲存。這個機制不依賴使用者的職能（Role），即使是系統管理員也無法繞過，除非去掉這條 Constraint。建議核心 Constraint（如出貨後不改品項、開票後不改數量）設為不可繞過，降低人為錯誤風險。 Processing Constraints work by defining a rule with "Entity" (e.g., Order Line), "Attribute" (e.g., Ordered Quantity), "Condition" (e.g., Line Status = Shipped), and "Action" (e.g., Prevent Update). When a user attempts to modify the specified Attribute while the Condition is met, the system displays a custom error message and rejects the save. This mechanism is not role-dependent — even system administrators cannot bypass it without removing the Constraint. Recommend making core Constraints (e.g., no item changes after shipping, no quantity changes after invoicing) non-bypassable to minimize human error risk.

模組 5：需求規劃 Module 5: Demand Planning

用統計方法預測未來需求，透過 S&OP 達成企業共識，驅動供應鏈上下游計劃

Use statistical forecasting to predict future demand, reach consensus through S&OP, and drive supply chain planning

Forecasting Profile MAPE S&OP CTO Causal Factors

為什麼需求規劃如此重要？

Why Does Demand Planning Matter?

想像 TechVision Electronics，一家生產 50 款 SKU 消費性電子產品的公司。每季末，業務部喊出 12,000 台的銷售目標，生產部卻說產能只有 10,000 台，採購部則已經依照去年同期的 8,000 台備了料。三個數字、三個部門、三套計劃——結果是過度庫存某些型號、熱門款式卻缺貨，最終錯失旺季商機，損失超過 NT$3,000 萬。

Picture TechVision Electronics, a consumer electronics company managing 50 SKUs. At every quarter-end, Sales shouts a target of 12,000 units, Manufacturing says capacity caps at 10,000, and Procurement has already ordered based on last year's 8,000-unit figure. Three numbers, three departments, three plans — the result is excess inventory on slow models, stockouts on hot items, and a missed peak season costing over $1M USD.

Oracle SCM Cloud 的需求規劃模組（Demand Planning）提供了解法：以 15 種以上統計演算法自動選出最佳預測方法（MAPE 最低者優先），將促銷活動、季節性波動、新品生命週期曲線全部納入預測模型；Configure-to-Order（CTO）預測更能將 "Pro X 手機" 的整體需求自動拆算成 128GB / 256GB / 512GB 的各自備料量。最終透過 S&OP 流程，讓業務、財務、供應鏈在同一個系統內達成共識計劃。

Oracle SCM Cloud's Demand Planning module provides the solution: over 15 statistical algorithms automatically select the best forecasting method (lowest MAPE wins), incorporating promotions, seasonality, and new-product lifecycle curves into the model. Configure-to-Order (CTO) forecasting automatically splits an aggregate "Pro X" phone forecast into individual demand for 128GB / 256GB / 512GB variants. Finally, the S&OP process brings Sales, Finance, and Supply Chain to consensus in a single system.

學完本模組，您將能：設定 Forecasting Profile、解讀 MAPE 並改善預測準確度、建立 Causal Factor 量化促銷影響、操作 CTO 規劃百分比、以及主持一場完整的 S&OP 共識會議。這些技能直接決定企業能否在對的時間、對的地點，備妥對的數量。

After completing this module, you will be able to: configure a Forecasting Profile, interpret MAPE and improve accuracy, create Causal Factors to quantify promotion impact, work with CTO Planning Percentages, and facilitate a complete S&OP consensus cycle. These skills directly determine whether your business has the right quantity, in the right place, at the right time.

🔑
核心價值：需求規劃是供應鏈的「起點」。預測錯 10%，可能導致採購多備 15%、生產多排 20%，整條供應鏈的成本浪費呈倍數放大。 Core Value: Demand Planning is the "starting point" of the supply chain. A 10% forecast error can cascade into 15% excess procurement and 20% over-scheduling in production — cost waste multiplies across the entire chain.

✨ 核心功能概覽 ✨ Key Feature Overview

▼
🧮

Forecasting ProfileForecasting Profile

15 種以上統計方法的配置容器。設定後系統自動為每個 SKU 選擇 MAPE 最低的方法。例：SKU-A01 系統選 Holt-Winters，SKU-B07 選 Croston（低頻需求）。 Container for 15+ statistical methods. After setup, the system auto-selects the lowest-MAPE method per SKU. Example: SKU-A01 uses Holt-Winters; SKU-B07 uses Croston (intermittent demand).

📉

MAPE 準確度量測MAPE Accuracy Measurement

Mean Absolute Percentage Error。Product A 預測 100，實際 85，MAPE = |100-85|/85 = 17.6%。消費電子業界標準：MAPE < 20% 為良好，< 10% 為優秀。 Mean Absolute Percentage Error. Product A forecast=100, actual=85: MAPE=|100-85|/85=17.6%. Consumer electronics benchmark: <20% is good, <10% is excellent.

📣

Causal Factors 因果因子Causal Factors

量化外部影響。促銷活動讓基準需求 500 件/週提升 40%，促銷期間 3 週預測 = 700 件/週。系統自動疊加在統計基準上。 Quantify external impact. A promotion lifts baseline demand of 500 units/week by 40% → 700 units/week for 3 weeks. System overlays this on the statistical baseline automatically.

🔧

CTO 規劃百分比CTO Planning Percentages

Configure-to-Order 預測：Pro X 手機預測 10,000 台，128GB 占 60% → 6,000 台，256GB 占 35% → 3,500 台，512GB 占 5% → 500 台。 Configure-to-Order: Pro X forecast 10,000 units. 128GB=60%→6,000; 256GB=35%→3,500; 512GB=5%→500 units automatically allocated.

🤝

S&OP 共識流程S&OP Consensus Process

業務提 12,000、供應說 10,000，S&OP 共識 11,000 + 供應改善計劃。所有版本在系統中可追溯、可比較。 Sales proposes 12,000; Supply says 10,000; S&OP consensus lands at 11,000 with supply improvement plan. All versions traceable and comparable in-system.

🔍

異常值偵測 Outlier DetectionOutlier Detection

COVID 期間 2020Q2 銷量暴跌至正常值的 30%。系統標記為異常值，排除後 MAPE 從 38% 降至 19%，預測品質倍增。 COVID Q2 2020 sales dropped to 30% of normal. System flags as outlier; after exclusion, MAPE drops from 38% to 19% — accuracy nearly doubles.

🧮 深入解析：Forecasting Profile 與 MAPE 🧮 Deep Dive: Forecasting Profile & MAPE

▼

什麼是 Forecasting Profile？What is a Forecasting Profile?

Forecasting Profile 是 Oracle Demand Planning 的核心配置物件。您在其中勾選允許系統嘗試的統計方法清單，設定回顧歷史期間（如 24 個月）、預測期間（如 12 個月）、最小歷史筆數等。執行預測時，系統對每個 SKU 分別試算所有啟用的方法，選出 MAPE 最低者作為最終預測。

A Forecasting Profile is the core configuration object in Oracle Demand Planning. You select which statistical methods the system may try, set the historical lookback period (e.g., 24 months), forecast horizon (e.g., 12 months), and minimum history count. When the forecast runs, the system tests all enabled methods per SKU and selects the one with the lowest MAPE as the final forecast.

Oracle 路徑： Supply Chain Planning → Demand Management → Configuration → Forecasting Profiles → Create

Oracle Path: Supply Chain Planning → Demand Management → Configuration → Forecasting Profiles → Create

MAPE 計算實例MAPE Calculation Example

💡
MAPE 公式： MAPE = (1/n) × Σ |Actual - Forecast| / Actual × 100%

Product A 三個月計算：
• 1月：預測 100，實際 85 → |100-85|/85 = 17.6%
• 2月：預測 120，實際 130 → |120-130|/130 = 7.7%
• 3月：預測 90，實際 95 → |90-95|/95 = 5.3%
MAPE = (17.6% + 7.7% + 5.3%) / 3 = 10.2% ✅ 優秀 MAPE Formula: MAPE = (1/n) × Σ |Actual - Forecast| / Actual × 100%

Product A Three-Month Calculation:
• Jan: Forecast=100, Actual=85 → |100-85|/85 = 17.6%
• Feb: Forecast=120, Actual=130 → |120-130|/130 = 7.7%
• Mar: Forecast=90, Actual=95 → |90-95|/95 = 5.3%
MAPE = (17.6% + 7.7% + 5.3%) / 3 = 10.2% ✅ Excellent

MAPE 業界基準MAPE Industry Benchmarks

MAPE 評估Rating 建議行動Recommended Action
< 10%優秀Excellent維持現有設定Maintain current setup
10% – 20%良好Good可嘗試加入 Causal FactorConsider adding Causal Factors
20% – 50%尚可Acceptable檢查異常值、換方法、加歷史資料Check outliers, change method, add history
> 50%需改善Needs Work考慮人工覆蓋、改用 Lifecycle、找根因Consider manual override, Lifecycle method, find root cause
Q：我需要多少歷史資料才能做統計預測？ Q: How much historical data do I need for statistical forecasting? ▶

最低要求依方法而異：Moving Average 需 3 個月，Simple Exponential Smoothing 需 6 個月，Holt's Double 需 12 個月，Winters（含季節）需至少 24 個月（至少覆蓋 2 個完整季節週期）。Oracle 建議：若歷史資料不足，先用 Lifecycle Planning 曲線，以同類商品的歷史資料作為參考品（Reference Product）。TechVision 新品 Pro X 就是利用上一代 Pro 9 的銷售曲線作為基準。

Minimum requirements vary by method: Moving Average needs 3 months, Simple Exponential Smoothing 6 months, Holt's Double 12 months, and Winters (seasonal) needs at least 24 months (covering at least 2 full seasonal cycles). Oracle recommendation: if history is insufficient, use Lifecycle Planning with a Reference Product from a similar item. TechVision's new Pro X uses the previous-generation Pro 9's sales curve as the reference baseline.

Q：MAPE 超過 50% 時應該怎麼辦？ Q: What should I do when MAPE is over 50%? ▶

MAPE > 50% 通常有三個根因：(1) 資料中含有異常值（需啟用 Outlier Correction）；(2) 歷史資料過短（不足方法所需最低月數）；(3) 選錯預測方法（例如對季節性商品用 Moving Average）。處理步驟：① 先執行 Outlier Detection Report 確認有無異常點 → ② 在 Forecasting Profile 中啟用「Automatically Correct Outliers」 → ③ 若 MAPE 仍高，嘗試 Lifecycle 或人工覆蓋（Manual Override）。注意：高 MAPE 品項可能根本不適合統計預測，業務員的市場判斷可能更可靠。

MAPE > 50% usually has three root causes: (1) outliers in the data (enable Outlier Correction); (2) insufficient historical data (shorter than the method's minimum); (3) wrong method selected (e.g., using Moving Average on a seasonal product). Steps: ① Run Outlier Detection Report to identify anomalies → ② Enable "Automatically Correct Outliers" in Forecasting Profile → ③ If MAPE remains high, try Lifecycle method or Manual Override. Note: high-MAPE items may simply not be suitable for statistical forecasting — a salesperson's market judgment may be more reliable.

⚠️
常見錯誤：在 Forecasting Profile 中勾選「所有方法」以為系統會選最好的。事實上，方法過多會大幅增加運算時間，且 Croston 法用在穩定高頻需求品項反而會降低準確度。建議：按品項特性分組，建立 2-3 個不同的 Forecasting Profile（穩定品、季節品、間歇品各一）。 Common Mistake: Enabling "all methods" in the Forecasting Profile assuming the system will always pick the best. In reality, too many methods dramatically increase compute time, and Croston's method applied to stable high-volume items actually degrades accuracy. Best practice: group items by characteristic and create 2-3 separate Forecasting Profiles (stable, seasonal, intermittent).

📣 深入解析：Causal Factors 因果因子 📣 Deep Dive: Causal Factors

▼

Causal Factors 讓您將外部事件（促銷、節慶、漲價）的影響量化並嵌入預測模型。不同於 Event Model 描述「發生了什麼事」，Causal Factor 描述「這個事件讓需求增加/減少了幾%」。Oracle 支援 Multiplicative 和 Additive 兩種疊加模式。

Causal Factors allow you to quantify the impact of external events (promotions, holidays, price changes) and embed them in the forecast model. Unlike Event Models which describe "what happened," Causal Factors describe "by how much this event increased/decreased demand." Oracle supports both Multiplicative and Additive overlay modes.

💡
促銷效果計算範例：
• 商品：Gaming Headset SKU-H07
• 基準需求（統計預測）：500 件/週
• 促銷活動：雙十一折扣，Causal Factor = 1.4（提升 40%）
• 促銷期間：3 週（11/7 – 11/28）
• 促銷期預測 = 500 × 1.4 = 700 件/週
• 總促銷期需求 = 700 × 3 = 2,100 件
• 恢復正常後 11月第5週 = 500 件/週 Promotion Effect Calculation:
• Item: Gaming Headset SKU-H07
• Baseline demand (statistical forecast): 500 units/week
• Promotion: Double-11 discount, Causal Factor = 1.4 (40% lift)
• Promotion period: 3 weeks (11/7 – 11/28)
• Forecast during promotion = 500 × 1.4 = 700 units/week
• Total promotion period demand = 700 × 3 = 2,100 units
• Return to normal week 5 = 500 units/week

Causal Factor 設定步驟Causal Factor Setup Steps

Oracle 路徑： Demand Management → Configuration → Causal Factors → Create

Oracle Path: Demand Management → Configuration → Causal Factors → Create

欄位Field 範例值Example Value 說明Description
Causal Factor Name Double11_Promo_2024 唯一識別名稱Unique identifier
Type Multiplicative 乘數型（最常用）Multiplier type (most common)
Factor Value 1.4 需求提升 40%40% demand lift
Start Date 2024-11-07 促銷開始日Promotion start date
End Date 2024-11-28 促銷結束日Promotion end date
Applicable Items Category: Gaming Audio 可套用至品類、品項群組或單品Apply to category, item group, or single item
Q：Causal Factor 和 Event Model 有什麼差別？ Q: What is the difference between Causal Factor and Event Model? ▶

Event Model 是「記錄型」工具，描述歷史上發生了什麼事（COVID、颱風停工）並用於解釋歷史資料異常；Causal Factor 是「預測型」工具，告訴系統未來某段期間需求會因某因素增減多少。實務上兩者常搭配使用：先用 Event Model 標記歷史異常值（排除其對統計模型的汙染），再用 Causal Factor 把已知的未來促銷疊加到預測上。

Event Models are "recording" tools that describe what happened historically (COVID, typhoon shutdowns) to explain historical data anomalies. Causal Factors are "forecasting" tools that tell the system how much demand will increase or decrease due to a known future factor. In practice, both are often used together: use Event Models to flag historical outliers (preventing contamination of the statistical model), then use Causal Factors to overlay known future promotions onto the forecast.

⚠️
常見錯誤：把歷史促銷的提升效果永久留在 Causal Factor 而不設結束日期，導致系統在未來無促銷期間仍以 1.4 倍計算需求，造成嚴重過度備料。一定要為每個 Causal Factor 設定明確的 Start Date 和 End Date。 Common Mistake: Leaving a historical promotion's Causal Factor active without an end date, causing the system to continue applying the 1.4x multiplier during non-promotion periods and resulting in severe overstock. Always set explicit Start Date and End Date for every Causal Factor.

🔍 深入解析：異常值偵測 Outlier Detection 🔍 Deep Dive: Outlier Detection

▼

異常值是指因非常規因素造成的需求極端值，例如突發性大單、工廠停工、全球疫情。如果讓這些數據汙染統計模型，預測方法會誤學成「需求本來就是這樣」，導致未來預測偏差。Oracle 提供三種異常值處理機制：(1) 系統自動偵測並修正；(2) 手動標記排除；(3) 以 Event Model 說明原因。

Outliers are extreme demand values caused by non-recurring factors such as one-time large orders, factory shutdowns, or global pandemics. If these contaminate the statistical model, the algorithm "learns" that this is normal demand and produces biased future forecasts. Oracle provides three outlier handling mechanisms: (1) automatic detection and correction; (2) manual flagging and exclusion; (3) Event Model documentation of the cause.

💡
COVID 異常值案例：
• 商品：Gaming Headset SKU-H07
• 2020 Q2 正常月均銷量：850 件
• 2020 Q2 實際銷量（COVID 停貨）：255 件（僅 30% 正常值）
• 含 COVID 資料的 MAPE：38%（系統誤以為旺季需求本就很低）
• 排除 COVID 資料後 MAPE：19%（系統重新學到正確季節模式）
• 結論：排除異常值讓預測準確度提升 50% COVID Outlier Case:
• Item: Gaming Headset SKU-H07
• Normal monthly average 2020 Q2: 850 units
• Actual 2020 Q2 (COVID stockout): 255 units (only 30% of normal)
• MAPE with COVID data included: 38% (system incorrectly learned low peak demand)
• MAPE after excluding COVID data: 19% (system relearns correct seasonal pattern)
• Conclusion: Excluding the outlier improves forecast accuracy by 50%
方法Method 觸發條件Trigger Condition Oracle 功能Oracle Feature
自動偵測Auto-detect 超過平均值 ± N 個標準差Beyond mean ± N standard deviations Outlier Correction = Automatic
手動標記Manual Flag 業務知識判斷Business knowledge judgment Manage History → Edit → Mark as Outlier
Event ModelEvent Model 可重複發生的已知事件Known recurring event Demand Management → Event Models
⚠️
常見錯誤：以為排除越多異常值越好。若把促銷旺季銷售高峰也標記為異常值，系統就永遠無法學到促銷帶來的真實需求提升，反而讓備貨不足。只排除「不會再發生」的異常，正常促銷/旺季資料應保留並搭配 Causal Factor 說明。 Common Mistake: Assuming that excluding more outliers is always better. If you flag promotion peak-season sales as outliers, the system can never learn the real demand lift from promotions, leading to chronic understocking. Only exclude events that "will not happen again." Normal promotion/peak-season data should be retained and explained via Causal Factors.

🔧 深入解析：CTO 配置到訂單預測 🔧 Deep Dive: Configure-to-Order (CTO) Forecasting

▼

Configure-to-Order（CTO）場景中，客戶下單時才選擇規格（記憶體大小、顏色、處理器）。在 Oracle Demand Planning 中，您對母品項（Model Item）做整體預測，再設定 Planning Percentages 讓系統自動拆算各選項（Option）的需求量，驅動正確的組件備料。

In Configure-to-Order (CTO) scenarios, customers choose configurations (memory size, color, processor) at the time of order. In Oracle Demand Planning, you forecast at the Model Item level, then set Planning Percentages so the system automatically allocates demand to each Option, driving the correct component procurement.

💡
Pro X 手機 CTO 計算範例：

母品項預測：Pro X Smartphone Model = 10,000 台/月

Planning Percentages 設定：
• Pro X 128GB（Option 1）：60% → 6,000 台
• Pro X 256GB（Option 2）：35% → 3,500 台
• Pro X 512GB（Option 3）：5% → 500 台

衍生組件需求：
• Samsung 128GB Memory Chip：6,000 顆
• Samsung 256GB Memory Chip：3,500 顆
• Samsung 512GB Memory Chip：500 顆 Pro X Smartphone CTO Calculation:

Model Item Forecast: Pro X Smartphone = 10,000 units/month

Planning Percentages:
• Pro X 128GB (Option 1): 60% → 6,000 units
• Pro X 256GB (Option 2): 35% → 3,500 units
• Pro X 512GB (Option 3): 5% → 500 units

Derived Component Demand:
• Samsung 128GB Memory Chip: 6,000 pcs
• Samsung 256GB Memory Chip: 3,500 pcs
• Samsung 512GB Memory Chip: 500 pcs

Oracle 路徑： Supply Chain Planning → Demand Management → Items → Select Model Item → Planning Percentages Tab

Oracle Path: Supply Chain Planning → Demand Management → Items → Select Model Item → Planning Percentages Tab

Q：Planning Percentages 加總必須等於 100% 嗎？ Q: Do Planning Percentages need to sum to 100%? ▶

是的，每個 Option Class（選項類別）內的 Planning Percentages 必須加總為 100%，否則系統在發布時會提示驗證錯誤。若某個選項機率極低但不為零（如 512GB 僅 5%），仍須包含在內確保加總正確。此外，Planning Percentages 可定期更新（建議每季複查），若市場趨勢轉移（如 256GB 逐漸主流），應及時調整百分比以反映最新銷售組合。

Yes, Planning Percentages within each Option Class must sum to 100%, otherwise the system issues a validation error at publish time. Even if a low-probability option exists (e.g., 512GB at only 5%), it must be included to ensure the total is correct. Planning Percentages should be reviewed periodically (quarterly is recommended); if market trends shift (e.g., 256GB becomes mainstream), adjust percentages to reflect the current sales mix.

⚠️
常見錯誤：Planning Percentages 設定後就不再更新。消費電子市場轉移很快——若去年 128GB 賣 60% 但今年因定價調整已變成 40%，舊百分比會造成 128GB 組件過多備料、256GB 嚴重短缺。建議設定每季自動複查提醒並根據近 3 個月實際 Mix 更新。 Common Mistake: Setting Planning Percentages once and never updating them. Consumer electronics markets shift quickly — if 128GB was 60% last year but price changes dropped it to 40% this year, stale percentages cause severe 128GB component overstock and 256GB shortages. Set a quarterly review reminder and update based on the last 3 months' actual sales mix.

🤝 深入解析：S&OP 銷售與營運規劃 🤝 Deep Dive: Sales & Operations Planning (S&OP)

▼

S&OP（銷售與營運規劃）是跨部門共識流程，目標是讓業務目標、供應能力、財務計劃在同一個數字上對齊。Oracle SCM Cloud 的 S&OP 功能讓各部門在系統中提交自己的版本，協調人員可在同一畫面比較差異、標記衝突、記錄共識決定並發布最終計劃。

S&OP is a cross-functional consensus process that aligns sales targets, supply capability, and financial plans on a single number. Oracle SCM Cloud's S&OP functionality allows each department to submit its version in the system; coordinators can compare gaps, flag conflicts, document consensus decisions, and publish the final plan — all in one screen.

💡
TechVision S&OP 共識案例：

• 統計預測（基準）：10,500 台
• 業務提案（Sales Forecast）：12,000 台（+14%，含新客戶管道）
• 供應能力評估：10,000 台（瓶頸：一台 SMT 機器待維修）
• 財務計劃：11,500 台（達成 Q4 Revenue Target 所需）

共識決定：11,000 台
行動計劃：
1. 生產主管承諾 11/15 前完成 SMT 維修，提升產能至 11,000
2. 業務調降新客戶管道預期（由 2,000 → 1,000）
3. 財務接受 11,000 作為 Q4 目標，下月 S&OP 複查 TechVision S&OP Consensus Case:

• Statistical Forecast (Baseline): 10,500 units
• Sales Proposal: 12,000 units (+14%, includes new pipeline accounts)
• Supply Capability: 10,000 units (bottleneck: one SMT machine awaiting repair)
• Financial Plan: 11,500 units (needed to hit Q4 Revenue Target)

Consensus Decision: 11,000 units
Action Plan:
1. Production Manager commits to completing SMT repair by 11/15, raising capacity to 11,000
2. Sales reduces new-account pipeline expectation (2,000 → 1,000 units)
3. Finance accepts 11,000 as Q4 target; review at next month's S&OP

S&OP 五步驟流程S&OP Five-Step Process
