共識計劃驅動供應鏈Consensus plan drives supply chain
Q：Demand Plan 和 Supply Plan 有什麼差別？ Q: What is the difference between Demand Plan and Supply Plan? ▶

Demand Plan 回答「客戶想買多少」，是從市場角度出發，以統計預測 + 業務判斷構成，不受供應限制約束；Supply Plan 回答「我們能生產/備料多少」，考慮產能上限、在製品、採購前置時間、安全庫存等約束條件。S&OP 的核心任務就是縮小兩者的 Gap：當 Demand Plan > Supply Plan，需要擴產或調降業務預期；當 Supply Plan > Demand Plan，需要啟動促銷或評估庫存風險。Oracle 中兩者位在不同模組：Demand Plan 在 Demand Management；Supply Plan 在 Supply Planning。

Demand Plan answers "how much do customers want to buy" — it takes a market-demand perspective built from statistical forecasts plus business judgment, unconstrained by supply. Supply Plan answers "how much can we produce/procure" — it factors in capacity limits, work-in-process, procurement lead times, and safety stock constraints. The core S&OP mission is to close the gap: when Demand > Supply, you either expand capacity or reduce sales expectations; when Supply > Demand, you launch promotions or evaluate inventory risk. In Oracle, they live in separate modules: Demand Plan in Demand Management; Supply Plan in Supply Planning.

Q：不同產品系列可以有不同的預測粒度嗎？ Q: Can I have different forecast granularities for different product families? ▶

可以。Oracle Demand Planning 支援多層次預測粒度，透過 Planning Hierarchy 設定。例如：旗艦手機系列（高價值、少 SKU）可設定 SKU × Location × Week 粒度做精細預測；配件系列（低單價、多 SKU）可設定 Product Family × Region × Month 粒度做聚合預測，再用 Disaggregation Rules 拆分到 SKU 層級。此外，可為不同產品系列建立不同的 Demand Plan，並在 S&OP 中合併比較。

Yes. Oracle Demand Planning supports multi-level forecast granularity through Planning Hierarchy configuration. Example: flagship phone series (high value, few SKUs) can use SKU × Location × Week granularity for fine-grained forecasting; accessories (low unit price, many SKUs) can use Product Family × Region × Month aggregation, then apply Disaggregation Rules to break down to SKU level. You can also create separate Demand Plans per product family and consolidate them in S&OP for comparison.

⚠️
常見錯誤：S&OP 會議中口頭達成共識，但沒有更新系統中的計劃數字。一個月後各部門仍依各自版本執行，造成採購超買、生產錯排。正確做法：S&OP 會議結束後 24 小時內，協調人員必須在 Oracle 中更新 Consensus Forecast 並發布，通知所有下游計劃系統更新。 Common Mistake: Reaching verbal consensus in the S&OP meeting but failing to update the system numbers. A month later, each department still executes based on its own version, causing procurement overbuying and production mis-scheduling. Correct practice: within 24 hours of the S&OP meeting, the coordinator must update the Consensus Forecast in Oracle and publish it, triggering all downstream planning systems to refresh.

📋 綜合案例：TechVision Q4 旺季需求規劃 📋 Case Study: TechVision Q4 Peak Season Demand Planning

▼

TechVision Electronics 正在準備 Q4 旺季（10-12月）的需求計劃，需涵蓋旗艦手機 Pro X、耳機系列、配件三大類共 50 SKU。以下是完整的端對端規劃流程。

TechVision Electronics is preparing the Q4 peak-season demand plan (Oct–Dec), covering flagship phone Pro X, headphone series, and accessories — 50 SKUs in total. The following is the complete end-to-end planning workflow.

步驟 1：資料準備與異常值處理Step 1: Data Preparation & Outlier Handling

匯入 2022-2024 年 36 個月銷售歷史。執行 Outlier Detection Report 後發現：2020 Q2（COVID）數據已在前期清理；但 2023 年 3 月有一筆一次性企業大單 3,500 台（正常月均 800 台），系統標記為異常。協調人員確認此大單不會重複，手動標記為 Outlier 並排除。

Import 36 months of sales history (2022–2024). After running the Outlier Detection Report: 2020 Q2 (COVID) data was already cleaned in a prior cycle. However, March 2023 shows a one-time enterprise bulk order of 3,500 units (normal monthly average: 800 units), flagged by the system. The coordinator confirms the order is non-recurring and manually marks it as an Outlier for exclusion.

AC Adapters (B2B) Intermittent_Profile Croston's Method 22.3%

步驟 3：Causal Factor 疊加雙十一促銷Step 3: Overlay Double-11 Promotion Causal Factor

建立 Causal Factor「Double11_2024」，Multiplicative = 1.4，適用品類：Gaming Headset + USB-C Cables，日期：11/7-11/28。疊加後耳機系列 11 月預測從 2,200 台提升至 3,080 台。

Create Causal Factor "Double11_2024", Multiplicative=1.4, applicable to: Gaming Headset + USB-C Cables, dates: 11/7–11/28. After overlay, Headset November forecast rises from 2,200 to 3,080 units.

512GB5%400700550

步驟 5：S&OP 共識與計劃發布Step 5: S&OP Consensus & Plan Publish

S&OP 會議中：業務希望 Pro X 11 月達到 16,000 台（新電商管道）；供應說 SMT 瓶頸限制 14,500 台；共識：14,000 台（與統計預測一致），業務承諾電商管道訂單若超出將優先履行 256GB。計劃發布後，Supply Planning 自動接收需求驅動 MRP。

In the S&OP meeting: Sales wants Pro X November at 16,000 (new e-commerce channel); Supply says SMT bottleneck limits to 14,500; consensus: 14,000 units (aligns with statistical forecast). Sales commits that if e-commerce orders exceed plan, 256GB fulfillment gets priority. After plan publish, Supply Planning automatically receives demand to drive MRP.

✅
Forecast Simulation 應用：某大型零售商要求下月備貨 20,000 台（正常兩倍）。規劃師使用 Forecast Simulation 功能建立「What-If 情境」模擬此需求衝擊，確認供應缺口為 6,000 台，並提前啟動緊急採購評估——而不更動已發布的官方計劃，避免整體供應鏈誤動。 Forecast Simulation Application: A major retailer requests 20,000 units next month (double normal). The planner uses Forecast Simulation to create a "What-If Scenario" modeling this demand surge, identifies a supply gap of 6,000 units, and initiates an emergency procurement assessment — without modifying the published official plan, preventing unnecessary supply chain disruption.

❓ 常見問題 FAQ ❓ Frequently Asked Questions

▼
Q1：統計預測需要多少歷史資料？各方法的最低要求？ Q1: How much historical data is needed? What are the minimums per method? ▶

最低要求：Moving Average 3 個月；Simple Exponential Smoothing 6 個月；Holt's Double Exponential 12 個月；Winters（季節型）24 個月。最佳實踐是使用 36 個月以上，讓系統能辨識 3 個完整季節週期。資料不足時：(1) 使用參考品（Reference Product）借用相似商品的歷史曲線；(2) 手動輸入市場研究資料作為初始歷史；(3) 先用 Moving Average 等短期方法，隨資料累積再切換至 Winters。

Minimums: Moving Average 3 months; Simple Exponential Smoothing 6 months; Holt's Double Exponential 12 months; Winters (seasonal) 24 months. Best practice is 36+ months so the system can identify 3 complete seasonal cycles. When data is insufficient: (1) use a Reference Product to borrow a similar item's historical curve; (2) manually enter market research data as initial history; (3) start with shorter-horizon methods like Moving Average and switch to Winters as data accumulates.

Q2：MAPE 超過 50% 時應該怎麼辦？有標準的除錯步驟嗎？ Q2: What should I do when MAPE is over 50%? Is there a standard debugging process? ▶

建議依序執行以下除錯步驟：
① 執行 Outlier Detection Report → 確認是否有極端值汙染資料（最常見原因）
② 啟用「Automatically Correct Outliers」或手動標記異常點後重新執行預測
③ 確認歷史資料月數是否達到該方法最低要求（如 Winters 需 24 個月）
④ 在 Forecasting Profile 中嘗試不同的方法組合（如改用 Moving Average）
⑤ 若以上均無改善，考慮：(a) 設定 Manual Override，以業務員判斷取代統計；(b) 改用 Lifecycle Planning（適合新品或不規律商品）；(c) 評估此 SKU 是否應降為 MTO（接單後生產），不做預測備料
注意：MAPE > 50% 有時是「商品本質」問題（如非常不規律的 B2B 大單），統計方法無法解決，此時業務員的市場情報比算法更有價值。

Follow these debugging steps in order:
① Run Outlier Detection Report → check for extreme value data contamination (most common cause)
② Enable "Automatically Correct Outliers" or manually flag anomalies and re-run forecast
③ Verify that historical data months meet the method's minimum requirement (e.g., Winters needs 24 months)
④ Try different method combinations in the Forecasting Profile (e.g., switch to Moving Average)
⑤ If no improvement: (a) apply Manual Override using salesperson judgment; (b) switch to Lifecycle Planning (suitable for new or irregular items); (c) evaluate whether this SKU should be MTO (make-to-order) with no forecast-based inventory
Note: MAPE > 50% sometimes reflects the product's inherent nature (e.g., highly irregular B2B bulk orders) that statistical methods cannot resolve. In these cases, sales intelligence is more valuable than algorithms.

Q3：不同產品系列可以有不同的預測粒度嗎？該怎麼設定？ Q3: Can different product families have different forecast granularities? How do I configure that? ▶

可以。在 Oracle Demand Management 中，透過 Planning Hierarchy 設定不同層級的預測粒度。常用方法：建立多個 Demand Plan，分別套用不同 Planning Hierarchy；或在同一 Demand Plan 中，為不同品項群組設定不同的預測層級，再用 Aggregation/Disaggregation 規則轉換。

實務案例：TechVision 旗艦手機（Pro X，5 SKU）：SKU × 地區 × 週 粒度（精細）；配件（USB-C Cable，30+ SKU）：Product Category × 全國 × 月 粒度（聚合）→ 再自動拆分到 SKU。此設計兼顧預測精度（旗艦）與系統效能（配件）。

Yes. In Oracle Demand Management, use Planning Hierarchy configuration to set different granularity per product group. Common approach: create multiple Demand Plans each with a different Planning Hierarchy, or within a single Demand Plan set different forecast levels per item group and use Aggregation/Disaggregation rules to convert between levels.

Practical example: TechVision flagship phones (Pro X, 5 SKUs): SKU × Region × Week granularity (fine-grained); accessories (USB-C Cable, 30+ SKUs): Product Category × National × Month (aggregated) → auto-disaggregated to SKU level. This design balances forecast precision (flagship) with system performance (accessories).

Q4：Demand Plan 和 Supply Plan 的根本差別是什麼？S&OP 如何連接兩者？ Q4: What is the fundamental difference between Demand Plan and Supply Plan? How does S&OP connect them? ▶

Demand Plan（需求計劃）：從市場視角出發，回答「客戶要買多少」，無約束（Unconstrained），是對未來需求的最佳估計，不考慮我能不能滿足。

Supply Plan（供應計劃）：從供應視角出發，回答「我能提供多少」，有約束（Constrained），考慮產能上限、前置時間、庫存水位、採購限制。

S&OP 的橋接角色：S&OP 是讓兩個計劃「對齊」的流程機制。當 Demand > Supply（供不應求）：執行緊急採購、外包、加班、或調降優先順序較低的客戶；當 Supply > Demand（供大於求）：啟動促銷、增加備貨、或評估未來庫存跌價風險。Oracle 中：Demand Plan 在 Demand Management 模組；Supply Plan 在 Supply Planning 模組；S&OP 流程在 Sales and Operations Planning 模組（三者整合運作）。

Demand Plan: Market-facing perspective, answers "how much do customers want to buy," Unconstrained — the best estimate of future demand without consideration of whether it can be fulfilled.

Supply Plan: Supply-facing perspective, answers "how much can we provide," Constrained — accounts for capacity limits, lead times, inventory levels, and procurement constraints.

S&OP as the bridge: S&OP is the process mechanism that aligns the two plans. When Demand > Supply: execute emergency procurement, outsourcing, overtime, or reprioritize lower-priority customers. When Supply > Demand: launch promotions, build inventory buffers, or assess future inventory write-down risk. In Oracle: Demand Plan lives in Demand Management; Supply Plan in Supply Planning; S&OP process in the Sales and Operations Planning module (all three integrate).

模組 6：供應規劃 Module 6: Supply Planning

根據需求和庫存計算最優補貨建議，管理供應例外，讓計劃員把時間花在真正需要決策的地方 Calculate optimal replenishment from demand and inventory, manage exceptions, and focus planners on decisions that truly matter

🔑
真實情境：醫療器材廠的供應規劃挑戰Real Scenario: Supply Planning Challenges at a Medical Device Manufacturer

MedTech Taiwan 是一家生產血糖監測儀的醫療器材公司，每週需要協調來自 12 家供應商的 340 種零件，並在台北、新竹兩座工廠之間調配庫存。過去，計劃員 James 每天花 6 小時手動比對 Excel 表格——哪些零件不夠？哪張工單會延誤？哪個供應商交期有問題？等他發現 Component A（感測晶片）庫存不足時，成品出貨已延誤 3 週，客戶投訴蜂擁而至。 MedTech Taiwan manufactures blood glucose monitors and must coordinate 340 components from 12 suppliers across two factories in Taipei and Hsinchu. Previously, planner James spent 6 hours daily reconciling Excel spreadsheets — which parts are short? Which work orders will be late? Which supplier has delivery issues? By the time he discovered Component A (sensor chips) was understocked, finished goods shipments were already 3 weeks late, and customer complaints flooded in.

導入 Oracle Supply Planning 後，James 每週一上午執行一次計劃，系統在 45 分鐘內完成全廠計算，自動生成 230 張補貨建議（採購、工單、轉撥），並標記 18 個需要人工處理的例外。James 不再需要找問題，系統直接告訴他：「銷售訂單 SO-5001 的 100 台設備，因為 PO-456（感測晶片）預計延誤 4 天到貨，工單 WO-123 將無法如期開工，建議緊急向備用供應商下單 200 片。」 After implementing Oracle Supply Planning, James runs the plan every Monday morning. The system completes the entire factory-wide calculation in 45 minutes, auto-generates 230 replenishment suggestions (purchase orders, work orders, transfers), and flags 18 exceptions requiring human attention. James no longer hunts for problems — the system tells him directly: "Sales Order SO-5001's 100 devices are at risk because PO-456 (sensor chips) is expected 4 days late, Work Order WO-123 cannot start on time. Recommend urgent order of 200 units from backup supplier."

更重要的是，當一家主力供應商突然宣佈漲價 15%，James 只需建立一個「模擬情境」，在 10 分鐘內就能看到：若改從備用供應商採購，成本增加多少？交期影響多大？哪些訂單有風險？這個功能讓 MedTech 在供應鏈動盪時期仍能做出有依據的採購決策，節省了數十萬的緊急採購溢價。本模組將帶你完整了解這套規劃邏輯。 More importantly, when a key supplier suddenly announced a 15% price increase, James simply created a simulation scenario and within 10 minutes could see: if switching to the backup supplier, how much does cost increase? What's the lead time impact? Which orders are at risk? This capability allowed MedTech to make evidence-based procurement decisions during supply chain disruptions, saving hundreds of thousands in emergency procurement premiums. This module walks you through the complete planning logic.

⭐ 核心功能一覽 ⭐ Key Features Overview

▼
📋

採購規則與指派集Sourcing Rules & Assignment Sets

定義每個品項「從哪裡取得」的邏輯。例：感測晶片 70% 向供應商 A 採購、30% 向供應商 B 採購，Hsinchu 工廠庫存不足時自動從 Taipei 工廠調撥。Defines "where to source" logic per item. Example: Sensor chips sourced 70% from Supplier A, 30% from Supplier B; if Hsinchu factory stock is low, auto-transfer from Taipei factory.

🚨

例外管理Exception Management

系統自動標記需要關注的情況。例：本週有 3 張銷售訂單短缺，2 張採購單預計逾期，1 個工作中心本週產能超載 140%。計劃員只處理這 6 個問題，不需掃描全部計劃。System auto-flags situations requiring attention. Example: 3 sales orders short this week, 2 POs expected late, 1 work center overloaded at 140% this week. Planners address only these 6 issues, not the entire plan.

🔗

需求追溯（Pegging）Demand Pegging

追蹤「為什麼短缺」的根本原因。例：SO-5001 → WO-123 → Component A → PO-456 延誤。一眼看清整條供應鏈，不用手動追查。Traces the root cause of shortages. Example: SO-5001 → WO-123 → Component A → PO-456 delayed. See the entire supply chain at a glance without manual investigation.

🏭

生產就緒（RTB）Ready to Build (RTB)

在工單開工前確認所有物料是否齊備。例：WO-234 預計週一開工，系統在週五自動檢查 8 項原材料，發現 2 項未到位，提早通知計劃員處理。Confirms all materials are available before work order start. Example: WO-234 scheduled for Monday, system checks 8 materials on Friday, finds 2 not yet received, alerts planner in advance.

🧮

安全庫存計算Safety Stock Calculation

系統根據需求波動和前置時間自動計算保險庫存。例：Component A 週需求 1000 件，前置時間 2 週，需求標準差 150 → 安全庫存 = 350 件（統計公式計算）。System auto-calculates safety stock from demand variability and lead time. Example: Component A weekly demand 1,000 units, lead time 2 weeks, σ=150 → safety stock = 350 units (statistical formula).

🔬

模擬情境分析Simulation Set Analysis

在不影響正式計劃的前提下進行假設分析。例：「如果供應商 X 延誤 2 週，哪些訂單受影響？改用備用供應商成本增加多少？」10 分鐘內得到答案。Perform what-if analysis without affecting the live plan. Example: "If Supplier X delays 2 weeks, which orders are impacted? How much extra cost from switching to backup?" Answer in 10 minutes.

🗂️ 採購規則 vs 指派集：層級與覆蓋邏輯 🗂️ Sourcing Rules vs Assignment Sets: Hierarchy & Override Logic

▼

採購規則（Sourcing Rule）定義「如何取得物料」的方法，包含來源類型（Make/Buy/Transfer）、供應商/工廠、分配比例和前置時間。指派集（Assignment Set）則決定「哪個品項、哪個組織」套用哪條採購規則。兩者是主從關係：指派集引用採購規則，並透過優先順序決定在多重指派時哪條規則生效。 Sourcing Rules define "how to obtain materials" — source type (Make/Buy/Transfer), supplier/factory, allocation percentage, and lead time. Assignment Sets determine "which item at which organization" uses which sourcing rule. They have a master-detail relationship: assignment sets reference sourcing rules, and priority determines which rule applies when multiple assignments exist.

具體範例：感測晶片的採購層級Concrete Example: Sensor Chip Sourcing Hierarchy

層級Level 指派對象Assignment Target 採購規則Sourcing Rule 優先序Rank 說明Notes
Item-Org 感測晶片 @ 台北工廠Sensor Chip @ Taipei SR-CHIP-TAIPEI 1 最高優先，台北工廠專屬規則Highest priority, Taipei-specific rule
Category-Org 電子零件 @ 台北工廠Electronics @ Taipei SR-ELEC-TAIPEI 2 品類層級，覆蓋所有電子零件Category level, covers all electronics
Global 所有品項（預設）All Items (Default) SR-DEFAULT-BUY 3 兜底規則，未匹配時使用Fallback rule for unmatched items

SR-CHIP-TAIPEI 的內容：Buy 70% 從 Supplier-A（前置 14 天）+ Buy 30% 從 Supplier-B（前置 21 天）。當台北工廠計劃需要 1,000 片感測晶片時，系統自動建議：PR-001 向 Supplier-A 700 片、PR-002 向 Supplier-B 300 片。 SR-CHIP-TAIPEI content: Buy 70% from Supplier-A (14-day lead time) + Buy 30% from Supplier-B (21-day lead time). When Taipei factory needs 1,000 sensor chips, system auto-suggests: PR-001 to Supplier-A for 700 units, PR-002 to Supplier-B for 300 units.

如何在 Oracle 中建立採購規則？How to create Sourcing Rules in Oracle?▶
導航路徑：Supply Chain Planning → Supply Planning → Manage Sourcing Rules。點 Create，填入規則名稱，在 Sourcing Lines 頁籤新增來源（選擇 Buy/Make/Transfer），設定 Supplier/Organization、Allocation Percentage（合計需等於 100%）及 Lead Time Days。儲存後至 Manage Assignment Sets 建立指派，選取採購規則並指定 Item/Category/Global 層級。 Navigation: Supply Chain Planning → Supply Planning → Manage Sourcing Rules. Click Create, enter rule name, add sourcing lines on the Sourcing Lines tab (select Buy/Make/Transfer), set Supplier/Organization, Allocation Percentage (must total 100%), and Lead Time Days. Save, then go to Manage Assignment Sets to create assignments, selecting the sourcing rule and specifying Item/Category/Global level.
指派集可以有多個嗎？同時生效還是互斥？Can there be multiple Assignment Sets? Do they coexist or are they mutually exclusive?▶
可以建立多個指派集（如：正式指派集、緊急指派集），但每個計劃只能指定一個有效指派集。要切換時，在計劃的 Edit Plan Options 中更改 Assignment Set 欄位，重新執行計劃即可。建議保留一個「Emergency」指派集，其中備用供應商的比例調高，緊急時快速切換。 Multiple assignment sets can be created (e.g., Standard Assignment Set, Emergency Assignment Set), but each plan can only use one active assignment set. To switch, edit the Assignment Set field in the plan's Edit Plan Options, then rerun the plan. Recommend maintaining an "Emergency" assignment set with higher backup supplier allocation for rapid switching during disruptions.
⚠️
常見錯誤：採購規則中多個來源的 Allocation Percentage 加總不等於 100%（例如設了 70% 和 40%），系統執行時會報錯或產生不預期結果。務必確認 Sourcing Lines 合計恰好為 100%。另外，「Transfer」類型必須指定來源組織，忘記填寫會導致計劃無法展開調撥建議。 Common Mistake: Sourcing rule lines with allocation percentages not summing to 100% (e.g., 70% + 40%). This causes errors or unexpected results during planning. Always verify sourcing lines total exactly 100%. Also, "Transfer" type requires specifying a source organization — omitting it prevents the plan from generating transfer suggestions.

🏭 Make vs Buy 決策分析 🏭 Make vs Buy Decision Analysis

▼

Oracle 供應規劃支援在同一品項上同時設定 Make 和 Buy 兩種來源，計劃員可根據成本、交期、產能等因素決定最終策略。但計劃系統本身不自動做成本比較，這個判斷需要計劃員主動觸發分析。 Oracle Supply Planning supports both Make and Buy sources for the same item simultaneously. Planners decide the optimal strategy based on cost, lead time, and capacity factors. However, the planning system does not automatically perform cost comparisons — this analysis requires proactive planner action.

實際案例：組裝模組的 Make vs Buy 分析Real Case: Assembly Module Make vs Buy Analysis

因素Factor 自製（Make）Make 外購（Buy）Buy
單位成本Unit Cost NT$45 NT$38（最低訂購量 500 件MOQ 500 units）
前置時間Lead Time 3 天（內部工單）3 days (internal WO) 21 天（供應商交期）21 days (supplier delivery)
彈性Flexibility 高：可隨需調整數量High: adjust quantity on demand 低：MOQ 500，不可小批Low: MOQ 500, no small lots
產能限制Capacity Constraint 最大 200 件/週Max 200 units/week 無上限Unlimited
品質控制Quality Control 完全掌握Full control 依賴供應商Dependent on supplier
✅
決策建議：
• 需求 < 200 件/週 → 優先自製（成本 NT$45，但彈性高，無庫存積壓風險）
• 需求 = 200–500 件/週 → 混合策略：200 件自製 + 外購補足（但注意 MOQ 500 的庫存成本）
• 需求 > 500 件/週 → 外購為主（NT$38 × 500 = NT$19,000 vs 自製 NT$45 × 500 = NT$22,500，節省 NT$3,500）
• 緊急需求（3 天內） → 必須自製，外購 21 天來不及 Decision Guide:
• Demand < 200/week → Prefer Make (NT$45/unit, high flexibility, no excess inventory risk)
• Demand 200–500/week → Mixed: make 200 + buy remainder (note MOQ 500 inventory carrying cost)
• Demand > 500/week → Buy preferred (NT$38 × 500 = NT$19,000 vs Make NT$45 × 500 = NT$22,500, saves NT$3,500)
• Urgent <3 days → Must Make; Buy's 21-day lead time is too slow
如何在 Oracle 中強制一個計劃使用 Buy（即使採購規則設 Make）？How to force Buy in Oracle even if the sourcing rule says Make?▶
有兩種方法：(1) 在採購規則中將 Make 的 Allocation 改為 0%，Buy 改為 100%，重新執行計劃。(2) 在計劃分析介面找到該品項的 Planned Work Order，右鍵選 Firm（固定化），然後手動新增 Planned Purchase Order 替代，系統下次執行時會保留已固定的訂單。建議方法 1 較乾淨，方法 2 適合一次性緊急處理。 Two approaches: (1) Change Make allocation to 0% and Buy to 100% in the sourcing rule, then rerun the plan. (2) Find the Planned Work Order in the plan analysis interface, right-click and select Firm (freeze it), then manually add a Planned Purchase Order as replacement — the system preserves firmed orders on the next run. Method 1 is cleaner; Method 2 suits one-off emergency handling.

⏳ 計劃時間欄（PTF）：凍結區 vs 自由區 ⏳ Planning Time Fence (PTF): Frozen Zone vs Free Zone

▼

Planning Time Fence（PTF）將計劃水平切成兩個區段。PTF 之內（凍結區）：計劃重新執行時，系統不會更動現有的已確認訂單，避免生產計劃頻繁變動。PTF 之外（自由區）：系統可以自由新增、修改、刪除計劃建議，根據最新需求自動調整。 The Planning Time Fence (PTF) divides the planning horizon into two zones. Inside PTF (frozen zone): when the plan reruns, the system does not modify existing firm orders, preventing frequent production plan changes. Outside PTF (free zone): the system can freely add, modify, or delete plan suggestions, auto-adjusting based on latest demand.

PTF 內（凍結）今天 → 第14天Inside PTF (Frozen) Day 0→14
PTF 外（自由）第15天 → 第90天Outside PTF (Free) Day 15→90

PTF = 14 天（典型設定）。凍結區內的計劃訂單除非計劃員手動修改，否則系統不會動它。 PTF = 14 days (typical setting). Planned orders inside the frozen zone remain unchanged unless the planner manually modifies them.

具體影響範例Concrete Impact Example

今天是週一（Day 0），PTF 設為 14 天。WO-123 預計週三（Day 3）開工。一個緊急銷售訂單在週二進來，需要 WO-123 的同一批產品提前出貨。重新執行計劃後：因為 WO-123 在 PTF 內，系統不會自動更改 WO-123 的排程。計劃員需手動評估是否可以調整，或者接受延期交貨。反之，如果需求是第 20 天的訂單（PTF 之外），系統會自動調整供應建議。 Today is Monday (Day 0), PTF set to 14 days. WO-123 scheduled to start Wednesday (Day 3). An urgent sales order arrives Tuesday needing the same products from WO-123 early. After rerunning: since WO-123 is inside PTF, the system will NOT auto-reschedule it. The planner must manually evaluate whether to adjust, or accept late delivery. Conversely, if the demand is for Day 20 (outside PTF), the system auto-adjusts supply suggestions.

PTF 應該設多長？How long should the PTF be set?▶
建議 PTF 不短於最長單一工序的前置時間。例如：如果最複雜的組裝工單需要 10 天，PTF 設 14 天合理。太短（如 3 天）→ 計劃頻繁變動，生產現場難以應對。太長（如 60 天）→ 計劃過於僵固，無法響應客戶變更。醫療器材廠通常設 10–21 天，視 Regulatory 要求而定。 PTF should not be shorter than the longest single-operation lead time. Example: if the most complex assembly WO takes 10 days, PTF of 14 days is reasonable. Too short (3 days) → frequent plan changes, difficult for shop floor to manage. Too long (60 days) → plan too rigid, cannot respond to customer changes. Medical device companies typically set 10–21 days depending on regulatory requirements.
什麼是 Demand Time Fence (DTF)？和 PTF 有什麼不同？What is Demand Time Fence (DTF)? How does it differ from PTF?▶
DTF 控制需求端：DTF 之內系統只考慮實際訂單（Actual Orders），忽略預測（Forecast）。DTF 之外則混合考慮訂單和預測。PTF 控制供應端：決定供應建議是否可被系統自動更改。兩個欄位獨立設定，通常 DTF ≤ PTF。例：DTF=7天、PTF=14天 → 第1–7天只看實際訂單、不動供應；第8–14天看訂單+預測、不動供應；第15天之後自由調整。 DTF controls the demand side: inside DTF, the system considers only actual orders, ignoring forecasts. Outside DTF, it considers both orders and forecasts. PTF controls the supply side: determines whether supply suggestions can be auto-changed by the system. Both fences are set independently; typically DTF ≤ PTF. Example: DTF=7 days, PTF=14 days → Days 1–7: actual orders only, frozen supply; Days 8–14: orders + forecast, frozen supply; Day 15+: free to adjust everything.
⚠️
常見錯誤：把 PTF 設為 0 天（或不設），以為這樣計劃最「靈活」。結果是每次重新執行計劃，所有訂單都被重新排程，生產現場的工單一直在變，操作員根本無法照計劃執行，最後大家都不相信計劃系統，又回到用 Excel 管理。 Common Mistake: Setting PTF to 0 days (or not setting it), thinking this maximizes "flexibility." Result: every plan rerun reschedules all orders; shop floor work orders keep changing; operators cannot follow the plan; everyone stops trusting the planning system and reverts to Excel management.

🚨 例外管理深度解析：四大例外類型 🚨 Exception Management Deep Dive: Four Major Exception Types

▼

Oracle 供應規劃的例外管理介面（Exception Summary）把需要人工介入的情況自動彙整。計劃員每週從這裡開始工作，而不是掃描整張計劃。以下是四大例外類型的詳細說明。 Oracle Supply Planning's Exception Summary automatically aggregates situations requiring human intervention. Planners start their week from here rather than scanning the entire plan. Below are detailed explanations of the four major exception types.

例外類型Exception Type 觸發條件Trigger Condition 具體範例Concrete Example 處理優先順序Priority 建議行動Recommended Action
Shortage 需求 > 可用供應Demand > Available Supply 第 3 週需 500 單位，但只有 320 可用，短缺 180Week 3 needs 500 units, only 320 available, short 180 P1 緊急 緊急採購或轉撥庫存Emergency PO or transfer
Overcommitted 同一批庫存被多個需求引用Same inventory referenced by multiple demands 200 單位被 SO-101 和 SO-102 各自預留，實際只有 200 不夠分配200 units reserved for both SO-101 and SO-102; only 200 total, insufficient to split P1 緊急 與銷售協商優先出貨哪個客戶Negotiate with Sales on priority customer
Late Supply 供應到達日晚於需求日期Supply arrives after demand date PO-456 預計第 22 天到，但 SO-5001 第 18 天就需要PO-456 arrives Day 22, but SO-5001 needs it by Day 18 P2 重要 催貨或找替代來源Expedite or find alternate source
Past Due 需求日期已過去但未滿足Demand date passed but unfulfilled SO-4800 的交貨日是上週三，到今天還沒出貨SO-4800 delivery was last Wednesday, still not shipped P2 重要 聯繫客戶說明，排定補救措施Contact customer, schedule remediation

例外分類排序策略（計劃員的一天）Exception Triage Strategy (A Planner's Day)

08:30 開啟 Exception Summary → 按 Priority 降序排列 → 先處理所有 Shortage 和 Overcommitted Open Exception Summary → Sort by Priority descending → Handle all Shortage and Overcommitted first
10:00 處理 Late Supply → 使用 Pegging 找根本原因 → 決定催貨或替代來源 Handle Late Supply → Use Pegging to find root cause → Decide expedite or alternate source
14:00 處理 Past Due → 聯繫客戶 → 更新系統承諾日期 Handle Past Due → Contact customers → Update committed dates in system
16:00 核准今日計劃建議 → 發布採購申請和工單 Approve today's plan suggestions → Release purchase requisitions and work orders
⚠️
常見錯誤：把所有例外都設為同等優先，導致計劃員花大量時間處理對業務影響小的例外，而真正影響客戶出貨的 Shortage 反而沒有及時處理。建議設定客製化例外規則，只讓高價值訂單（訂單金額 >100萬）或重要客戶的例外自動推播通知。 Common Mistake: Treating all exceptions with equal priority, causing planners to spend significant time on low-impact exceptions while critical Shortages affecting customer shipments are not addressed timely. Recommend setting custom exception rules to only push notifications for high-value orders (>NT$1M) or key customer exceptions.

🔗 需求追溯（Pegging）完整演練 🔗 Demand Pegging: Complete Walkthrough

▼

Pegging 是供應規劃中最強大的根本原因分析工具。它建立從最終需求（銷售訂單）到最底層供應（採購單）之間的完整追溯鏈，讓計劃員秒速找到「到底是哪個環節出了問題」。 Pegging is the most powerful root cause analysis tool in supply planning. It creates a complete traceability chain from the final demand (sales order) to the lowest-level supply (purchase order), enabling planners to instantly identify "exactly which link in the chain has the problem."

完整 Pegging 鏈範例：SO-5001 的故事Complete Pegging Chain Example: The Story of SO-5001

🛍️
SO-5001 — 客戶：台大醫院 | 需求：血糖監測儀 100 台 | 交期：第 18 天Customer: NTU Hospital | Demand: 100 Blood Glucose Monitors | Due: Day 18
⚠️ 有短缺風險⚠️ At shortage risk
▼ pegs to（追溯至）pegs to ▼
🔧
WO-123 — 品項：血糖監測儀成品 | 數量：100 台 | 計劃開工：第 10 天Item: Glucose Monitor Finished Good | Qty: 100 units | Start: Day 10
等待物料Waiting for materials
▼ needs（需要）needs ▼
🔩
Component A — 感測晶片 | 需求：100 片（每台 1 片）| 需求日：第 10 天Sensor Chip | Need: 100 units (1/monitor) | Need date: Day 10
庫存 0，完全依賴 PO-456Zero stock, fully dependent on PO-456
▼ pegs to（追溯至）pegs to ▼
📦
PO-456 — 供應商：Supplier-A | 數量：200 片 | 原交期：第 8 天 → 最新預計：第 22 天Supplier: Supplier-A | Qty: 200 units | Original due: Day 8 → Latest ETA: Day 22
🚨 根本原因：供應商延誤 14 天🚨 Root Cause: Supplier delayed 14 days
✅
結論與行動：根本原因確認為 PO-456 延誤。計劃員的選項：
(A) 向 Supplier-B 緊急訂購 100 片感測晶片（前置 21 天，來不及）
(B) 查 Supplier-C 是否有現貨（前置 5 天，可行！但單價高 20%）
(C) 與台大醫院協商，交期推遲 12 天（最後手段）
→ James 選擇 (B) + 同時對 Supplier-A 催貨，爭取提早 5 天交貨。 Conclusion & Action: Root cause confirmed: PO-456 delay. Planner options:
(A) Emergency order 100 sensor chips from Supplier-B (21-day lead time — too slow)
(B) Check if Supplier-C has stock (5-day lead time — feasible! But 20% higher price)
(C) Negotiate with NTU Hospital to push delivery 12 days (last resort)
→ James chooses (B) + expedites Supplier-A for 5-day early delivery.
如何在 Oracle 中開啟 Pegging 視圖？How to open Pegging view in Oracle?▶
在計劃分析介面（View Plan），找到有短缺的銷售訂單。右鍵點該銷售訂單 → 選 Pegging → View Pegging Details。系統顯示樹狀結構的 Demand-Supply 鏈。也可以從供應端開始（如從一張延誤的採購單），右鍵 → Pegging → View Pegged Demand，看這張採購單支撐了哪些上游需求。 In the plan analysis interface (View Plan), find the sales order with a shortage. Right-click → Pegging → View Pegging Details. The system displays a tree-structured Demand-Supply chain. You can also start from the supply side (e.g., a delayed PO), right-click → Pegging → View Pegged Demand, to see which upstream demands this PO supports.

🛡️ 安全庫存計算：統計公式與實務設定 🛡️ Safety Stock Calculation: Statistical Formula & Practical Setup

▼

安全庫存是為了應對需求波動和供應不確定性而保留的緩衝庫存。Oracle 支援三種安全庫存設定方式：手動固定值、Min-Max 計算、和統計計算（推薦）。統計計算方法考慮需求波動（σ）和前置時間，是最科學的方式。 Safety stock is buffer inventory maintained to handle demand variability and supply uncertainty. Oracle supports three safety stock setting methods: manual fixed value, Min-Max calculation, and statistical calculation (recommended). The statistical method considers demand variability (σ) and lead time, making it the most scientific approach.

完整計算範例：感測晶片（Component A）Complete Calculation Example: Sensor Chip (Component A)

已知條件：Given:

• 週需求量（D）= 1,000 件/週Weekly Demand (D) = 1,000 units/week

• 前置時間（LT）= 2 週Lead Time (LT) = 2 weeks

• 需求標準差（σ）= 150 件/週Demand Std Dev (σ) = 150 units/week

• 服務水準 = 95%（Z = 1.645）Service Level = 95% (Z = 1.645)

公式：Formula:

SS = Z × σ × √LT

SS = 1.645 × 150 × √2

SS = 1.645 × 150 × 1.414

SS ≈ 349 ≈ 350 件

再訂購點（ROP）：Reorder Point (ROP):

ROP = D × LT + SS = 1,000 × 2 + 350 = 2,350 件

當庫存跌破 2,350 件時，系統觸發採購建議When stock drops below 2,350 units, system triggers purchase suggestion

服務水準Service Level Z 值 安全庫存（σ=150, LT=2週）Safety Stock (σ=150, LT=2wks) 適用情境Use Case
90% 1.28 272 件units 一般物料，缺貨影響小General materials, low stockout impact
95% 1.645 350 件 重要零件，推薦設定Key components, recommended
99% 2.326 494 件units 醫療/航太關鍵件，不可缺貨Medical/aerospace critical parts, zero tolerance
如何在 Oracle 中設定統計安全庫存？How to set statistical safety stock in Oracle?▶
導航：Supply Chain Planning → Supply Planning → Manage Items（在計劃分析介面）。選取品項 → Edit → Safety Stock Tab → 將 Safety Stock Method 設為 "Statistical" → 輸入 Service Level（如 95）。系統會根據歷史需求自動計算 σ，或允許手動輸入。確認後儲存，下次執行計劃時生效。若需一次性批量更新多個品項，可使用 File-Based Data Import (FBDI) 匯入模板。 Navigation: Supply Chain Planning → Supply Planning → Manage Items (in plan analysis interface). Select item → Edit → Safety Stock Tab → Set Safety Stock Method to "Statistical" → Enter Service Level (e.g., 95). System auto-calculates σ from historical demand, or allows manual input. Save to take effect on the next plan run. For bulk updates across many items, use File-Based Data Import (FBDI) import template.
⚠️
常見錯誤：對所有品項一律設 99% 服務水準，導致安全庫存量龐大，資金積壓嚴重。正確做法是 ABC 分析後分層設定：A 類（高價值/高缺貨影響）→ 99%；B 類 → 95%；C 類（低價值/易取得）→ 90% 甚至不設安全庫存。 Common Mistake: Setting 99% service level for all items, resulting in enormous safety stock and severe capital lockup. Correct approach: after ABC analysis, tier the settings — A items (high value/high stockout impact) → 99%; B items → 95%; C items (low value/easy to source) → 90% or no safety stock.

🔬 模擬情境（Simulation Set）：假設分析 🔬 Simulation Set: What-If Analysis

▼

Simulation Set 讓計劃員在不影響正式生產計劃的前提下，快速評估「如果……怎麼辦？」的情境。MedTech Taiwan 的案例：Supplier X 突然通知因原物料短缺，下個月交期延誤 2 週。計劃員需要在 4 小時內向管理層匯報影響範圍和應對方案。 Simulation Sets let planners quickly evaluate "what if?" scenarios without affecting the live production plan. MedTech Taiwan case: Supplier X suddenly notifies of a 2-week delivery delay next month due to raw material shortage. Planners need to report impact and response options to management within 4 hours.

「供應商 X 延誤 2 週」模擬步驟"Supplier X Delays 2 Weeks" Simulation Steps

①
建立模擬情境：Manage Plans → Create → 選 Simulation Set → 複製現有計劃 Create simulation: Manage Plans → Create → Select Simulation Set → Copy existing plan
②
修改供應商 X 的所有在途採購單（PO-456, PO-457, PO-458），將 Promise Date 各延後 14 天 Modify all in-transit POs from Supplier X (PO-456, PO-457, PO-458), push Promise Date by 14 days each
③
重新執行模擬計劃（不影響正式計劃）→ 等待 45 分鐘 Rerun the simulation plan (does not affect live plan) → Wait 45 minutes
④
分析結果：查看 Exception Summary → 新增短缺數量、受影響銷售訂單清單、延誤金額統計 Analyze results: View Exception Summary → New shortage quantities, affected sales order list, delay amount statistics
⑤
比較模擬 vs 正式計劃：Plan Comparison → 導出影響報告給管理層 Compare simulation vs live plan: Plan Comparison → Export impact report for management
💡
模擬分析結果示例（MedTech Taiwan）：
• 受影響採購單：3 張（PO-456/457/458，合計 600 片感測晶片）
• 受衝擊銷售訂單：7 張（合計 NT$3,820,000）
• 可轉移至 Supplier-B 的數量：200 片（其餘 400 片需緊急開發新供應商）
• 轉移成本增加：NT$114,000（200 片 × NT$570 溢價）
→ 管理層決策：接受成本增加，保護客戶出貨；同時啟動供應商多元化計劃。 Simulation Results Example (MedTech Taiwan):
• Affected POs: 3 (PO-456/457/458, total 600 sensor chips)
• Impacted sales orders: 7 (total NT$3,820,000)
• Quantity transferable to Supplier-B: 200 units (remaining 400 need urgent new supplier development)
• Transfer cost increase: NT$114,000 (200 units × NT$570 premium)
→ Management decision: accept cost increase to protect customer shipments; simultaneously launch supplier diversification plan.

⚖️ 受限規劃 vs 非受限規劃 ⚖️ Constrained vs Unconstrained Planning

▼
比較項目Comparison 非受限規劃（Unconstrained）Unconstrained Planning 受限規劃（Constrained）Constrained Planning
產能限制Capacity Limits 忽略，假設產能無限Ignored; assumes infinite capacity 考慮，不超過工作中心上限Respected; cannot exceed work center limits
物料限制Material Limits 忽略，假設物料無限Ignored; assumes infinite material 考慮，受現有庫存/採購約束Respected; constrained by stock/POs
計劃結果Plan Output 顯示「理論需求」，例外多Shows "theoretical demand," many exceptions 顯示「可執行計劃」，更貼近現實Shows "executable plan," closer to reality
計算速度Calculation Speed 快（不需優化求解）Fast (no optimization solver needed) 較慢（需要 LP/優化計算）Slower (requires LP/optimization)
適用時機Best Use Case 長期需求規劃、產能分析參考Long-term demand planning, capacity gap analysis 實際執行計劃、生產排程Actual execution planning, production scheduling
💡
MedTech Taiwan 的做法：每月底執行一次非受限計劃，用於識別未來 3 個月的產能缺口，提前安排外包或加班。每週執行受限計劃，作為實際生產排程依據。 MedTech Taiwan approach: Run an unconstrained plan at month-end to identify capacity gaps 3 months ahead and arrange outsourcing or overtime in advance. Run a constrained plan weekly as the actual production scheduling basis.

📖 完整案例研究：MedTech Taiwan 一週規劃實況 📖 Comprehensive Case Study: MedTech Taiwan's Weekly Planning Reality

▼

以下是 MedTech Taiwan 計劃員 James 在某週一的完整工作流程，展示供應規劃各功能如何協同運作。 Below is a complete Monday workflow for MedTech Taiwan planner James, demonstrating how supply planning features work in concert.

08:00 — 執行週供應計劃08:00 — Run Weekly Supply Plan

James 執行 Plan: MEDTECH-WEEKLY-CONSTRAINED。輸入條件： 需求端 → 30 張未結銷售訂單（合計 2,450 台設備），週需求預測 400 台。 供應端 → 成品庫存 320 台，在製 WO 12 張，在途 PO 28 張。 45 分鐘後系統完成計算，生成：建議 PR 15 張、建議 WO 8 張、建議調撥 3 張、例外 18 個。 James runs Plan: MEDTECH-WEEKLY-CONSTRAINED. Input conditions: Demand → 30 open sales orders (2,450 devices total), weekly forecast 400 units. Supply → Finished goods stock 320 units, 12 active WOs, 28 in-transit POs. After 45 minutes: system generates 15 suggested PRs, 8 suggested WOs, 3 transfer suggestions, 18 exceptions.

09:00 — 處理例外（按優先順序）09:00 — Handle Exceptions (by priority)

P1 例外（Shortage × 2）：
例外 #1：SO-5001（台大醫院）100 台，第 18 天需要，目前短缺 → 使用 Pegging 追蹤 → 根本原因：PO-456 延誤。James 聯繫 Supplier-C 確認有現貨，下緊急 PO（100 片，5 天交期）。
例外 #2：SO-5015（長庚醫院）50 台，第 14 天需要 → Pegging 顯示：WO-130 缺少 Component B（電路板），庫存 20 片，需要 50 片，差額 30 片。James 在指派集中啟用備用供應商，生成新 PR。 P1 Exceptions (Shortage × 2):
Exception #1: SO-5001 (NTU Hospital) 100 units, needed Day 18, currently short → Use Pegging → Root cause: PO-456 delayed. James contacts Supplier-C confirming stock available, places emergency PO (100 units, 5-day lead time).
Exception #2: SO-5015 (Chang Gung Hospital) 50 units, needed Day 14 → Pegging shows: WO-130 missing Component B (circuit board), 20 in stock, needs 50, short 30 units. James activates backup supplier in assignment set, generates new PR.

11:00 — RTB 檢查（本週開工工單）11:00 — RTB Check (Work Orders Starting This Week)

系統 RTB 報告顯示本週 8 張工單中，6 張 Ready（所有物料已到位），1 張 Not Ready（WO-145 缺 1 項零件，預計週三到貨），1 張 At Risk（WO-148 的關鍵零件 PO-460 今天應該到但還沒到）。James 電話追蹤 PO-460，確認今天下午 3 點會到廠，WO-148 可以週二開工。 The RTB report shows 6 of this week's 8 work orders are Ready (all materials on hand), 1 Not Ready (WO-145 missing 1 part, expected Wednesday), 1 At Risk (WO-148's critical component PO-460 due today but not yet received). James calls to track PO-460, confirms arrival today at 3 PM, WO-148 can start Tuesday.

14:00 — 核准並發布計劃建議14:00 — Approve and Release Plan Suggestions

James 在 Review Planned Orders 介面，選取 15 張建議 PR 和 8 張建議 WO，確認無誤後批量核准。系統自動將 PR 轉成採購申請（Requisition）提交採購部門，WO 轉為正式工單發布至生產現場。整個週一工作完成，處理了 18 個例外，發布了 23 張正式單據，這在以前需要 James 花整整三天。 James enters the Review Planned Orders interface, selects 15 suggested PRs and 8 suggested WOs, confirms all details, and batch-approves them. The system automatically converts PRs to Purchase Requisitions submitted to procurement, and WOs to official work orders released to the shop floor. Monday's work is complete — 18 exceptions handled, 23 official documents released, a task that previously took James three full days.

🔑
本案例的關鍵成果：導入前 → James 3 天 + Excel。導入後 → James 半天 + Oracle。計劃準確率：從 68% 提升到 94%。緊急採購溢價：從月均 NT$450,000 降至 NT$80,000。客戶準時交貨率：從 72% 提升到 91%。 Key outcomes from this case: Before implementation → James 3 days + Excel. After → James half day + Oracle. Plan accuracy: improved from 68% to 94%. Emergency procurement premium: reduced from monthly NT$450,000 to NT$80,000. Customer on-time delivery rate: improved from 72% to 91%.

✅ 供應規劃設定清單（8 個關鍵步驟） ✅ Supply Planning Setup Checklist (8 Key Steps)

▼

❓ 常見問題 FAQ ❓ Frequently Asked Questions

▼
受限規劃和非受限規劃有什麼差異？我該用哪個？ What's the difference between constrained and unconstrained planning? Which should I use? ▶
非受限規劃假設資源（產能、物料）無限，計算速度快，結果顯示「如果沒有任何限制，理論上應該生產多少」。它的例外清單很長，因為很多訂單在現實中無法達成。適合做長期產能規劃和需求分析。

受限規劃考慮實際產能上限和物料可用量，計算較慢，但結果是「在現有資源下，真正可以執行的計劃」。例外少但更精準，適合做週計劃或日計劃作為執行依據。

建議：月底用非受限看 3 個月產能缺口；每週用受限跑執行計劃。Oracle Cloud 中在 Edit Plan Options → Plan Options Tab → Constraints Section 切換。 Unconstrained planning assumes unlimited resources (capacity, materials), calculates quickly, and shows "theoretically, how much should be produced without any constraints." Its exception list is long because many orders are unachievable in reality. Best for long-term capacity planning and demand analysis.

Constrained planning respects actual capacity limits and material availability. Slower to calculate, but produces "plans that can actually be executed within current resources." Fewer exceptions but more precise — best for weekly or daily plans as execution guidance.

Recommendation: Use unconstrained at month-end to view 3-month capacity gaps; use constrained weekly for execution planning. Switch in Oracle Cloud at Edit Plan Options → Plan Options Tab → Constraints Section.
供應計劃應該多久執行一次？ How often should I run the supply plan? ▶
沒有絕對答案，取決於業務的需求波動頻率和供應商前置時間。常見做法：
• 週計劃（最常見）： 適合製造業，每週一早上跑計劃，計劃員週一上午處理例外，週一下午發布採購和工單。
• 日計劃： 適合高需求波動行業（如快消品、電商），每天早上跑，但計劃員要有足夠時間處理每日例外。
• 月計劃： 僅用於長期產能和供應商規劃，不作為執行計劃。

MedTech Taiwan 採用週計劃 + 緊急觸發機制（若有大客戶緊急訂單，計劃員可手動觸發重新規劃）。注意：頻繁重新執行計劃會讓供應商和生產現場疲於應對，PTF 設定可以緩解這個問題。 No absolute answer — depends on demand variability frequency and supplier lead times. Common approaches:
• Weekly (most common): Suitable for manufacturing — run plan Monday morning, planners handle exceptions Monday morning, release PRs and WOs Monday afternoon.
• Daily: Suitable for high-demand-variability industries (FMCG, e-commerce). Run every morning, but planners need sufficient time for daily exception handling.
• Monthly: Used only for long-term capacity and supplier planning, not as execution plans.

MedTech Taiwan uses weekly plans + emergency trigger mechanism (if a key customer places an urgent order, planners can manually trigger a replan). Note: Frequent replanning strains suppliers and shop floor — PTF settings help mitigate this.
什麼時候應該手動覆蓋計劃建議？什麼時候讓系統自動決定？ When should I manually override plan suggestions vs let the system decide? ▶
讓系統決定（不要手動干預）：
• 常規補貨計算（系統已掌握完整資訊）
• PTF 之外的長期計劃調整
• 批量重新排程（系統效率遠高於手動）

應該手動覆蓋的情況：
• 系統不知道的資訊（如：口頭答應客戶提前交貨）
• 特殊商業決策（如：為保留重要客戶關係，接受虧損出貨）
• 緊急情況下的實時調整（系統計劃週一跑，但週三發生緊急狀況）
• 品質問題導致的物料需要緊急替代

覆蓋計劃建議後，務必使用「Firm」功能固定訂單，否則下次計劃執行時會被系統覆蓋掉。 Let the system decide (avoid manual intervention):
• Routine replenishment calculations (system has complete information)
• Long-term plan adjustments outside PTF
• Batch rescheduling (system is far more efficient than manual)

Situations requiring manual override:
• Information the system doesn't know (e.g., verbal commitment to expedite for a customer)
• Special business decisions (e.g., accepting a loss shipment to preserve a key customer relationship)
• Real-time adjustments during emergencies (plan runs Monday, but emergency occurs Wednesday)
• Material requiring urgent substitution due to quality issues

After overriding a plan suggestion, always use the "Firm" function to lock the order, or it will be overwritten on the next plan run.
「固定（Firm）」一張計劃訂單是什麼意思？什麼時候要 Firm？ What does "firming" a planned order mean? When should I firm? ▶
「Firm」是指告訴系統：「這張訂單的數量/日期已經確定，下次重新執行計劃時不要更動它。」

計劃訂單有兩種狀態：
• Planned（未固定）：每次重新執行計劃都可能被更改/取消
• Firm（已固定）：系統保留，計劃員可以手動修改但系統不會自動變動

應該 Firm 的情況：
① 已經和供應商確認的採購訂單數量
② 已經開工或即將開工的工單（PTF 內）
③ 手動覆蓋後需要保護的建議

操作方法：在計劃分析介面，選取訂單 → Actions → Firm。注意：Firm 太多訂單會讓計劃失去彈性；Firm 太少會讓人工調整在下次跑計劃後消失。建議 Firm 的範圍不超過 PTF 之內的訂單。 "Firm" tells the system: "This order's quantity/date is confirmed — do not change it on the next plan run."

Planned orders have two states:
• Planned (unfirmed): May be modified or cancelled on every plan rerun
• Firm (firmed): System preserves it; planners can manually modify but system will not auto-change

When to firm:
① Purchase order quantities confirmed with the supplier
② Work orders already started or starting soon (within PTF)
③ Manual overrides that need protection

How to do it: In the plan analysis interface, select the order → Actions → Firm. Note: Firming too many orders reduces plan flexibility; too few causes manual adjustments to disappear after the next plan run. Recommend limiting firming to orders within the PTF.

📚 供應規劃術語表 📚 Supply Planning Terminology

▼
英文術語English Term 中文Chinese 定義與用途Definition & Usage
Sourcing Rule 採購規則採購規則 定義物料來源類型（Make/Buy/Transfer）、供應商、比例和前置時間Defines material source type (Make/Buy/Transfer), supplier, allocation, and lead time
Assignment Set 指派集指派集 將採購規則指派給特定品項/品類/組織的配置集合Configuration set assigning sourcing rules to specific items/categories/organizations
Planning Time Fence (PTF) 計劃時間欄計劃時間欄 區分計劃凍結區（內）和自動調整區（外）的時間邊界Time boundary dividing the frozen zone (inside) from the auto-adjust zone (outside)
Demand Time Fence (DTF) 需求時間欄需求時間欄 之內只考慮實際訂單（忽略預測），之外混合訂單和預測Inside DTF: actual orders only (ignore forecast); outside DTF: mix orders and forecast
Pegging 需求追溯需求追溯 追蹤需求（SO）和供應（PO/WO）之間的連結，用於根本原因分析Traces links between demand (SO) and supply (PO/WO) for root cause analysis
Exception 例外例外 計劃中需要計劃員注意或干預的異常狀況（短缺、超載、逾期等）Abnormal conditions in the plan requiring planner attention or intervention (shortage, overload, late, etc.)
Firm 固定化固定化 鎖定計劃訂單不被系統自動更改，通常用於已確認或已開工的訂單Lock a planned order from system auto-changes; typically used for confirmed or started orders
Safety Stock 安全庫存安全庫存 為應對需求波動和供應不確定性預留的緩衝庫存量Buffer inventory maintained to handle demand variability and supply uncertainty
Ready to Build (RTB) 生產就緒生產就緒 工單開工前的物料齊備確認機制，分 Ready/At Risk/Not Ready 三個狀態Pre-work-order material availability check mechanism with Ready/At Risk/Not Ready status
Simulation Set 模擬情境集模擬情境集 不影響正式計劃的假設分析沙盒，用於評估供應鏈變動的影響What-if analysis sandbox that does not affect the live plan; used to evaluate supply chain change impacts
Telescoping 漸進式時間桶漸進式時間桶 計劃水平的時間粒度從近到遠由細到粗（如：近1個月日計、2-3個月週計、之後月計）Planning horizon time granularity from fine to coarse (e.g., daily for Month 1, weekly for Months 2-3, monthly thereafter)
MOQ (Minimum Order Qty) 最小訂購量最小訂購量 供應商規定的單次採購最低數量，計劃系統在生成 PR 時會自動取整到 MOQMinimum single-purchase quantity required by supplier; planning system auto-rounds PRs up to MOQ

模組 7：供應鏈協作 Module 7: Supply Chain Collaboration

透過供應商門戶和電子資料交換實現供應承諾管理、廠商自管庫存和委外製造協作 Enable supplier commit management, vendor-managed inventory, and contract manufacturing via supplier portals and EDI

Supply Collaboration VMI Contract Mfg Supplier Portal B2B / EDI
🔑
情境導讀：為什麼供應鏈協作如此關鍵？Scenario: Why Supply Chain Collaboration Is Critical

AutoParts Corp 是一家年營收超過 15 億美元的汽車零件製造商，旗下 30 家一級供應商分布於台灣、墨西哥和德國。過去，採購員每週要發送數十封 Excel 附件郵件給供應商，確認未來 13 週的需求預測；供應商再以電話或回信方式回覆「能交貨幾個」。這個流程平均耗費 3 個工作天，資料常常版本不一，導致生產線兩度因為緊急缺料停線，損失合計超過 200 萬美元。 AutoParts Corp is an automotive parts manufacturer with annual revenue exceeding $1.5 billion and 30 tier-1 suppliers across Taiwan, Mexico, and Germany. Previously, buyers sent dozens of Excel-attachment emails every week to suppliers confirming 13-week demand forecasts; suppliers replied by phone or email with "how many we can deliver." This process consumed an average of 3 business days, data versions were constantly mismatched, and production lines halted twice due to emergency shortages — a combined loss exceeding $2 million.

導入 Oracle Supply Chain Collaboration 後，AutoParts Corp 的採購部門在每月第一個工作日，系統自動將 13 週滾動預測發布至供應商入口網站（iSupplier / Supply Collaboration Portal）。供應商登入後，可在線上逐週填寫承諾數量，系統立即進行差異分析。若供應商承諾量低於預測 20% 以上，系統自動觸發例外警示，讓計劃員能在 4 小時內採取替代行動，而非 3 天後才察覺問題。 After implementing Oracle Supply Chain Collaboration, AutoParts Corp's procurement team now has the system automatically publish 13-week rolling forecasts to the supplier portal (iSupplier / Supply Collaboration Portal) on the first business day of every month. Suppliers log in and fill in committed quantities week by week online; the system immediately performs gap analysis. If a supplier's commit falls more than 20% below forecast, an exception alert fires automatically, letting planners take alternative action within 4 hours instead of discovering the problem 3 days later.

同時，針對高周轉率的電子控制單元（ECU）零件，AutoParts Corp 設定了廠商自管庫存（VMI）：供應商負責監控 AutoParts 的倉庫庫位，當庫存低於最小量 200 個時，供應商直接在系統中建立補貨請求，系統自動轉為採購申請（PR）並通知採購員審核。對於複雜子總成，則透過委外製造（Contract Manufacturing）機制，把工單委派給組裝協力廠，讓整個供應網路在一個統一平台上協作，徹底消除資訊孤島。 Meanwhile, for high-turnover Electronic Control Unit (ECU) parts, AutoParts Corp set up Vendor-Managed Inventory (VMI): suppliers monitor AutoParts' warehouse bins, and when stock drops below the minimum of 200 units, the supplier directly creates a replenishment request in the system, which auto-converts to a Purchase Requisition (PR) and notifies the buyer for approval. For complex sub-assemblies, the Contract Manufacturing mechanism delegates work orders to assembly subcontractors — bringing the entire supply network onto one unified platform and eliminating information silos entirely.

✨ 核心功能模組 ✨ Key Feature Modules

▼
📤

供應協作Supply Collaboration

計劃員每月 1 日發布 W1–W13 預測給供應商 SUP-001 (鴻毅精密)；供應商 3 日內回覆承諾量，系統比對差異並推送例外給計劃員。 Planner publishes W1–W13 forecast to supplier SUP-001 (Hung-Yi Precision) on the 1st; supplier returns commits within 3 days; system compares and pushes exceptions to the planner.

📦

廠商自管庫存 VMIVendor-Managed Inventory

Item ECU-A200 設 Min=200、Max=500。供應商登入 Portal 見庫存降至 180，立即建立補貨 320 個，系統轉 PR-12345，採購員 1 小時內審核放行。 Item ECU-A200 set Min=200, Max=500. Supplier logs in, sees stock at 180, creates replenishment of 320 units; system converts to PR-12345; buyer approves within 1 hour.

🏭

委外製造Contract Manufacturing

WO-789（500 個子總成）委派給協力廠 Pro-Mfg Ltd，協力廠每日上傳生產進度 CSV，系統自動更新完工率，預計完工日從 D+10 精確至 D+7。 WO-789 (500 sub-assemblies) delegated to Pro-Mfg Ltd; subcontractor uploads daily production CSV; system auto-updates completion %; projected finish refined from D+10 to D+7.

🌐

供應商入口網站Supplier Portal

供應商 SUP-008 登入後可見：未結 PO 清單、13 週預測、ASN 建立介面、電子發票上傳、付款狀態查詢，全程免電話聯繫採購員。 Supplier SUP-008 logs in and sees: open PO list, 13-week forecast, ASN creation, e-invoice upload, payment status — all without calling the buyer.

🔄

B2B 電子訊息B2B Messaging / EDI

大廠供應商（如博世）走 EDI 850 接訂單、856 傳 ASN、810 開發票；中小廠走 cXML 或直接使用 Portal 介面，雙軌並行，不強制 EDI 能力。 Large suppliers (e.g., Bosch) use EDI 850 for PO receipt, 856 for ASN, 810 for invoice; SME suppliers use cXML or Portal UI — both tracks coexist, no forced EDI requirement.

🚨

例外警示與重計劃Exception Alerts & Re-plan

供應商 SUP-003 承諾量僅達預測 60%（差距 800 個），系統自動發出 Priority-1 例外，計劃員在 ASCP 中點選「Accept Commit」後，隔夜計劃立即更新替代供應建議。 Supplier SUP-003 commits only 60% of forecast (gap: 800 units); system auto-raises Priority-1 exception; planner clicks "Accept Commit" in ASCP; overnight plan immediately updates alternate supply suggestions.

🔍 深入解析：供應協作月循環 🔍 Deep Dive: Monthly Supply Collaboration Cycle

▼

供應協作（Supply Collaboration）的核心是「預測→承諾→重計劃」的月循環。計劃員在每月初將 ASCP 計劃建議的 13 週滾動需求發布給供應商；供應商回覆實際能供應的數量（Commit）；系統分析差距後，計劃員決定是否接受、協商，或啟動備援供應。這個循環每月重複，使供應鏈在不斷變動的需求環境中保持同步。 The core of Supply Collaboration is the "Forecast → Commit → Re-plan" monthly cycle. At the beginning of each month, the planner publishes ASCP-recommended 13-week rolling demand to suppliers; suppliers return the quantities they can actually supply (Commit); the system analyzes gaps; the planner decides whether to accept, negotiate, or activate backup supply. This cycle repeats monthly, keeping the supply chain synchronized in a constantly changing demand environment.

具體範例：6 月循環（Item: ECU-A200）Concrete Example: June Cycle (Item: ECU-A200)

週次Week ASCP 預測量ASCP Forecast Qty 供應商承諾量Supplier Commit Qty 差距Gap 狀態Status
W1 (6/2) 1,000 1,000 0 ✅ OK
W2 (6/9) 1,200 1,000 -200 ⚠️ Minor
W3 (6/16) 1,500 900 -600 🚨 Exception
W4 (6/23) 1,200 1,200 0 ✅ OK
W5–W13 ~1,000/wk ~1,000/wk 0 ✅ OK
⚠️
常見錯誤：Common Mistake: W3 差距 600 個觸發例外，但計劃員若沒有在 ASCP 中點選「Accept Commit」，計劃引擎仍會按原預測 1,500 個計劃，導致計劃數字和供應現實脫節。必須在接受承諾後重新執行計劃。 W3 gap of 600 triggers an exception, but if the planner doesn't click "Accept Commit" in ASCP, the planning engine still plans based on the original 1,500 forecast, creating a disconnect between plan and reality. You must re-run the plan after accepting the commit.
Q：發布預測的頻率可以調整嗎？Q: Can the forecast publishing frequency be adjusted? ▶
可以。Oracle 支援每週、每兩週或每月發布。高波動產業（如消費電子）建議每週發布；穩定產業（如汽車 OEM）每月發布即可。路徑：Supply Chain Collaboration → Setup → Collaboration Parameters → Forecast Publish Frequency。 Yes. Oracle supports weekly, bi-weekly, or monthly publishing. High-volatility industries (e.g., consumer electronics) should publish weekly; stable industries (e.g., automotive OEM) can publish monthly. Path: Supply Chain Collaboration → Setup → Collaboration Parameters → Forecast Publish Frequency.
Q：供應商承諾截止日如何設定？Q: How do you set the supplier commit deadline? ▶
在 Collaboration Parameters 中設定「Commit Due Days」。例如設為 3，代表預測發布後 3 個工作日是供應商回覆承諾的截止時間；超過截止日未回覆，系統自動以預測量作為承諾量（或依設定產生 Overdue 例外警示）。 Set "Commit Due Days" in Collaboration Parameters. For example, setting it to 3 means suppliers have 3 business days from forecast publication to respond; if no commit is received by the deadline, the system either uses forecast as commit or generates an Overdue exception alert, depending on configuration.

📦 深入解析：廠商自管庫存（VMI） 📦 Deep Dive: Vendor-Managed Inventory (VMI)

▼

VMI（Vendor-Managed Inventory，廠商自管庫存）是一種讓供應商直接負責維持買方庫存水位的協作模式。買方設定最小量（Min）和最大量（Max），供應商定期登入 Portal 查看即時庫存，當庫存低於 Min 時，供應商主動發起補貨請求；系統將此請求轉換為採購申請（Purchase Requisition, PR），觸發採購流程。買方節省採購員監控庫存的時間，供應商則能更靈活安排自己的生產排程。 VMI (Vendor-Managed Inventory) is a collaboration model where the supplier directly takes responsibility for maintaining the buyer's inventory levels. The buyer sets a minimum (Min) and maximum (Max); the supplier periodically logs into the Portal to check real-time stock; when inventory drops below Min, the supplier proactively initiates a replenishment request; the system converts this into a Purchase Requisition (PR), triggering the procurement process. The buyer saves time monitoring inventory; the supplier gains flexibility in scheduling their own production.

Can also be configured at the Blanket Agreement level so replenishment automatically references contract pricing.

⚠️
常見錯誤：Min 設得比安全庫存還低Common Mistake: Min set below safety stock
若 Min=200 但生產日耗用量為 150 個，補貨前置時間 3 天，則安全庫存應為 450 個（150×3）。將 Min 設為 200 會讓補貨太晚觸發，導致實際斷料。正確的 Min 應設為 日耗量 × 前置天數 × 1.2（安全係數）。 If Min=200 but daily consumption is 150 units with a 3-day replenishment lead time, safety stock should be 450 units (150×3). Setting Min at 200 triggers replenishment too late, causing actual stockouts. The correct Min should be Daily Usage × Lead Time × 1.2 (safety factor).
Q：Supply Collaboration 和 VMI 有什麼不同？Q: What is the difference between Supply Collaboration and VMI? ▶
Supply Collaboration 是「買方主導」的預測共享機制：買方發布需求預測，供應商回覆能做多少。整個訂購流程仍由買方發起 PO。

VMI 是「供應商主導」的補貨機制：供應商監控買方庫存，主動決定何時送貨、送多少，只要不超出 Min/Max 範圍即可。兩者可以同時並用：Supply Collaboration 管中長期需求訊號，VMI 管日常庫存補貨操作。 Supply Collaboration is a "buyer-driven" forecast-sharing mechanism: the buyer publishes demand forecast and the supplier replies with how much they can supply. The buyer still initiates POs.

VMI is a "supplier-driven" replenishment mechanism: the supplier monitors the buyer's inventory and proactively decides when and how much to ship, within Min/Max boundaries. Both can be used simultaneously: Supply Collaboration manages mid-to-long-term demand signals; VMI handles day-to-day inventory replenishment.

📊 深入解析：承諾 vs 預測差異處理 📊 Deep Dive: Commit vs. Forecast Reconciliation

▼

當供應商承諾量低於預測時，計劃員面臨三種選擇：①接受承諾並調整計劃（縮減生產或找替代源），②協商要求供應商提高承諾，③啟動備援供應商。Oracle 提供「承諾差異分析」視圖，讓計劃員在一個螢幕上看到所有例外，並做出決策。 When supplier commits fall below forecast, the planner has three options: ①Accept the commit and adjust the plan (reduce production or find alternate source), ②Negotiate with the supplier to increase the commit, ③Activate a backup supplier. Oracle provides a "Commit Gap Analysis" view where planners see all exceptions on one screen and make decisions.

範例：供應商承諾 80% 情境Example: Supplier commits 80% scenario

供應商 SUP-001（主力）Supplier SUP-001 (Primary) 供應商 SUP-007（備援）Supplier SUP-007 (Backup)
預測需求Forecast Demand 1,000 —
收到承諾Received Commit 800（80%） —
缺口Gap 200 個 / 200 units
計劃員行動Planner Action 接受 800 承諾（點選 Accept Commit）Accept 800 commit (click Accept Commit) 發出緊急 PO 200 個（SUP-007 單價高 15%）Issue emergency PO for 200 units (SUP-007 unit price 15% higher)
額外成本Additional Cost 200 × $0.75 premium = $150
💡
Oracle 在「Manage Supplier Commits」畫面中提供「% Fulfilled」欄位，可快速篩選低於閾值（如 <90%）的供應商，並大量接受承諾或批次協商，不需逐筆處理。 Oracle's "Manage Supplier Commits" screen provides a "% Fulfilled" column so you can quickly filter suppliers below a threshold (e.g., <90%) and bulk-accept commits or batch-negotiate instead of processing line by line.
Q：供應商部分承諾時，系統如何處理？Q: How does the system handle partial commitments from a supplier? ▶
系統允許供應商逐週填入不同的承諾量，也允許部分週次無承諾（空白視為 0 或視設定沿用預測）。計劃員在「Manage Supplier Commits」中看到每週的預測 vs 承諾比較，可：
(1) Accept Commit：接受現有承諾，更新至計劃引擎
(2) Request Revision：向供應商發回修訂請求，要求提高承諾量
(3) Override：計劃員手動覆蓋承諾量（例如供應商口頭確認但尚未線上更新）
ASCP 在下次計劃執行時，將採用計劃員「接受」的承諾量作為供應約束。 The system allows suppliers to enter different commit quantities week by week, and allows some weeks to have no commit (blank is treated as 0 or the forecast depending on configuration). The planner sees week-by-week forecast vs. commit comparisons in "Manage Supplier Commits" and can:
(1) Accept Commit: Accept the current commit and update to the planning engine
(2) Request Revision: Send a revision request back to the supplier asking for a higher commit
(3) Override: Planner manually overrides the commit quantity (e.g., supplier verbally confirmed but hasn't updated online yet)
ASCP uses the planner-"accepted" commit quantity as a supply constraint in the next planning run.

🏭 深入解析：委外製造（Contract Manufacturing） 🏭 Deep Dive: Contract Manufacturing

▼

委外製造（Contract Manufacturing, Co-Man）是指將工單（Work Order）委派給外部協力廠商執行的協作模式。AutoParts Corp 本身不具備某些複雜子總成的製造能力，因此將這類工單委派給專業組裝廠 Pro-Mfg Ltd。協力廠接收委派後，在 Supplier Portal 上回報每日生產進度，系統同步更新工單完工百分比，計劃員可即時掌握外包生產狀況，不需電話追蹤。 Contract Manufacturing (Co-Man) is a collaboration model where work orders are delegated to external subcontractors for execution. AutoParts Corp lacks certain complex sub-assembly manufacturing capabilities, so it delegates these work orders to specialist assembler Pro-Mfg Ltd. The subcontractor receives the delegation, reports daily production progress on the Supplier Portal, and the system synchronously updates the work order completion percentage. Planners can monitor outsourced production in real time without phone follow-ups.

CSV 上傳格式：Pro-Mfg 使用系統提供的標準 CSV 模板（欄位：WO Number, Date, Completed Qty, Scrap Qty），透過 Supplier Portal 的「Upload Production Report」功能上傳。系統自動驗證格式並更新工單。 CSV upload format: Pro-Mfg uses the system-provided standard CSV template (fields: WO Number, Date, Completed Qty, Scrap Qty), uploaded via "Upload Production Report" in the Supplier Portal. The system automatically validates the format and updates the work order.
⚠️
常見錯誤：原物料出庫後忘記建立 Subcontract POCommon Mistake: Forgetting to create Subcontract PO after material issue
委外製造中，除了委派工單外，通常還需要一張加工費的採購訂單（Subcontract PO），記錄向 Pro-Mfg 支付的組裝費用。若忽略此步驟，財務上的加工成本無法正確入帳至成品標準成本。 In contract manufacturing, in addition to delegating the work order, you typically also need a Subcontract PO to record the processing fee paid to Pro-Mfg. If this step is skipped, the processing cost cannot be correctly allocated to the finished goods standard cost in financials.
Q：協力廠可以看到 AutoParts 的全部庫存資料嗎？Q: Can a subcontractor see all of AutoParts' inventory data? ▶
不行。Oracle 的供應商入口採用嚴格的資料隔離機制。供應商/協力廠只能看到與自己相關的品項、訂單和庫存數據。Pro-Mfg Ltd 在 Portal 登入後，只能看到委派給自己的工單（WO-789 等），以及該工單所需原物料在 Pro-Mfg 倉位的庫存。AutoParts 其他產品線的庫存、訂單、客戶資訊等，完全不可見。這是透過 Collaboration Agreement 和 Item Access Control 設定實現的。 No. Oracle's Supplier Portal uses strict data isolation. Suppliers/subcontractors can only see items, orders, and inventory data related to themselves. After Pro-Mfg Ltd logs into the Portal, they can only see work orders delegated to them (WO-789, etc.) and the inventory of raw materials for those work orders at Pro-Mfg's location. All of AutoParts' other product lines' inventory, orders, and customer information is completely invisible. This is achieved through Collaboration Agreement and Item Access Control settings.

🌐 深入解析：供應商入口網站功能導覽 🌐 Deep Dive: Supplier Portal Feature Walkthrough

▼

Oracle iSupplier Portal（現稱 Oracle Supplier Portal in Fusion）是供應商與買方互動的統一介面。供應商無需安裝任何軟體，只需一個瀏覽器即可完成從查詢訂單、確認交期、建立 ASN 到上傳發票的全部工作。以下是供應商 SUP-008（德國百特電子）的一日操作流程： Oracle iSupplier Portal (now Oracle Supplier Portal in Fusion) is the unified interface for supplier-buyer interaction. Suppliers need no software installation — just a browser to handle everything from checking orders, confirming delivery dates, creating ASNs, and uploading invoices. Below is a day-in-the-life walkthrough for supplier SUP-008 (Baxter Electronics Germany):

⚠️
常見錯誤：未設定供應商聯絡人角色權限Common Mistake: Not configuring supplier contact role permissions
每家供應商公司可以有多個聯絡人（業務、倉管、財務），需在 Supplier Setup → Contacts → Roles 中分別指定角色。若未設定，供應商業務可能看到財務付款資料；倉管可能誤觸發 ASN 建立。應按職能精確設定：業務=PO+Forecast，倉管=ASN，財務=Invoice+Payment。 Each supplier company can have multiple contacts (sales, warehouse, finance); roles must be assigned individually in Supplier Setup → Contacts → Roles. Without this, a supplier's sales rep might see financial payment data; warehouse staff might accidentally create ASNs. Configure by function precisely: Sales=PO+Forecast, Warehouse=ASN, Finance=Invoice+Payment.

🔄 深入解析：B2B 訊息格式（EDI / cXML） 🔄 Deep Dive: B2B Message Formats (EDI / cXML)

▼

Oracle SCM Cloud 支援多種 B2B 訊息格式，滿足不同規模供應商的整合需求。大型跨國供應商通常已有 EDI 基礎設施；中小型供應商則透過 Portal UI 或 cXML 進行整合。Oracle 透過 Oracle B2B（整合至 OIC / Oracle Integration Cloud）支援這些協定。 Oracle SCM Cloud supports multiple B2B message formats to accommodate integration needs across supplier sizes. Large multinational suppliers typically have existing EDI infrastructure; SME suppliers integrate via the Portal UI or cXML. Oracle supports these protocols through Oracle B2B (integrated with OIC / Oracle Integration Cloud).

For large implementations, first inventory whether existing EDI VAN (Value Added Network) can connect directly to OIC.

成果：AutoParts Corp 在 6 月全程無生產中斷；採購員處理 VMI 補貨的時間從 4 小時縮短至 30 分鐘（審核點選即可）；WO-789 提前完工讓 6 月底成品庫存水位提高 3 天，為 7 月旺季備料。 Results: AutoParts Corp had zero production interruptions throughout June; buyer time on VMI replenishment dropped from 4 hours to 30 minutes (just one approval click); WO-789 early completion increased end-of-June finished goods stock by 3 days' worth, building a buffer for July peak season.

❓ 常見問題 FAQ ❓ Frequently Asked Questions

▼
Q1：Supply Collaboration 和 VMI 到底有什麼不同？我們需要兩個都用嗎？ Q1: What exactly is the difference between Supply Collaboration and VMI? Do we need both? ▶

Supply Collaboration 解決的是「中長期需求可視性」問題：買方告訴供應商未來 13 週要多少，供應商確認能不能做到，雙方協調計劃。重點是需求預測的共享與承諾。 Supply Collaboration solves the "mid-to-long-term demand visibility" problem: the buyer tells the supplier how much is needed for the next 13 weeks; the supplier confirms whether they can deliver; both parties synchronize their plans. The focus is on sharing demand forecasts and obtaining commits.

VMI 解決的是「日常庫存補貨效率」問題：供應商看著買方的庫存水位，自主決定什麼時候送貨。重點是將補貨決策權下放給供應商，降低買方的庫存管理負擔。 VMI solves the "daily inventory replenishment efficiency" problem: the supplier watches the buyer's inventory levels and autonomously decides when to ship. The focus is delegating replenishment decisions to the supplier, reducing the buyer's inventory management burden.

兩者可以同時使用（AutoParts 的做法），也可以只選其一。建議：對高周轉、標準零件用 VMI；對長料期、需要提前拉動的零件用 Supply Collaboration；對特別重要的關鍵零件兩者並用。 Both can be used simultaneously (as AutoParts does), or you can choose just one. Recommendation: use VMI for high-turnover, standard parts; use Supply Collaboration for long lead-time parts requiring advance demand pull; use both for critically important key parts.

Q2：供應商登入 Portal 後，能看到我們公司的全部庫存資料嗎？ Q2: After a supplier logs into the Portal, can they see all of our company's inventory data? ▶
絕對不行。Oracle Supplier Portal 有嚴格的多租戶資料隔離。每個供應商只能看到：
• 與自己的採購訂單、預測、ASN 相關的資料
• 在 VMI 協議中明確指定給自己管理的品項庫存
• 在委外製造中委派給自己的工單

實作上，Oracle 透過 Collaboration Agreement（指定供應商可見的品項/組織）和 Portal Role（控制功能存取）雙重機制確保隔離。連同一家供應商的不同聯絡人，也可以被限制只看特定功能。 Absolutely not. Oracle Supplier Portal has strict multi-tenant data isolation. Each supplier can only see:
• Data related to their own purchase orders, forecasts, and ASNs
• Inventory of items explicitly assigned to them to manage under a VMI agreement
• Work orders delegated to them in contract manufacturing

In practice, Oracle ensures isolation through two mechanisms: Collaboration Agreements (specifying which items/organizations the supplier can see) and Portal Roles (controlling feature access). Even different contacts within the same supplier company can be restricted to specific functions only.
Q3：供應商只能承諾預測量的 60%，系統如何處理這個情況？ Q3: A supplier can only commit to 60% of the forecast. How does the system handle this? ▶
以具體數字說明：預測 1,000 個，供應商承諾 600 個，差距 400 個。

Step 1 — 例外警示：系統自動產生例外（若差距超過設定閾值，如 15%），計劃員在工作清單中看到。
Step 2 — 計劃員決策（三選一）：
①「Accept Commit」：接受 600 個承諾，ASCP 在下次計劃中以 600 為供應約束，自動尋找替代來源補足 400 個缺口
②「Request Revision」：發回修訂請求，供應商可更新承諾量（適合有緩衝空間的供應商）
③「Override Commit」：計劃員手動輸入覆蓋值（例如供應商口頭答應 700 但尚未更新系統）

Step 3 — ASCP 重計劃：接受承諾後，下一次 ASCP 計劃執行時，600 個承諾量成為「預排供應」，剩餘 400 個需求觸發替代供應訂單建議。 Using specific numbers: Forecast 1,000 units, supplier commits 600 units, gap of 400 units.

Step 1 — Exception Alert: System auto-generates exception (if gap exceeds configured threshold, e.g., 15%); planner sees it in their work list.
Step 2 — Planner Decision (3 options):
①"Accept Commit": Accept 600 commit; ASCP uses 600 as supply constraint in next plan run and automatically seeks alternate sources to fill the 400-unit gap
②"Request Revision": Send revision request back; supplier can update commit quantity (suitable for suppliers with buffer capacity)
③"Override Commit": Planner manually enters an override value (e.g., supplier verbally agreed to 700 but hasn't updated the system yet)

Step 3 — ASCP Re-plan: After accepting the commit, in the next ASCP planning run, the 600-unit commit becomes a "pre-scheduled supply"; the remaining 400-unit demand triggers suggested alternative supply orders.
Q4：Oracle SCM Cloud 支援哪些 B2B 訊息格式？我們的供應商沒有 EDI 能力怎麼辦？ Q4: What B2B message formats does Oracle SCM Cloud support? What if our suppliers don't have EDI capability? ▶
Oracle 支援三個層次的 B2B 整合，滿足不同供應商能力：

層次 1 — EDI（大型供應商）：透過 Oracle B2B / OIC 支援 ANSI X12（850/855/856/810/830）和 EDIFACT 標準。供應商需有 EDI 軟體和 VAN 帳號。

層次 2 — cXML（中型供應商）：透過 HTTPS 傳輸的 XML 格式，不需 EDI VAN，供應商端只需能發送/接收 HTTPS 請求的系統即可（大多數 ERP 都支援）。

層次 3 — Supplier Portal（小型供應商）：供應商完全不需要 IT 整合，直接用瀏覽器操作。這是 Oracle 的最大優勢之一——30 家供應商中，EDI 能力各異，但全部都能用同一套系統協作，只是操作方式不同。

建議策略：交易量大（每月 >50 張 PO）的供應商優先建立 EDI；交易量中等的用 cXML；小型或低頻交易的直接用 Portal。 Oracle supports three levels of B2B integration to accommodate different supplier capabilities:

Level 1 — EDI (Large Suppliers): Supports ANSI X12 (850/855/856/810/830) and EDIFACT standards via Oracle B2B / OIC. Supplier needs EDI software and a VAN account.

Level 2 — cXML (Mid-size Suppliers): XML format transmitted via HTTPS; no EDI VAN required — the supplier's system just needs to send/receive HTTPS requests (most ERPs support this).

Level 3 — Supplier Portal (Small Suppliers): Suppliers need zero IT integration; they operate directly from a browser. This is one of Oracle's biggest advantages — among 30 suppliers with varying EDI capabilities, all can collaborate on the same system, just using different operation modes.

Recommended strategy: Build EDI first for high-volume suppliers (>50 POs/month); use cXML for mid-volume; use Portal directly for small or low-frequency transaction suppliers.

模組 8：成本管理 Module 8: Cost Management

追蹤從採購到銷售每一筆財務成本，確保庫存評價準確、GL 分錄正確、管理報表有意義

Track every financial cost from procurement to sales — ensuring accurate inventory valuation, correct GL entries, and meaningful management reports

Receipt Accounting Cost Methods Cost Roll-up Landed Cost SLA

為什麼成本管理至關重要？

Why Cost Management Is Mission-Critical

ManufactureCo 是一家在台灣組裝電子產品的製造商，主要從中國進口 IC 元件。2023 年初，他們的財務長發現：每個月結帳後，帳上的庫存金額和實際盤點差了將近 8%，GL 的進銷存科目永遠對不起來。追查之後，發現問題來自三個地方：採購單用 Standard Cost $100 入帳，但實際發票是 $102，$2 的差額 (PPV) 沒有被正確分攤；從深圳出貨的海運費 $5,000 和關稅 $8,000 沒有被分配到各品項的存貨成本；加上月底 Cost Processor 沒跑完就關帳，導致期末成本根本不準確。

ManufactureCo assembles electronics in Taiwan, importing IC components primarily from China. In early 2023, their CFO discovered that every month after close, the book value of inventory was off by nearly 8% from physical counts — and the GL inventory accounts never reconciled. Investigation revealed three root causes: POs were received at Standard Cost $100, but actual invoices came in at $102 with the $2 PPV (Purchase Price Variance) never properly posted; ocean freight of $5,000 and duties of $8,000 from Shenzhen shipments were not allocated into item inventory cost; and the Cost Processor was not completed before period close, leaving ending costs fundamentally unreliable.

導入 Oracle SCM Cloud Cost Management 之後，ManufactureCo 首先為每一個採購料號建立了 Cost Profile，指定使用 Standard Cost Method；接著設定了 Landed Cost Trade Operation，把每次進口的海運費和關稅依採購金額比例分攤到各料號；SLA Rules Engine 確保每一筆 Receipt、Invoice Match、Inventory Transfer 都自動過到正確的 GL 科目，不再需要手動補傳票。這樣一來，財務人員每個月的結帳時間從原本的 5 天縮短到 1.5 天。

After implementing Oracle SCM Cloud Cost Management, ManufactureCo first established a Cost Profile for every purchased item, designating the Standard Cost Method. They then configured Landed Cost Trade Operations to allocate each shipment's ocean freight and duties proportionally across items by PO value. The SLA Rules Engine ensured every Receipt, Invoice Match, and Inventory Transfer automatically posted to the correct GL accounts — eliminating manual journal entries entirely. As a result, their month-end close shrank from 5 days to 1.5 days.

成本管理不只是「算錢」，它是連接採購、庫存、製造和財務的核心橋樑。當 Standard Cost 設錯、Landed Cost 沒有分攤、SLA 規則設定有誤，問題會在財務報表上像滾雪球一樣擴大。本模組將帶你了解四種成本方法的選擇邏輯、如何做 Cost Roll-up、Landed Cost 的實際分攤計算，以及 Period End Close 的正確順序。

Cost Management is not merely "counting money" — it is the central bridge connecting procurement, inventory, manufacturing, and finance. When Standard Cost is wrong, Landed Cost unallocated, or SLA rules misconfigured, problems compound exponentially on financial statements. This module walks you through the logic for selecting among four costing methods, how to perform a Cost Roll-up, the actual math behind Landed Cost allocation, and the correct sequence for Period End Close.

🔑
核心洞察Key Insight
成本管理的每一個設定錯誤，最終都會以「財務報表不準確」的形式出現。先把 Cost Method、SLA Rules 和 Period Close 順序設對，其他問題都會迎刃而解。 Every misconfiguration in Cost Management ultimately surfaces as "inaccurate financial statements." Get the Cost Method, SLA Rules, and Period Close sequence right first, and other issues resolve themselves.

📊 核心流程：從採購到關帳 📊 Core Process: From Procurement to Period Close

▼

Cost Management 在整個供應鏈流程中扮演「財務核算」的角色，每個採購、入庫、發料、製造步驟都會觸發成本事件，最終彙集到 GL。

Cost Management plays the "financial accounting" role throughout the supply chain. Every procurement, receipt, issue, and manufacturing step triggers a cost event that ultimately flows into the GL.
