🎯 核心功能模組 🎯 Core Functional Areas

▼
📥

Receipt AccountingReceipt Accounting

PO 收貨時自動產生暫估分錄。例：收貨 $100 → Dr 庫存 $100 / Cr 應計採購 $100；發票 $102 到時 → Dr 應計採購 $100, Dr PPV $2 / Cr AP $102。所有分錄由系統自動生成，無需手動過帳。 Auto-generates accrual entries on PO receipt. Example: receive $100 → Dr Inventory $100 / Cr Accrued Purchases $100; invoice at $102 arrives → Dr Accrued Purchases $100, Dr PPV $2 / Cr AP $102. All entries generated automatically — no manual journals.

⚖️

四種成本方法Four Costing Methods

Standard（製造業首選）、FIFO（先進先出，適合食品）、Periodic Average（期間加權平均）、Perpetual Average（移動加權平均）。同一 Organization 只能用一種方法，但不同 Organization 可以不同。 Standard (preferred for manufacturing), FIFO (food industry), Periodic Average (weighted avg per period), Perpetual Average (moving weighted avg). One method per Organization — but different Orgs can use different methods.

🧮

Cost Roll-upCost Roll-up

成品 X 的標準成本由 BOM 和 Routing 計算：元件 A $10 + 元件 B $15 + 勞工 0.5hr×$30=$15 + 製造費用 50%=$7.50 = 合計 $47.50。Roll-up 確保每次元件成本異動都能重算成品成本。 Finished Good X standard cost calculated from BOM and Routing: Component A $10 + Component B $15 + Labor 0.5hr×$30=$15 + Overhead 50%=$7.50 = Total $47.50. Roll-up ensures any component cost change re-calculates finished good cost.

⚓

Landed Cost ManagementLanded Cost Management

把採購以外的附加成本（海運費、關稅、保險）分攤到庫存料號。例：PO $100,000，海運費 $5,000 + 關稅 $8,000 = $13,000。品項 A 占 PO 60%，分得 $7,800 到岸成本，使 Item A 真實存貨成本更準確。 Allocates ancillary acquisition costs (ocean freight, duties, insurance) to inventory items. Example: PO $100,000, freight $5,000 + duties $8,000 = $13,000. Item A is 60% of PO, receives $7,800 landed cost, making Item A's true inventory cost accurate.

⚙️

SLA Rules EngineSLA Rules Engine

Subledger Accounting (SLA) 是 GL 分錄的規則引擎，可針對每種交易類型（Receipt、Issue、Transfer）設定借貸帳戶。例：設定 Receipt from Supplier → Dr 原料存貨 (1310000) / Cr 應計採購 (2130000)，完全彈性且可依 BU 分流。 Subledger Accounting (SLA) is the rules engine for GL entries, configurable per transaction type (Receipt, Issue, Transfer). Example: Receipt from Supplier → Dr Raw Material Inventory (1310000) / Cr Accrued Purchases (2130000). Fully flexible, configurable by BU.

📅

Period End ClosePeriod End Close

月底關帳的正確順序：先跑 Create Cost Accounting Distributions → 再 Transfer to GL → 最後 Close Period。若未跑 Cost Processor，期末庫存餘額和 GL 會不一致。順序錯誤會造成無法回復的資料問題。 Correct month-end close sequence: first Create Cost Accounting Distributions → then Transfer to GL → finally Close Period. Skipping Cost Processor leaves inventory balances inconsistent with GL. Wrong order creates irreversible data problems.

📥 深入探討：Receipt Accounting 暫估與 PPV 📥 Deep Dive: Receipt Accounting Accruals & PPV

▼

Receipt Accounting 在採購收貨時立即產生會計分錄，不需等到發票。這符合應計基礎 (Accrual Basis) 的要求：貨已到，成本應立即認列。當實際發票與 PO 金額不同時，差額以 Purchase Price Variance (PPV) 記錄。

Receipt Accounting generates accounting entries immediately upon PO receipt, without waiting for the invoice. This satisfies accrual basis requirements: goods received means cost should be immediately recognized. When the actual invoice differs from PO, the difference is recorded as Purchase Price Variance (PPV).

具體範例：ManufactureCo 採購 IC 元件Concrete Example: ManufactureCo Purchasing IC Components

步驟Step 事件Event 借方 (Dr)Debit (Dr) 貸方 (Cr)Credit (Cr) 金額Amount
1 PO 建立（不過帳）PO Created (no entry) — — —
2 收貨 @ PO Price $100Receive @ PO Price $100 庫存 (Inventory)Inventory 應計採購 (Accrued Purchases)Accrued Purchases $100
3 AP 發票到 @ $102（比 PO 高 $2）AP Invoice arrives @ $102 ($2 above PO) 應計採購 $100 + PPV $2Accrued Purchases $100 + PPV $2 應付帳款 (AP)Accounts Payable $102
4 AP 付款AP Payment 應付帳款 (AP)Accounts Payable 銀行 (Bank)Bank $102
✅
PPV 的意義What PPV Means
PPV = $2 是「採購實際付出」和「庫存計價成本」之間的差額。在 Standard Cost 方法下，庫存永遠以標準成本 $100 計，PPV 直接進 P&L。這樣可以清楚看出採購績效：PPV 越高，表示採購部門議價能力越差或市場漲價。 PPV = $2 is the gap between what was actually paid and the inventory valuation cost. Under Standard Cost, inventory is always valued at $100 standard; PPV flows directly to P&L. This clearly shows purchasing performance — higher PPV means weaker purchasing negotiation or rising market prices.
如果 PO 和發票都是 $100，應計採購帳戶會保持零餘額嗎？ If both PO and invoice are $100, will the Accrued Purchases account net to zero? ▶
理論上是的——收貨時 Cr $100，Invoice Match 時 Dr $100，餘額清零。但實際上，如果月底有「已收貨未開票」的情況（GR/IR 未清），應計採購帳戶就會有餘額，這正是 Accrual 的目的：反映已發生但未開票的負債。期末需跑 Uninvoiced Receipts 報表來核對這個差異。 Theoretically yes — receipt Cr $100, invoice match Dr $100, net zero. But in practice, if month-end has "received not invoiced" items (uncleaned GR/IR), Accrued Purchases will have a balance. This is exactly the purpose of accruals: reflecting liabilities incurred but not yet invoiced. Run the Uninvoiced Receipts report at period-end to reconcile this balance.
PPV 和 Manufacturing Variance 有什麼不同？ What is the difference between PPV and Manufacturing Variance? ▶
PPV (Purchase Price Variance) 發生在採購時：實際採購價格和 PO 單價之間的差異，或（在 Standard Cost 下）實際採購價和標準成本之間的差異。它反映的是採購部門的績效。
Manufacturing Variance 發生在生產時：實際投入的原料、人工、製費和標準成本之間的差異，反映的是生產部門的效率。例如：標準用料 10 個元件，實際用了 11 個，多出的 1 個就是 Material Usage Variance。 PPV (Purchase Price Variance) occurs at procurement: the difference between actual purchase price and PO unit price, or (under Standard Cost) between actual price and standard cost. It reflects purchasing department performance.
Manufacturing Variance occurs in production: the difference between actual inputs (material, labor, overhead) and standard cost, reflecting production efficiency. Example: standard calls for 10 components, actual used 11 — the extra 1 is Material Usage Variance.
⚠️
常見錯誤：忘記設定 Receipt Accounting OptionsCommon Mistake: Forgetting Receipt Accounting Options
如果 Inventory Organization 的 Receipt Accounting 選項沒有勾選「Accrue at Receipt」，系統不會在收貨時產生暫估分錄，只有在 Invoice Match 時才會過帳。這會導致月底庫存金額和 GL 差異巨大，且難以追查原因。
Navigation：Setup → Manufacturing → Manage Inventory Parameters → 確認 Accrue at Receipt = Yes。 If the Inventory Organization's Receipt Accounting option does not have "Accrue at Receipt" enabled, no accrual entries are generated at receipt — entries only post at Invoice Match. This causes massive discrepancies between inventory value and GL at month-end that are difficult to trace.
Navigation: Setup → Manufacturing → Manage Inventory Parameters → confirm Accrue at Receipt = Yes.

⚖️ 深入探討：四種成本方法比較 ⚖️ Deep Dive: Comparing Four Costing Methods

▼

選擇成本方法是導入 Cost Management 最重要的決策之一，一旦有交易記錄後就很難更改。以下以「100 單位 @$10 入庫，再入 100 單位 @$12，出庫 150 單位」為例說明四種方法的差異。

Choosing a costing method is one of the most critical decisions when implementing Cost Management — it's very difficult to change once transactions exist. The following example illustrates the four methods: receive 100 units @$10, then receive 100 more @$12, then issue 150 units.

成本方法Cost Method 出庫 150 單位的成本Cost of 150-unit Issue 剩餘 50 單位庫存值Remaining 50-unit Inventory 計算邏輯Calculation Logic 適用情境Best For
Standard Cost 150 × $10 = $1,500 (標準) + PPV 50 × $10 = $500 固定用預設標準成本，差異進 VarianceFixed standard; differences go to Variance 製造業、高度重複生產Manufacturing, repetitive production
FIFO 100×$10 + 50×$12 = $1,600 50 × $12 = $600 先入先出，最舊的批次先出Oldest batch exits first 食品、藥品（先進先出符合物流）Food, pharma (matches physical flow)
Periodic Average $1,650 × 75% = $1,237.50 $1,650 × 25% = $412.50 期末計算全期平均，期中用估計成本Period-end weighted average; mid-period uses estimate 批發/零售，不需即時精確成本Wholesale/retail, real-time cost not critical
Perpetual Average 每次入庫即更新平均，動態計算Avg updated each receipt: dynamic 依更新後平均成本計算Based on updated average 移動加權平均，每筆交易後重算Moving weighted average, recalculated after each transaction 商品貿易、進口商Trading companies, importers
💡
FIFO vs Average 對利潤的影響：在漲價趨勢下（$10 → $12），FIFO 出庫成本 $1,600 > Average 出庫成本 $1,237.50（Periodic）。因此 FIFO 方法下毛利較低，Average 方法下毛利較高。若售價相同 $1,800，FIFO 毛利 = $200，Average 毛利 = $562.50。這對財務報表影響顯著。 FIFO vs Average Impact on Profit: In a rising-price environment ($10 → $12), FIFO issue cost $1,600 > Periodic Average issue cost $1,237.50. So under FIFO, gross profit is lower; under Average, gross profit is higher. With the same selling price of $1,800: FIFO gross profit = $200, Average gross profit = $562.50. This materially impacts financial statements.
同一個 Organization 可以對不同料號用不同成本方法嗎？ Can I use different costing methods for different items in the same Organization? ▶
不行。Oracle SCM Cloud 中，Costing Method 是在 Inventory Organization 層級設定的，整個 Org 所有料號必須用相同的成本方法。如果你有不同需求（例如成品用 Standard，但貿易品用 Average），需要設立不同的 Inventory Organization。
Navigation：Setup → Cost Management → Manage Cost Organizations → 查看 Default Cost Method。 No. In Oracle SCM Cloud, the Costing Method is set at the Inventory Organization level — all items in the same Org must use the same method. If you have different requirements (e.g., finished goods on Standard, trading goods on Average), you need separate Inventory Organizations.
Navigation: Setup → Cost Management → Manage Cost Organizations → view Default Cost Method.
⚠️
常見錯誤：Standard Cost 忘記年度更新Common Mistake: Forgetting Annual Standard Cost Update
Standard Cost 是「固定成本」，通常每年設定一次。如果年初設 $10，但年中原料漲到 $15，全年的 PPV 累計達 50%，管理報表完全失真。建議每季或半年做一次 Cost Scenario 分析，確認標準成本是否仍然合理，必要時進行 Cost Update。 Standard Cost is a "fixed cost," typically set once per year. If set at $10 at year-start but material rises to $15 mid-year, cumulative annual PPV hits 50% and management reports become meaningless. Recommend quarterly or semi-annual Cost Scenario analysis to confirm standard cost reasonableness; perform Cost Update if necessary.

🧮 深入探討：Standard Cost Roll-up（標準成本展開） 🧮 Deep Dive: Standard Cost Roll-up

▼

Cost Roll-up 是根據 BOM（物料清單）和 Routing（工藝路線）自動計算成品的標準成本。每次元件成本或資源費率改變，都需要重新 Roll-up 才能更新成品的標準成本。

Cost Roll-up automatically calculates the standard cost of finished goods based on BOM (Bill of Materials) and Routing (operations sequence). Every time a component cost or resource rate changes, a Roll-up is required to update the finished good's standard cost.

實際範例：成品 FG-001（ManufactureCo 電路板）Real Example: Finished Good FG-001 (ManufactureCo Circuit Board)

成本元素Cost Element 來源Source 計算方式Calculation 金額Amount
元件 A（IC 晶片）Component A (IC Chip) BOM Qty 1 × Standard $10 1 × $10 $10.00
元件 B（電阻電容套件）Component B (Resistor/Cap Kit) BOM Qty 1 × Standard $15 1 × $15 $15.00
製造人工（Labor）Manufacturing Labor Routing 0.5 hr × Resource Rate $30/hr 0.5 × $30 $15.00
製造費用（Overhead）Manufacturing Overhead Labor Cost × Overhead Rate 50% $15 × 50% $7.50
成品 FG-001 標準成本合計FG-001 Total Standard Cost $47.50
✅
Navigation（執行 Cost Roll-up）：
Cost Management → Cost Accounting → Manage Cost Scenarios → 建立 Scenario → 選擇 BOM/Routing → 執行 Roll-up → 審核結果 → 若滿意則 Publish（更新為現行標準成本）。
建議：先在 Pending Cost Scenario 中測試，確認結果合理後再 Publish，避免直接影響現行成本。 Navigation (Running Cost Roll-up):
Cost Management → Cost Accounting → Manage Cost Scenarios → Create Scenario → Select BOM/Routing → Run Roll-up → Review results → Publish if satisfactory (updates as current standard cost).
Tip: Test in a Pending Cost Scenario first; confirm results are reasonable before Publishing to avoid directly impacting current costs.
Cost Scenario 和 Cost Roll-up 有什麼關係？ What is the relationship between a Cost Scenario and a Cost Roll-up? ▶
Cost Scenario 是一個「沙盒環境」，讓你可以在不影響現行成本的情況下測試成本異動的影響。在 Scenario 裡調整某個元件的標準成本，然後執行 Roll-up，系統會計算所有相關成品的新成本。確認結果後，Publish 這個 Scenario 才會正式更新現行標準成本。這是一種「What-if 分析工具」。 A Cost Scenario is a "sandbox environment" that lets you test the impact of cost changes without affecting current costs. In the Scenario, adjust a component's standard cost, then run Roll-up — the system calculates new costs for all affected finished goods. After confirming results, Publishing the Scenario officially updates current standard costs. Think of it as a "What-if analysis tool."
⚠️
常見錯誤：BOM 版本未更新就做 Roll-upCommon Mistake: Running Roll-up with Outdated BOM Version
Cost Roll-up 讀取的是 Cost Accounting BOM（不一定是生產用的 Engineering BOM）。如果工程部門更新了 BOM 加入新元件，但沒有同步到 Cost Accounting 使用的 BOM 版本，Roll-up 結果會低估成品成本。
每次做 Roll-up 前，確認 Manage Production Recipes 或 Manage Bills of Materials 中的有效 BOM 版本與生產實際使用的版本一致。 Cost Roll-up reads the Cost Accounting BOM (which may differ from the Engineering BOM used in production). If engineering updates the BOM to add a new component but doesn't sync to the Cost Accounting BOM version, Roll-up results will understate finished good cost.
Before each Roll-up, confirm the effective BOM version in Manage Production Recipes or Manage Bills of Materials matches what production actually uses.

⚓ 深入探討：Landed Cost（到岸成本） ⚓ Deep Dive: Landed Cost Management

▼

Landed Cost 解決了一個常見問題：採購單的價格只是「貨物本身」的價格，但實際取得存貨還需要支付運費、關稅、保險等費用。Landed Cost 把這些附加費用依照一定的分攤基準（金額、重量、數量等）分配到各料號，使庫存成本更真實反映取得成本。

Landed Cost solves a common problem: the PO price only covers the goods themselves, but actually acquiring inventory also requires paying freight, duties, insurance, and more. Landed Cost allocates these ancillary costs across items using an allocation basis (value, weight, quantity, etc.), making inventory cost truly reflect acquisition cost.

實際範例：ManufactureCo 從深圳進口一批零件Real Example: ManufactureCo Importing from Shenzhen

費用項目Cost Item 金額Amount Trade Operation TypeTrade Operation Type
PO 採購金額PO Purchase Amount $100,000 —
海運費Ocean Freight $5,000 (5%) Freight
進口關稅Import Duties $8,000 (8%) Duty
貨物保險Cargo Insurance $500 (0.5%) Insurance
總到岸成本附加費Total Landed Cost Surcharges $13,500 —

按採購金額比例分攤（Allocation by Value）Allocation by PO Value Proportion

料號Item PO 金額PO Value 占比% of PO 分攤到岸成本Allocated Landed Cost 真實到岸成本True Landed Cost
IC-A001 $60,000 60% $13,500 × 60% = $8,100 $60,000 + $8,100 = $68,100
IC-B002 $30,000 30% $13,500 × 30% = $4,050 $30,000 + $4,050 = $34,050
IC-C003 $10,000 10% $13,500 × 10% = $1,350 $10,000 + $1,350 = $11,350
💡
Navigation（設定 Landed Cost）：
Supply Chain Management → Landed Cost Management → Manage Trade Operations
1. 建立 Trade Operation Type（如 Ocean Freight、Import Duty）
2. 設定 Charge（費用項目）和 Allocation Basis
3. 收到 Carrier 發票後，在 Trade Operation 中輸入實際費用
4. 執行 Allocate and Post 將費用分攤至各料號庫存成本 Navigation (Setting Up Landed Cost):
Supply Chain Management → Landed Cost Management → Manage Trade Operations
1. Create Trade Operation Types (e.g., Ocean Freight, Import Duty)
2. Define Charges (cost items) and Allocation Basis
3. After receiving carrier invoice, enter actual amount in Trade Operation
4. Run Allocate and Post to distribute costs to item inventory costs
如果海運費發票很晚才來（已過期末），怎麼處理？ What if the freight invoice arrives late (after period close)? ▶
Oracle 提供兩種處理方式：
1. Estimated Charges（估計費用）：在收貨前就建立 Trade Operation 並輸入估計費用，系統先以估計值分攤。等實際發票到時，過 Actual Charge，系統自動計算差異並調整。
2. Actual Period Posting：若費用在下一個 Period 才知道，在下一 Period 過帳，費用認列到發生的 Period（使用 Landed Cost Adjustment）。
建議使用方式 1，以確保各期成本更準確。 Oracle provides two approaches:
1. Estimated Charges: Create a Trade Operation before receipt and enter estimated costs; system allocates based on estimate. When the actual invoice arrives, post Actual Charge — system automatically calculates and adjusts the difference.
2. Actual Period Posting: If the cost is only known in the next period, post in the next period with a Landed Cost Adjustment.
Method 1 is recommended for more accurate period costs.
⚠️
常見錯誤：Trade Operation 和 PO 沒有正確關聯Common Mistake: Trade Operation Not Correctly Associated with PO
建立 Trade Operation 時必須關聯到正確的 Shipment/Receipt。如果關聯錯誤（例如關聯到前一批貨的 PO），到岸成本會被分攤到錯誤的庫存批次。每次建立 Trade Operation 後，務必在分攤前確認 Reference Document（PO / Shipment）是否正確。 When creating a Trade Operation, it must be associated with the correct Shipment/Receipt. If associated incorrectly (e.g., linked to a previous batch's PO), landed costs will be allocated to the wrong inventory batch. Always verify the Reference Document (PO/Shipment) is correct before running allocation.

⚙️ 深入探討：SLA Rules Engine（分類帳規則引擎） ⚙️ Deep Dive: SLA Rules Engine (Subledger Accounting)

▼

Subledger Accounting (SLA) 是 Oracle 用來決定「每筆庫存或採購交易，應該過到哪個 GL 帳戶」的規則引擎。它位於 Inventory/Procurement 子分類帳和 GL 總帳之間，透過 Journal Entry Rule Sets 和 Account Derivation Rules 彈性設定借貸帳戶。

Subledger Accounting (SLA) is Oracle's rules engine for determining "which GL account each inventory or procurement transaction should post to." It sits between the Inventory/Procurement subledger and the GL, using Journal Entry Rule Sets and Account Derivation Rules to flexibly configure debit/credit accounts.

SLA 架構層次SLA Configuration Hierarchy

📌
Account Derivation Rule 判斷帳戶的條件邏輯（如：若 Item Category = 原料，則帳戶 = 1310000）Conditional logic to derive account (e.g., if Item Category = Raw Material → account 1310000)
▶
📋
Journal Line Rule 定義單一分錄行（借或貸、對應哪個 Subledger 金額）Defines one journal line (Dr or Cr, which subledger amount)
▶
📁
Journal Entry Rule Set 組合多條 Journal Line Rules 為完整傳票Combines multiple Journal Line Rules into a complete entry
▶
🔗
Accounting Method 把 Rule Set 指定給特定 Application 和 Event TypeAssigns Rule Sets to specific Applications and Event Types
▶
🏢
Ledger Assignment 將 Accounting Method 指定給分類帳（Ledger）Assigns Accounting Method to a Ledger

常見 Event Type 的 SLA 設定範例SLA Configuration Examples for Common Event Types

交易類型Event Type 借方帳戶Debit Account 貸方帳戶Credit Account
Receipt from Supplier 原料存貨 1310000Raw Material Inventory 1310000 應計採購 2130000Accrued Purchases 2130000
Inventory Issue to WIP WIP 1320000 原料存貨 1310000Raw Material Inventory 1310000

SLA 規則設定後為何 GL 分錄看起來不對？ After setting up SLA rules, why do GL entries look wrong? ▶
最常見的原因有三：
1. Rule 優先順序錯誤：SLA 會按條件規則的順序依序評估，第一個符合條件的規則即適用。若較廣泛的規則排在較精細的規則前面，精細規則永遠不會被執行。
2. Accounting Method 未正確指定：Rule Set 建好了，但沒有在 Accounting Method 中被引用，或 Accounting Method 沒有指定給正確的 Ledger。
3. 沒有 Validate 規則：修改 SLA 設定後必須執行 Validate，否則舊版本設定還在生效。
Navigation：Setup → Financial Reporting → Subledger Accounting → Manage Accounting Methods。 Three most common causes:
1. Wrong Rule Priority: SLA evaluates condition rules in sequence — the first matching rule applies. If a broad rule appears before a specific rule, the specific rule never executes.
2. Accounting Method Not Correctly Assigned: Rule Set is built, but not referenced in an Accounting Method, or the Accounting Method is not assigned to the correct Ledger.
3. Rules Not Validated: After modifying SLA setup, you must run Validate; otherwise the old version remains in effect.
Navigation: Setup → Financial Reporting → Subledger Accounting → Manage Accounting Methods.
⚠️
常見錯誤：複製 Standard Accounting Method 後直接修改Common Mistake: Directly Modifying a Copied Standard Accounting Method
Oracle 提供預設的 Standard Accrual Accounting Method。很多客戶直接複製後修改，但忘記把修改後的 Accounting Method 重新指定到 Ledger。結果：Ledger 仍然使用原始的 Standard Method，自訂的規則完全沒有生效。
每次修改或建立新的 Accounting Method 後，務必到 Manage Accounting Methods → 確認 Ledger Assignment 已更新。 Oracle provides a default Standard Accrual Accounting Method. Many customers copy and modify it, but forget to reassign the modified Accounting Method back to the Ledger. Result: the Ledger still uses the original Standard Method; custom rules never take effect.
After modifying or creating a new Accounting Method, always go to Manage Accounting Methods → confirm Ledger Assignment is updated.

🔒 深入探討：Period End Close 關帳流程 🔒 Deep Dive: Period End Close Sequence

▼

月底關帳是 Cost Management 最容易出錯的環節。步驟必須按照特定順序執行，且需要在正確的時間點截斷交易，否則後面的步驟無法執行或結果不準確。

Month-end close is the step in Cost Management where most errors occur. Steps must be executed in a specific sequence, with transactions cut off at the right time, or subsequent steps cannot run or produce incorrect results.

# 步驟Step 系統操作System Action 注意事項Notes
1 確認所有月內交易完成Confirm all month-end transactions complete 盤點、入庫、出庫、轉倉全部過帳All inventory, receipts, issues, transfers posted 截止後的交易強制進下一期Post-cutoff transactions forced to next period
2 關閉 Inventory PeriodClose Inventory Period Manage Inventory Accounting Periods → Close 關閉後不可再入庫存交易No more inventory transactions after close
3 執行 Cost ProcessorRun Cost Processor Cost Accounting → Create Cost Accounting Distributions 最關鍵步驟，計算所有期內成本分攤Most critical step — calculates all period cost distributions
4 執行 Landed Cost 分攤Run Landed Cost Allocation Landed Cost Management → Allocate and Post 確認所有 Trade Operation 都已過帳Ensure all Trade Operations are posted
5 核對 Uninvoiced ReceiptsReview Uninvoiced Receipts 執行 Uninvoiced Receipts 報表Run Uninvoiced Receipts report 確認應計採購帳戶餘額合理Confirm Accrued Purchases balance is reasonable
6 Transfer to GLTransfer to GL Cost Accounting → Transfer Costs to General Ledger 將 Subledger 分錄傳到 GLTransfers subledger entries to GL
7 關閉 Cost Accounting PeriodClose Cost Accounting Period Manage Cost Accounting Periods → Close 確認 GL 餘額與 Inventory 值相符Confirm GL balance matches Inventory value
8 GL Period CloseGL Period Close General Ledger → Manage Accounting Periods → Close 最後關閉 GL PeriodFinally close GL Period
如果忘記跑 Cost Processor 就關帳了，會怎樣？ What happens if I forget to run the Cost Processor before period close? ▶
這是最嚴重的 Period Close 錯誤之一。後果：
1. 期末庫存成本不準確——Cost Processor 未跑，表示某些交易的成本分攤計算沒有完成，庫存帳面值可能偏低或偏高。
2. GL 分錄不完整——Transfer to GL 時只會傳已處理的交易，未處理的交易沒有 GL 分錄，造成 GL 和 Inventory 的差異。
3. 一旦 Close Cost Accounting Period，無法重跑 Cost Processor（因為 Period 已關閉，系統不接受新的成本分攤）。
唯一補救方式：重新開啟 Period（如果 GL 尚未 Close）或在下一個期間做 Prior Period Adjustment。
預防方法：在月底關帳 SOP 中加入「確認 Cost Processor 所有批次狀態 = Completed」的核對項目。 This is one of the most serious Period Close errors. Consequences:
1. Inaccurate period-end inventory cost — Cost Processor not run means cost distribution calculations for some transactions are incomplete; inventory book value may be under or overstated.
2. Incomplete GL entries — Transfer to GL only sends processed transactions; unprocessed transactions have no GL entries, creating a GL-vs-Inventory discrepancy.
3. Once the Cost Accounting Period is Closed, Cost Processor cannot be re-run (period closed, system rejects new cost distributions).
Only remedies: reopen the period (if GL not yet closed) or post a Prior Period Adjustment in the next period.
Prevention: Add "confirm all Cost Processor batches have status = Completed" as a mandatory checklist item in the month-end close SOP.
⚠️
常見錯誤：Inventory Period 和 Cost Accounting Period 的關閉時序混淆Common Mistake: Confusing Inventory Period vs. Cost Accounting Period Close Timing
Oracle 有兩個不同的 Period 概念：
- Inventory Accounting Period：控制庫存交易（入庫/出庫/轉倉）是否可以過帳，先關
- Cost Accounting Period：控制成本分攤計算是否完成，後關
錯誤順序：若先關 Cost Accounting Period 再跑 Cost Processor，Cost Processor 會失敗。正確順序：Inventory Period Close → Cost Processor → Transfer to GL → Cost Accounting Period Close → GL Close。 Oracle has two distinct Period concepts:
- Inventory Accounting Period: Controls whether inventory transactions (receipts/issues/transfers) can post — close first
- Cost Accounting Period: Controls whether cost distribution calculations are complete — close last
Wrong sequence: closing Cost Accounting Period before running Cost Processor causes Cost Processor to fail. Correct: Inventory Period Close → Cost Processor → Transfer to GL → Cost Accounting Period Close → GL Close.

🔄 深入探討：SCFO 跨法人調撥與內部利潤 🔄 Deep Dive: SCFO Cross-Legal-Entity Transfer Pricing

▼

SCFO（Supply Chain Financial Orchestration）處理跨法人（Legal Entity）的庫存調撥，當 Factory Org（製造法人）和 Sales Org（銷售法人）屬於不同公司時，需要設定 Transfer Price 和內部利潤，並在合併報表時做消除分錄。

SCFO (Supply Chain Financial Orchestration) handles inventory transfers across legal entities. When the Factory Org (manufacturing entity) and Sales Org (selling entity) belong to different legal entities, Transfer Price and internal profit must be configured, with elimination entries at consolidation.

範例：Factory TW → Sales HKExample: Factory TW → Sales HK

Factory TW Sales HK 合併消除Consolidation Elimination
存貨成本Inventory Cost $47.50 (Standard) $60.00 (Transfer Price) 消除 $12.50 內部利潤Eliminate $12.50 internal profit
分錄（Factory）Entry (Factory) Dr 應收帳款 $60 / Cr 銷售收入 $60 + Dr 銷貨成本 $47.50 / Cr 存貨 $47.50 — —
分錄（Sales HK）Entry (Sales HK) — Dr 存貨 $60 / Cr 應付帳款 $60 —
💡
SCFO 透過 Financial Orchestration Flow 自動生成上述分錄，不需要手動過帳。設定路徑：Setup → Supply Chain Financial Orchestration → Manage Financial Orchestration Flows。 SCFO automatically generates the above entries through Financial Orchestration Flows, eliminating manual journal entries. Setup: Setup → Supply Chain Financial Orchestration → Manage Financial Orchestration Flows.

🗑️ 深入探討：製造廢料成本處理 🗑️ Deep Dive: Handling Scrap Cost in Manufacturing

▼

製造過程中不可避免地會產生廢料（Scrap），廢料的成本處理方式會直接影響成品成本和 P&L。Oracle SCM Cloud 提供兩種主要廢料處理方式。

Manufacturing inevitably generates scrap, and how scrap costs are handled directly impacts finished good cost and P&L. Oracle SCM Cloud provides two main approaches.

處理方式Approach 說明Description GL 分錄GL Entry 適用情境Best For
納入 BOM 計畫廢料Planned Scrap in BOM BOM 中設定元件的 Scrap % (如 5%)，Roll-up 時自動把廢料成本算進標準成本Set component Scrap % (e.g., 5%) in BOM; Roll-up auto-includes scrap cost in standard cost 成本已含在成品成本中，無額外分錄Cost included in finished good cost, no extra entry 可預測的固定廢料率Predictable, stable scrap rates
非計畫廢料 (Scrap Transaction)Unplanned Scrap Transaction 生產異常廢料，在 WO 執行 Scrap TransactionAbnormal scrap during production; run Scrap Transaction on Work Order Dr 廢料損失 (Scrap Loss) / Cr WIP 偶發性品質問題Occasional quality issues
✅
若廢料還有殘值（可回收），需先做 Miscellaneous Receipt 把廢料入庫（以殘值計），再沖銷 WIP 成本差異。SLA 規則要確保廢料殘值的 GL 帳戶（如 1390000 廢料庫存）和 Scrap Loss（如 7020000）分別設定正確。 If scrap has salvage value (recyclable), first do a Miscellaneous Receipt to receive scrap into inventory at salvage value, then offset the WIP cost variance. SLA rules must correctly map scrap residual value to a separate GL account (e.g., 1390000 Scrap Inventory) and Scrap Loss (e.g., 7020000).

1月份損益分析January P&L Analysis

這就是為什麼財務報表需要同時追蹤 PPV 和 Landed Cost——它們分別影響採購績效分析和真實庫存評價。 Sales Revenue: $64,000 | COGS (Standard): $38,000 | Standard Gross Profit: $26,000
Unfavorable PPV: -$200 (paid more than PO) | Landed Cost: $1,300 (in inventory, flows to COGS when sold)
Period-end Inventory (200 units at Standard): $9,500
This illustrates why financial statements must track both PPV and Landed Cost — they separately impact purchasing performance analysis and true inventory valuation.

❓ 常見問題解答 (FAQ) ❓ Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)

▼
Q1：如果忘記在期末前跑 Cost Processor，會怎樣？有補救方法嗎？ Q1: What happens if I forget to run Cost Processor before period end? Any remedy? ▶
忘記跑 Cost Processor 是最嚴重的 Period Close 錯誤之一。

後果：
- 部分交易沒有成本分攤分錄，庫存帳面值不準確
- Transfer to GL 時，這些未處理的交易不會產生 GL 分錄
- Cost Accounting Period Close 後，Cost Processor 不可再跑

補救方法：
1. 若 GL Period 尚未 Close：重新開啟 Cost Accounting Period（需申請系統權限），跑 Cost Processor，再重新 Transfer to GL，再關帳
2. 若 GL Period 已 Close：在下一期間過 Prior Period Adjustment（但這需要 GL 層面的手動傳票，且不能改變已關閉期間的成本帳）

預防方法：建立月底關帳 Checklist，其中一項就是「確認 Cost Processor 最後一次執行的結果 = Completed，且無 Error 訊息」，並設定在期末前一天自動跑 Cost Processor。 Forgetting to run Cost Processor is one of the most serious Period Close errors.

Consequences:
- Some transactions have no cost distribution entries; inventory book value inaccurate
- During Transfer to GL, unprocessed transactions generate no GL entries
- After Cost Accounting Period Close, Cost Processor cannot be re-run

Remedies:
1. If GL Period not yet Closed: Reopen Cost Accounting Period (requires elevated system privilege), run Cost Processor, re-run Transfer to GL, then re-close
2. If GL Period already Closed: Post a Prior Period Adjustment in the next period (requires manual GL journal; cannot change costs in the closed period)

Prevention: Build a month-end Checklist with one item: "Confirm last Cost Processor run result = Completed with no Error messages." Also schedule Cost Processor to auto-run the day before period-end.
Q2：同一個 Inventory Organization 可以有不同料號用不同成本方法嗎？ Q2: Can different items in the same Inventory Organization use different costing methods? ▶
不行。Oracle SCM Cloud 的 Costing Method 是 Organization 層級的設定，整個 Org 所有料號都必須用相同的成本方法。

但可以在 Cost Profile 層級做一些差異設定，例如：
- 部分料號啟用 Lot-based Costing（追蹤每個批號的獨立成本）
- 部分料號啟用 Landed Cost，其他不啟用

如果你的業務確實需要不同成本方法，解決方案是設立不同的 Inventory Organization（例如：成品 Org 用 Standard Cost，貿易品 Org 用 Perpetual Average），這需要重新規劃 Organization Structure。 No. In Oracle SCM Cloud, Costing Method is set at the Organization level — all items in the same Org must use the same method.

However, some differentiation is possible at the Cost Profile level, for example:
- Enable Lot-based Costing for some items (tracking individual batch costs)
- Enable Landed Cost for some items but not others

If your business truly requires different costing methods, the solution is separate Inventory Organizations (e.g., Finished Goods Org on Standard Cost, Trading Goods Org on Perpetual Average). This requires redesigning the Organization Structure.
Q3：PPV 和 Manufacturing Variance 有什麼不同？ Q3: What is the difference between PPV and Manufacturing Variance? ▶
PPV (Purchase Price Variance)：
- 發生時機：採購時（PO Receipt 或 Invoice Match）
- 公式：(實際採購單價 - 標準成本) × 採購數量
- 責任部門：採購部
- 範例：標準成本 $10，實際採購 $10.20，採購 1,000 pcs → PPV = ($10.20 - $10) × 1,000 = $200 不利差異
- 意義：反映採購是否能以標準成本取得材料，是採購績效指標

Manufacturing Variance（製造差異）：
- 發生時機：生產完工時
- 類型：Material Usage Variance（用料差異）、Labor Efficiency Variance（工時差異）、Overhead Spending Variance（費用差異）
- 責任部門：生產部
- 範例：標準用料 10 pcs/unit，實際用 11 pcs → Material Usage Variance = 1 pc × $10 × 1,000 units = $10,000 不利差異
- 意義：反映生產效率，是生產部績效指標

簡記：PPV 比較「買多貴」，Manufacturing Variance 比較「用多少」。 PPV (Purchase Price Variance):
- When: At procurement (PO Receipt or Invoice Match)
- Formula: (Actual unit price - Standard cost) × Qty purchased
- Responsibility: Purchasing department
- Example: Standard cost $10, actual purchase price $10.20, 1,000 pcs → PPV = ($10.20 - $10) × 1,000 = $200 unfavorable
- Meaning: Reflects whether purchasing can procure at standard cost; a purchasing KPI

Manufacturing Variance:
- When: At production completion
- Types: Material Usage Variance, Labor Efficiency Variance, Overhead Spending Variance
- Responsibility: Production department
- Example: Standard 10 pcs/unit, actual 11 pcs used → Material Usage Variance = 1 pc × $10 × 1,000 units = $10,000 unfavorable
- Meaning: Reflects production efficiency; a production department KPI

Memory aid: PPV measures "how much more we paid," Manufacturing Variance measures "how much more we used."
Q4：製造過程中產生的廢料成本要怎麼在 Oracle 中處理？ Q4: How do I handle the cost of scrap in manufacturing in Oracle? ▶
Oracle 提供兩種廢料成本處理方式，選擇哪種取決於廢料是否可預測：

方法一：在 BOM 中設定計畫廢料率（Planned Scrap %）
適合：固定且可預測的廢料（如電路板生產良率 95%，即 5% 廢料率）
設定：在 BOM 元件的 Yield Factor 欄位輸入 0.95（或 Scrap % = 5%）
效果：Cost Roll-up 時自動把廢料成本納入成品標準成本，每生產 1 個成品，BOM 會要求投入 1/0.95 = 1.053 個元件

方法二：在工單執行 Scrap Transaction（非計畫廢料）
適合：偶發性品質問題（如特定批次原料品質不良）
步驟：在 Work Order 上執行 Scrap Operation，系統產生 Dr Scrap Loss / Cr WIP 的分錄
若廢料有殘值：先做 Misc Receipt 把廢料入庫（以殘值計），再沖銷 WIP

最佳實踐：兩種方法可以並用。在 BOM 設定正常廢料率，異常廢料用 Scrap Transaction 處理，這樣財務報表可以清楚區分「正常生產損耗」和「異常廢料損失」。 Oracle provides two approaches for scrap cost handling — which to choose depends on whether scrap is predictable:

Method 1: Set Planned Scrap Rate in BOM (Planned Scrap %)
Best for: Fixed, predictable scrap (e.g., PCB production yield 95%, meaning 5% scrap rate)
Setup: Enter Yield Factor 0.95 (or Scrap % = 5%) in the BOM component's Yield Factor field
Effect: Cost Roll-up automatically includes scrap cost in finished good standard cost — producing 1 unit requires 1/0.95 = 1.053 components in the BOM

Method 2: Run Scrap Transaction on Work Order (Unplanned Scrap)
Best for: Occasional quality issues (e.g., a specific raw material batch with quality problems)
Steps: Run Scrap Operation on the Work Order; system generates Dr Scrap Loss / Cr WIP
If scrap has salvage value: First do Misc Receipt to receive scrap into inventory at salvage value, then offset WIP

Best Practice: Use both methods together. Set normal scrap rate in BOM; handle abnormal scrap with Scrap Transaction. This allows financial statements to clearly distinguish "normal production loss" from "abnormal scrap loss."

📚 術語對照表 📚 Terminology Reference

▼
英文術語English Term 中文Chinese 說明Description
Receipt Accounting 收貨會計 / 暫估入帳 在 PO 收貨時立即產生 GL 暫估分錄的機制Mechanism that generates immediate GL accrual entries upon PO receipt
PPV (Purchase Price Variance) 採購價格差異 實際採購價格與標準成本（或 PO 單價）之差Difference between actual purchase price and standard cost (or PO unit price)
Standard Cost 標準成本 預先設定的計畫成本，用於製造業成本計算和績效比較Pre-determined planned cost used in manufacturing for cost calculation and performance comparison
FIFO (First In First Out) 先進先出 最早入庫的存貨最先出庫，適合食品、藥品等有效期管理Earliest received inventory exits first; suitable for food, pharma with expiry management
Perpetual Average 移動加權平均 每次入庫後即時更新加權平均成本Weighted average cost updated in real-time after each receipt
Periodic Average 期間加權平均 期末計算全期加權平均成本，期中用估計成本Weighted average cost calculated at period-end; estimate used during the period
Cost Roll-up 成本展開 / 成本匯總 根據 BOM 和 Routing 自動計算成品標準成本的過程Process of automatically calculating finished good standard cost from BOM and Routing
Cost Scenario 成本情境 / 成本模擬 用於在不影響現行成本的情況下測試成本異動影響的沙盒Sandbox for testing cost change impacts without affecting current live costs
Landed Cost 到岸成本 把採購附加費用（運費、關稅等）分攤到庫存料號的機制Mechanism to allocate ancillary procurement costs (freight, duties) to inventory items
Trade Operation 貿易作業 Landed Cost 中，一次進口的費用分攤作業（含費用類型和分攤基準）In Landed Cost, the cost allocation operation for one import shipment (including charge types and allocation basis)
SLA (Subledger Accounting) 子分類帳會計 / 分類帳規則引擎 決定各種庫存交易類型對應 GL 帳戶的規則引擎Rules engine that determines which GL accounts each inventory transaction type maps to
Account Derivation Rule 帳戶推導規則 SLA 中根據交易屬性（料號、類別、OU 等）動態判斷 GL 帳戶的條件邏輯Conditional logic in SLA that dynamically determines GL accounts based on transaction attributes
Journal Entry Rule Set 傳票分錄規則集 SLA 中組合多條 Journal Line Rules 形成完整傳票的規則集合Collection of Journal Line Rules in SLA that combine into a complete journal entry
Cost Processor 成本處理器 期末關帳必跑的程序，計算並產生所有成本分攤的會計分錄Mandatory period-end process that calculates and generates all cost distribution accounting entries
SCFO (Supply Chain Financial Orchestration) 供應鏈財務協調 處理跨法人庫存調撥時的 Transfer Price 和自動財務分錄生成機制Mechanism for handling Transfer Price and automatic financial entry generation for cross-legal-entity inventory transfers
Manufacturing Variance 製造差異 實際生產投入（用料、工時、製費）與標準成本之間的差異Difference between actual production inputs (material, labor, overhead) and standard cost
WIP (Work In Process) 在製品 已開始生產但尚未完工的半成品，在製造期間存在於 WIP 帳戶Items in production but not yet completed; costs held in WIP accounts during manufacturing
Accrued Purchases 應計採購 / GR/IR 科目 收貨但尚未收到發票的暫估負債科目，是 Receipt Accounting 的核心Estimated liability account for goods received but invoice not yet received; central to Receipt Accounting

模組 9：資產與維護管理 Module 9: Asset & Maintenance Management

管理可維護資產的全生命週期，從登錄到預防性維護、IoT 整合，把被動維修變成主動預防

Manage maintainable asset lifecycle from registration to PM programs and IoT integration — shifting from reactive to preventive maintenance

Asset Lifecycle PM Programs Work Orders IoT Warranty
🔑
情境背景：ChemPlant 化工廠的設備維護轉型Scenario: ChemPlant's Maintenance Transformation

ChemPlant 化工廠擁有 200 台關鍵設備，包括壓縮機、反應爐、輸送泵和 CNC 加工機台。過去，維護部門採用「壞了再修」的被動模式——一旦壓縮機在凌晨 3 點故障，不只要緊急呼叫技師，還得停線等待備件，每次非計畫停機平均損失 NT$80 萬。工廠在 2023 年記錄了 47 次非計畫停機，全年維護成本高得嚇人，員工士氣也因頻繁緊急維修而低落。 ChemPlant operates 200 pieces of critical equipment including compressors, reactors, transfer pumps, and CNC machining centers. Previously, the maintenance team operated in purely reactive mode — when a compressor failed at 3 AM, they scrambled for technicians and waited for spare parts, with each unplanned downtime event averaging NT$800,000 in losses. In 2023, the plant recorded 47 unplanned stoppages, and annual maintenance costs soared while technician morale suffered from constant firefighting.

導入 Oracle Maintenance Cloud 後，ChemPlant 首先建立了完整的資產層級結構：以「CNC 加工線 #3」為頂層，往下拆分主軸組件（Spindle Assembly）、主軸軸承（Spindle Bearing）等子資產，每一層都有獨立的維護計畫。壓縮機裝上計時器，每 500 小時自動觸發換油工單；電動馬達裝設溫度感測器，一旦溫度超過 85°C，IoT 條件事件立即生成高優先級工單，技師在溫度超標前就能介入處理。 After implementing Oracle Maintenance Cloud, ChemPlant built a complete asset hierarchy: CNC Machine Line #3 at the top level, breaking down into Spindle Assembly and Spindle Bearing sub-assets, each with its own maintenance program. Compressors were fitted with hour meters — every 500 hours triggers an automatic oil-change work order. Electric motors received temperature sensors; when temperature exceeds 85°C, an IoT Condition Event instantly generates a high-priority work order, allowing technicians to intervene before failure occurs.

實施後的第一年，非計畫停機次數從 47 次降至 11 次，降幅達 77%。更重要的是，2025 年 6 月一台新購的 CNC 機台主軸在保固期內損壞，系統自動比對供應商保固記錄，生成保固索賠單，成功向供應商追回維修費用。這個模組將帶你完整走過 Oracle Maintenance Cloud 的核心功能，從資產登錄到 IoT 整合，讓你的工廠也能從被動救火轉型為主動預防。 In the first year after implementation, unplanned stoppages dropped from 47 to 11 — a 77% reduction. Even more impactful: in June 2025, a newly purchased CNC spindle failed within its warranty period. The system automatically matched the supplier warranty record and generated a Warranty Claim, successfully recovering repair costs from the supplier. This module walks you through Oracle Maintenance Cloud end-to-end: from asset registration through IoT integration, transforming your plant from reactive firefighting to proactive prevention.

核心功能一覽 Key Features Overview

▼
🏗️

資產層級管理Asset Hierarchy

三層結構：CNC 加工線 #3（設備）→ 主軸組件（子系統）→ 主軸軸承（元件）。每層可設定獨立 PM 計畫，軸承每 2,000 小時換，整機每年大修。Three-level structure: CNC Line #3 (equipment) → Spindle Assembly (subsystem) → Spindle Bearing (component). Each level has independent PM — bearing replaced every 2,000 hours, full overhaul annually.

⏱️

計量表 PMMeter-Based PM

壓縮機每年運轉 1,200 小時，每 500 小時換油，系統自動計算：下次換油 = 上次 + 500h，一年觸發 2.4 次工單，第 3 次跨年自動排到次年 2 月。Compressor runs 1,200 hr/year; oil change every 500 hr. System calculates: next due = last reading + 500 hr. Triggers 2.4 WOs/year; the 3rd occurrence auto-schedules into February next year.

📅

日曆式 PMCalendar-Based PM

每季安全巡檢（1/4/7/10 月第一週），系統預測未來 12 個月自動生成 4 張預測工單，排程顯示在維護日曆上，提前 2 週發料通知。Quarterly safety inspection (week 1 of Jan/Apr/Jul/Oct). System generates 4 forecast WOs for next 12 months, displayed on the maintenance calendar with 2-week advance parts notification.

📡

IoT 條件事件IoT Condition Events

馬達溫度感測器：正常 40-80°C，超過 85°C → 系統接收 IoT 訊號 → 建立條件事件 → 自動生成高優先工單 WO-IOT-789，派給在班技師。Motor temp sensor: normal 40-80°C. Above 85°C → IoT signal received → Condition Event created → auto-generates high-priority WO-IOT-789, dispatched to on-shift technician.

🛡️

供應商保固管理Supplier Warranty

CNC 機台 2024-01 購入，3 年保固至 2027-01。2025-06 主軸故障，系統比對保固有效期，自動生成保固索賠單 WC-2025-001，追回供應商維修費 NT$15 萬。CNC purchased 2024-01, 3-year warranty to 2027-01. Spindle fails 2025-06; system checks warranty validity, auto-generates Warranty Claim WC-2025-001 to recover NT$150,000 repair cost from supplier.

🚚

服務物流Service Logistics

外派技師攜帶備品出廠：從備品子庫存發料（5L 機油、1 個濾芯），出廠差旅與工時成本自動過帳至資產成本帳，維護成本可追溯至單台設備。Field technician dispatched with parts from spare parts subinventory (5L oil, 1 filter). Travel and labor costs auto-posted to the asset cost account — maintenance cost traceable to individual equipment.

深度解析 1：資產層級結構與計量表 Deep Dive 1: Asset Hierarchy & Meter Templates

▼

Oracle Maintenance Cloud 的可維護資產（Maintainable Asset）支援多層父子結構。最頂層通常是一條生產線或一台完整設備，往下可拆解至子系統乃至單一元件。這種層級的意義在於：維護成本可以在各層累計，也可以在特定子層設定不同的 PM 頻率。 Oracle Maintenance Cloud's Maintainable Assets support multi-level parent-child structures. The top level is typically a production line or complete equipment unit, drilling down to subsystems and individual components. This hierarchy means maintenance costs accumulate at each level, and different PM frequencies can be configured at specific sub-levels.

具體範例：CNC 加工線 #3 層級 Concrete Example: CNC Machine Line #3 Hierarchy

層級Level 資產名稱Asset Name 資產編號Asset Number 計量表Meter PM 設定PM Setting
L1 CNC 加工線 #3CNC Machine Line #3 ASSET-CNC-003 運轉小時數Operating Hours 年度大修（每 8,760 小時）Annual overhaul (every 8,760 hr)
L2 主軸組件Spindle Assembly ASSET-CNC-003-SA 運轉小時數（繼承）Operating Hours (inherited) 潤滑脂補充（每 1,000 小時）Grease replenishment (every 1,000 hr)
L3 主軸軸承Spindle Bearing ASSET-CNC-003-SB 運轉小時數（繼承）Operating Hours (inherited) 軸承更換（每 2,000 小時）Bearing replacement (every 2,000 hr)

計量表範本（Meter Templates）類型 Meter Template Types

計量表類型Meter Type 單位Unit 適用設備Applicable Equipment 設定路徑Setup Path
Hours / 小時 HR 壓縮機、馬達、機台Compressors, motors, machines Maintenance → Setup → Meter Templates
Mileage / 里程 KM / MI 廠內運輸車、叉車In-plant vehicles, forklifts Maintenance → Setup → Meter Templates
Cycles / 循環次數 CYC 沖壓機、射出成型機Punch presses, injection molders Maintenance → Setup → Meter Templates
Q：計量表讀數要怎麼輸入？可以和 IoT 自動同步嗎？ Q: How are meter readings entered? Can they sync automatically with IoT? ▶

手動輸入路徑：Maintenance → Assets → Record Meter Readings。技師每天巡檢時手動登錄小時數，如今天 CNC #3 記錄 3,450 小時。自動同步方面，透過 Oracle IoT Cloud Service 或第三方 SCADA 系統以 REST API 推送計量表讀數，系統每小時接收一次，自動更新。當累計小時數到達觸發閾值，PM 程式自動生成預測工單。 Manual entry path: Maintenance → Assets → Record Meter Readings. Technicians log readings during daily rounds — e.g., CNC #3 today reads 3,450 hours. For automatic sync, Oracle IoT Cloud Service or third-party SCADA systems push readings via REST API, received hourly and auto-updated. When the cumulative reading reaches the trigger threshold, the PM program automatically generates a forecast work order.

⚠️
常見錯誤：Common Mistake: 忘記將子資產的計量表設為「繼承父資產讀數」。若主軸組件（L2）的小時計不繼承 CNC 整機（L1）的讀數，L2 的 PM 就永遠不會觸發。設定路徑：資產主檔 → Meter tab → 勾選「Inherited from Parent Asset」。 Forgetting to set child asset meters to "Inherited from Parent Asset." If the Spindle Assembly (L2) hour meter doesn't inherit CNC Line #3's (L1) readings, L2's PM will never trigger. Setup path: Asset Master → Meter tab → check "Inherited from Parent Asset."

深度解析 2：維護程式 — 計量式 vs 日曆式 vs IoT Deep Dive 2: Maintenance Programs — Meter vs Calendar vs IoT

▼

三種 PM 觸發方式比較 Three PM Trigger Types Compared

類型Type 觸發條件Trigger Condition ChemPlant 範例ChemPlant Example 適用情境Best For
Calendar 固定日期或間隔天數Fixed date or day interval 每季（90天）安全巡檢Quarterly (90-day) safety inspection 法規要求、時效性維護Regulatory, time-based tasks
Meter 計量表達到閾值Meter reaches threshold 壓縮機每 500 小時換油Compressor oil change every 500 hr 使用量相關維護（油品、輪胎）Usage-based tasks (oil, tires, wear parts)
IoT Condition 感測器值超出範圍Sensor value out of range 馬達溫度 > 85°CMotor temp > 85°C 預測式維護、品質異常Predictive maintenance, quality anomalies

範例 A：計量式 PM — 壓縮機換油計算 Example A: Meter-Based PM — Compressor Oil Change Calculation

設備：空氣壓縮機 C-001 | 年運轉時數：1,200 小時 | 換油週期：每 500 小時 Asset: Air Compressor C-001 | Annual Hours: 1,200 hr | Oil Change Interval: every 500 hr

工單次序WO Sequence 觸發小時數Trigger Hour Reading 預估日期（1月1日起算）Estimated Date (from Jan 1) 說明Note
WO#1 500 hr 5 月 1 日（約第 150 天）May 1 (~Day 150) 500 ÷ 1,200 × 365 = 152 天500 ÷ 1,200 × 365 = 152 days
WO#2 1,000 hr 9 月 28 日（約第 304 天）Sep 28 (~Day 304) 1,000 ÷ 1,200 × 365 = 304 天1,000 ÷ 1,200 × 365 = 304 days
WO#3 1,500 hr 次年 2 月 24 日Next Feb 24 1,500 ÷ 1,200 × 365 = 456 天（跨年排程）1,500 ÷ 1,200 × 365 = 456 days (crosses into next year)

範例 B：日曆式 PM — 季度安全巡檢預測工單 Example B: Calendar-Based PM — Quarterly Safety Inspection Forecast

設定：PM 程式「SAFETY-QTR」，頻率 = 每 90 天，起始日 2025-01-06（1月第一週）。執行「Generate Maintenance Forecast」後，系統在維護日曆產生： Configuration: PM Program "SAFETY-QTR", frequency = every 90 days, start date 2025-01-06 (first week of January). After running "Generate Maintenance Forecast," the system produces on the maintenance calendar:

  • WO-SAFE-2501 → 2025-01-06 Q1Q1
  • WO-SAFE-2502 → 2025-04-06 Q2
  • WO-SAFE-2503 → 2025-07-05 Q3
  • WO-SAFE-2504 → 2025-10-04 Q4
Q：如果計量式和日曆式同時設定，哪個優先觸發？ Q: If both meter-based and calendar-based PM are configured, which triggers first? ▶

兩者都會觸發，各自獨立生成工單。Oracle 允許在同一個維護程式中同時設定多個觸發條件（稱為 Multiple Criteria），例如：每 500 小時 OR 每 6 個月（以先到者為準）。設定路徑：Maintenance Program → Maintenance Requirement → 在 Scheduling tab 設定多個 Criteria，勾選「Use Earliest Trigger」。 Both trigger independently and each generates its own work order. Oracle allows multiple trigger criteria within one Maintenance Program (called Multiple Criteria) — e.g., every 500 hours OR every 6 months, whichever comes first. Setup path: Maintenance Program → Maintenance Requirement → Scheduling tab → add multiple Criteria → check "Use Earliest Trigger."

⚠️
常見錯誤：Common Mistake: 設定計量式 PM 後，忘記執行「Generate Maintenance Forecast」（路徑：Maintenance → Maintenance Forecast → Generate），導致工單不出現。此步驟需定期執行（建議每月執行一次，或設排程自動執行）。 After setting up meter-based PM, forgetting to run "Generate Maintenance Forecast" (Maintenance → Maintenance Forecast → Generate), causing work orders not to appear. This step must be run periodically (recommended monthly, or set as a scheduled process).

深度解析 3：IoT 條件事件與預測式維護 Deep Dive 3: IoT Condition Events & Predictive Maintenance

▼

IoT 整合讓 Oracle Maintenance 從「預防」進化到「預測」。透過 Oracle IoT Cloud Service 作為中介平台，設備感測器的數值即時傳入雲端，超出設定閾值時自動觸發「條件事件（Condition Event）」，再由條件事件規則引擎自動建立緊急維護工單。 IoT integration elevates Oracle Maintenance from "preventive" to "predictive." Via Oracle IoT Cloud Service as the middleware, sensor values stream to the cloud in real time. When a value exceeds configured thresholds, the system auto-triggers a "Condition Event," and the event rules engine automatically creates an emergency maintenance work order.

具體設定範例：馬達溫度監控 Concrete Configuration Example: Motor Temperature Monitoring

設定項目Setting 值Value
資產Asset Motor M-007 (ASSET-MTR-007)
感測器參數Sensor Parameter TEMP_WINDING (°C)
正常範圍Normal Range 40 – 80°C
警告閾值Warning Threshold 81 – 85°C → 生成中優先工單Medium-priority WO
緊急閾值Critical Threshold > 85°C → 生成高優先工單 + 停機通知High-priority WO + shutdown alert
工單範本WO Template WDef-MOTOR-OVERHEAT
設定路徑Setup Path Maintenance → Setup → Condition Events → Rules
Q：IoT 裝置需要提供什麼格式的資料？如何連接到 Oracle？ Q: What data format do IoT devices need to provide, and how do they connect to Oracle? ▶

Oracle 接受兩種連接方式：(1) Oracle IoT Cloud Service：裝置透過 MQTT 或 HTTPS 將數據推送到 IoT 平台，IoT 平台再以 REST API 呼叫 Oracle Maintenance Cloud 的 Condition Event API（格式：JSON）。(2) 直接 REST API：若公司有 SCADA 或 MES，可由 SCADA 直接呼叫 Oracle Maintenance REST API endpoint：POST /fscmRestApi/resources/.../conditionEvents，傳入 assetId、parameterName、currentValue、observedDate。Oracle 技術顧問需協助設定 OAuth 2.0 認證。 Oracle accepts two connection methods: (1) Oracle IoT Cloud Service: devices push data via MQTT or HTTPS to the IoT platform, which calls the Oracle Maintenance Cloud Condition Event API via REST (JSON format). (2) Direct REST API: if your company has SCADA or MES, SCADA can directly call Oracle Maintenance REST API: POST /fscmRestApi/resources/.../conditionEvents, passing assetId, parameterName, currentValue, observedDate. An Oracle technical consultant is needed to configure OAuth 2.0 authentication.

✅
最佳實踐：Best Practice: 先設定「警告級」閾值（溫度 81-85°C），讓技師有時間在設備真正損壞前介入。不要只設「緊急級」——等到觸發緊急工單時，設備往往已需更昂貴的修理。兩級閾值設計讓維護更有層次。 First configure a "warning" threshold (temp 81-85°C) so technicians have time to intervene before actual failure. Don't configure only a "critical" level — by the time the emergency WO triggers, the equipment often needs far more expensive repairs. Two-tier thresholds make maintenance more graduated and cost-effective.

深度解析 4：維護工單執行流程 Deep Dive 4: Maintenance Work Order Execution

▼

維護工單（Maintenance Work Order）與製造工單（Manufacturing Work Order）在 Oracle Cloud 中是兩個獨立的功能模組，但共享 Work Center 和資源定義。維護工單的核心是「Work Definition（工作定義）」——它定義了每種維護任務的標準作業程序（SOP）、所需零件和工時。 Maintenance Work Orders and Manufacturing Work Orders are two separate functional modules in Oracle Cloud, but they share Work Center and resource definitions. The core of a maintenance work order is the "Work Definition" — it defines the standard operating procedure (SOP), required parts, and labor hours for each maintenance task type.

範例：WO-M-456 — CNC 機台換油作業 Example: WO-M-456 — CNC Machine Oil Change

步驟Step 作業說明Operation Description 標準工時Std. Time 所需資源Resource
Step 1 設備鎖定（Lock Out/Tag Out）Lock Out / Tag Out 15 min 維護技師 1 名1 Maintenance Tech
Step 2 舊油排放Drain used oil 30 min 廢油桶、排油工具Waste oil drum, drain tools
Step 3 濾芯更換Replace oil filter 20 min Item: FILTER-CNC-001（1個）Item: FILTER-CNC-001 (1 ea)
Step 4 新油注入Fill new oil 20 min Item: CNC-OIL-5L（5 公升）Item: CNC-OIL-5L (5 liters)
Step 5 試車與確認Test run & verification 15 min 技師 + 操作員Tech + Operator

發料流程：工單發布後，倉庫收到揀貨單，從「備品子庫存（Spare Parts Subinventory）」揀出 FILTER-CNC-001 × 1 和 CNC-OIL-5L × 5L，掃碼確認，材料成本 NT$2,800 自動過帳至工單成本，最終轉至資產累計維護費用帳。 Parts Issuance Flow: After WO release, the warehouse receives a pick list, picks FILTER-CNC-001 × 1 and CNC-OIL-5L × 5L from the Spare Parts Subinventory, scans to confirm. Material cost NT$2,800 auto-posts to WO cost, then transferred to the asset's cumulative maintenance expense account.

Q：維護工單和製造工單有什麼差別？ Q: What is the difference between a Maintenance Work Order and a Manufacturing Work Order? ▶
比較項目Comparison 維護工單Maintenance WO 製造工單Manufacturing WO
模組Module Oracle Maintenance Cloud Oracle Manufacturing Cloud
目的Purpose 維修 / 保養設備Repair/maintain equipment 生產產品Produce products
產出Output 設備可用性提升，無庫存產出Improved asset availability, no inventory output 成品入庫Finished goods to inventory
成本去向Cost Destination 過帳至資產成本帳Posted to asset cost account 過帳至產品標準成本Posted to product standard cost
BOM/Work DefinitionBOM/Work Definition Maintenance Work DefinitionMaintenance Work Definition Manufacturing Work Definition（含 BOM）Manufacturing Work Definition (with BOM)
共用 Work Center？Shared Work Center? ✅ 可共用同一個 Work Center（如工具間），但建議設不同班別排程以避免衝突✅ Yes, same Work Center can be shared (e.g., toolroom), but configure different shift schedules to avoid conflicts
Q：如何處理 PM 排程外的緊急維修？ Q: How does the system handle emergency maintenance outside the PM schedule? ▶

緊急維修通過建立「Corrective Work Order（矯正性工單）」處理，不需要 PM 程式觸發，由技師或主管手動建立，路徑：Maintenance → Work Orders → Create Work Order → Work Order Type: Corrective。緊急工單可設優先級 = Urgent，並在工單上標記維修原因碼（如：突發故障 / Unexpected Failure）。完成後的工單資料會累積成資產維護歷史，用於後續分析改善 PM 頻率。 Emergency maintenance is handled by creating a "Corrective Work Order" — no PM program trigger required, manually created by technician or supervisor via: Maintenance → Work Orders → Create Work Order → Work Order Type: Corrective. Emergency WOs can be set to Priority = Urgent and tagged with a failure code (e.g., Unexpected Failure). Completed WO data accumulates in the asset's maintenance history for analysis and PM frequency optimization.

⚠️
常見錯誤：Common Mistake: 緊急維修完成後忘記「關閉工單」並記錄實際工時和用料。這會導致資產成本帳低估，且維護歷史不完整，無法準確分析 MTBF（平均故障間隔時間）。工單應在 5 個工作日內完成關閉。 After emergency repairs, forgetting to "Close the Work Order" and record actual labor and materials. This understates asset cost accounts and creates incomplete maintenance history, preventing accurate MTBF (Mean Time Between Failures) analysis. Work orders should be closed within 5 business days of completion.

深度解析 5：供應商保固管理 Deep Dive 5: Supplier Warranty Management

▼

Oracle Maintenance Cloud 的保固模組讓企業不必手動追蹤每台設備的保固期限。系統在建立維護工單時，自動比對該資產的供應商保固記錄——如果在保固期內，則提示建立保固索賠（Warranty Claim），維護費用轉向供應商追回。 Oracle Maintenance Cloud's warranty module eliminates manual tracking of warranty expiry dates. When a maintenance work order is created, the system automatically cross-references the asset's supplier warranty record. If within the warranty period, it prompts creating a Warranty Claim to recover repair costs from the supplier.

具體案例：CNC 機台主軸保固索賠 Concrete Case: CNC Spindle Warranty Claim

項目Item 資訊Information
資產Asset CNC Machine Line #3 (ASSET-CNC-003)
購入日期Purchase Date 2024-01-15
供應商Supplier Mazak Taiwan (Supplier: S-MAZAK-001)
保固條款Warranty Terms 3 年整機保固（至 2027-01-14）；主軸 2 年（至 2026-01-14）3-year full machine warranty (to 2027-01-14); Spindle 2-year (to 2026-01-14)
故障日期Failure Date 2025-06-10
系統判斷System Decision 保固期內 ✅Within Warranty ✅
保固索賠單Warranty Claim WC-2025-001
追回金額Recovered Amount NT$150,000
設定路徑Setup Path Maintenance → Assets → Manage Supplier Warranties
💡
保固索賠流程：工單建立 → 系統提示「此資產在供應商保固期內」→ 點擊「Create Warranty Claim」→ 系統自動填入供應商、保固條款、預計回收金額 → 送出索賠後轉 AP 模組追蹤應收款 → 供應商核准後進行貸項記帳（Credit Memo） Warranty Claim Process: WO created → system prompts "This asset is within supplier warranty" → click "Create Warranty Claim" → system auto-fills supplier, warranty terms, estimated recovery amount → claim sent → transferred to AP module for receivable tracking → upon supplier approval, Credit Memo is posted

深度解析 6：三種維護策略的成本效益分析 Deep Dive 6: Cost-Benefit Analysis of Three Maintenance Strategies

▼
維護策略Strategy 定義Definition ChemPlant 範例ChemPlant Example 年成本估算Annual Cost Est. 停機風險Downtime Risk
矯正式Corrective 壞了才修Fix when broken 壓縮機故障停線修理，急件採購Compressor breaks, emergency repair, rush parts NT$4.7M 高（47 次/年）High (47/yr)
預防式Preventive 定期計畫保養Scheduled PM 壓縮機每 500hr 換油，無論油品狀況Compressor oil change every 500hr regardless of oil condition NT$1.8M 中（11 次/年）Med (11/yr)
預測式Predictive 依狀態判斷維修時機Condition-based maintenance 溫度感測器偵測油品劣化，精準觸發換油Temp sensor detects oil degradation, precise oil change trigger NT$1.1M 低（3 次/年）Low (3/yr)

實務上最佳策略是混合使用：高危設備（如壓縮機、反應爐）採用預測式；一般設備採用預防式；低重要性設備採用矯正式。Oracle Maintenance Cloud 允許三種策略在同一套系統並存，依設備重要性分類設定。 In practice, the best approach is a hybrid: high-criticality equipment (compressors, reactors) uses predictive; standard equipment uses preventive; low-criticality uses corrective. Oracle Maintenance Cloud supports all three strategies simultaneously within one system, configured by equipment criticality classification.

常見問題 FAQ Frequently Asked Questions

▼
Q1：維護工單和製造工單的根本差異是什麼？ Q1: What is the fundamental difference between a Maintenance Work Order and a Manufacturing Work Order? ▶

最核心的差異在於目的與成本去向。製造工單的目的是生產產品，成本（材料、工時、製造費）過帳到「在製品（WIP）」再轉至「成品標準成本」；維護工單的目的是維持設備可用性，成本過帳到「資產維護費用帳（Asset Maintenance Cost Account）」，最終體現在資產的總持有成本（Total Cost of Ownership）報表中。此外，製造工單有 BOM（物料清單）和路由（Routing）的概念；維護工單對應的是 Maintenance Work Definition，含有作業步驟和零件需求，但無成品產出。兩者在 Oracle UI 中入口完全不同：製造工單在 Manufacturing 模組，維護工單在 Maintenance 模組。 The core difference is purpose and cost destination. Manufacturing work orders produce goods — costs (materials, labor, overhead) flow to WIP then to finished goods standard cost. Maintenance work orders maintain equipment availability — costs flow to the Asset Maintenance Cost Account, ultimately reflected in Total Cost of Ownership reports. Additionally, manufacturing WOs use BOM and Routing; maintenance WOs use Maintenance Work Definitions with operation steps and parts requirements but no finished goods output. In Oracle UI, the entry points are completely different: manufacturing WOs are in the Manufacturing module, maintenance WOs in the Maintenance module.

Q2：製造和維護可以共用同一個 Work Center 嗎？ Q2: Can the same Work Center be used for both manufacturing and maintenance? ▶

技術上可以，Oracle 不限制 Work Center 只用於製造或維護。例如，「精密工具間（Tool Room）」這個 Work Center 可以同時服務製造工單（刀具修磨）和維護工單（設備零件精加工）。但在實務上需要注意產能衝突：若同一個 Work Center 在同一時段有製造工單和維護工單的需求，排程工具（Manufacturing → Scheduling）無法自動偵測跨模組的衝突。建議做法：在 Work Center 設定中為維護工作指定不同的班別（Shift）或特定時段（如每週一上午 8-12 點保留給維護），或建立獨立的「維護 Work Center」以避免混淆。 Technically yes — Oracle does not restrict Work Centers to manufacturing or maintenance only. For example, a "Tool Room" Work Center can serve both manufacturing WOs (tool grinding) and maintenance WOs (precision part machining). However, in practice, watch for capacity conflicts: if the same Work Center has both manufacturing and maintenance demand in the same time slot, the scheduling tool (Manufacturing → Scheduling) cannot auto-detect cross-module conflicts. Best practice: assign different shifts or reserved time slots for maintenance work within the Work Center settings (e.g., every Monday morning 8-12 reserved for maintenance), or create a separate "Maintenance Work Center" to avoid confusion.

Q3：PM 排程外的緊急維修，系統怎麼處理？ Q3: How does the system handle emergency maintenance outside the PM schedule? ▶

緊急維修（非計畫性）有兩種觸發方式：(1) 手動建立矯正性工單（Corrective WO）：維護主管或技師發現故障，手動建立工單（Work Order Type = Corrective，Priority = Urgent），路徑：Maintenance → Work Orders → Create Work Order。(2) IoT 自動觸發：感測器超標，系統自動建立緊急工單（已如前述）。無論哪種方式，緊急工單不需要來自 PM 程式，可以立即建立。完工後，這些工單的資料（故障原因、用料、工時）會保存在資產的維護歷史中。定期分析這些歷史資料，可以調整 PM 頻率——例如發現某台機器每 430 小時就出現油品污染，就應把換油週期從 500 小時縮短至 400 小時。 Emergency (unplanned) maintenance has two trigger methods: (1) Manual Corrective WO creation: maintenance supervisor or technician identifies failure and manually creates WO (Work Order Type = Corrective, Priority = Urgent). Path: Maintenance → Work Orders → Create Work Order. (2) IoT auto-trigger: sensor exceeds threshold, system auto-creates emergency WO (as described above). Either way, emergency WOs don't require a PM program — they can be created immediately. After completion, WO data (failure cause, materials, labor) is saved in the asset's maintenance history. Regular analysis of this history enables PM frequency adjustments — for example, if a machine shows oil contamination every 430 hours, shorten the oil change interval from 500 to 400 hours.

Q4：IoT 裝置需要提供什麼資料格式，如何連接 Oracle？ Q4: What data format do IoT devices need to provide and how do they connect to Oracle? ▶

Oracle Maintenance Cloud 接受兩種 IoT 整合架構： Oracle Maintenance Cloud supports two IoT integration architectures:

方式 1 — Oracle IoT Cloud Service（推薦）：感測器透過 MQTT 協議（port 8883）或 HTTPS 連接到 Oracle IoT Cloud，IoT Cloud 建立裝置模型和警示規則，當條件觸發時呼叫 Oracle Maintenance Cloud 的 REST API 建立條件事件。資料格式為 JSON，例如：{"assetNumber": "ASSET-MTR-007", "parameterName": "TEMP_WINDING", "value": 87.3, "timestamp": "2025-05-01T14:23:00Z"}。 Method 1 — Oracle IoT Cloud Service (recommended): Sensors connect to Oracle IoT Cloud via MQTT (port 8883) or HTTPS. IoT Cloud establishes device models and alert rules; when conditions trigger, it calls Oracle Maintenance Cloud REST API to create Condition Events. Data format is JSON, e.g.: {"assetNumber": "ASSET-MTR-007", "parameterName": "TEMP_WINDING", "value": 87.3, "timestamp": "2025-05-01T14:23:00Z"}.

方式 2 — 直接 REST API 整合：若公司已有 SCADA/MES，可由 SCADA 直接呼叫 Oracle Maintenance REST API endpoint。需要先取得 Oracle Fusion 的 OAuth 2.0 Access Token，再呼叫 POST /fscmRestApi/resources/11.13.18.05/maintenanceConditionEvents。Oracle 技術顧問需協助設定服務帳號（Service Account）和 OAuth 客戶端。初期建議先以方式 1 試行，再視需要評估直接整合。 Method 2 — Direct REST API Integration: If your company has SCADA/MES, SCADA can directly call Oracle Maintenance REST API. An OAuth 2.0 Access Token from Oracle Fusion must be obtained first, then call POST /fscmRestApi/resources/11.13.18.05/maintenanceConditionEvents. An Oracle technical consultant is needed to configure the Service Account and OAuth client. For initial deployment, Method 1 is recommended; evaluate direct integration as needs evolve.

兩大業務主線總覽

Two Core Business Flows Overview

Procure-to-Pay (P2P)

1需求確認 → 建立請購單 (PR)Identify Need → Create PR
2審核 → 產生採購訂單 (PO)Approve → Generate PO
3供應商出貨 → 收料 (Receipt)Supplier ships → Receive
4發票比對 → 付款 (AP)Invoice match → Payment (AP)

涉及模組：採購 + 庫存 + 成本（收料應計）+ 應付帳款

Modules involved: Procurement + Inventory + Cost (Receipt Accounting) + Accounts Payable

Order-to-Cash (O2C)

1客戶下單 → 定價 → GOP 承諾Customer order → Pricing → GOP Promise
2Orchestration 履行協調Orchestration fulfillment
3揀貨 → 出貨確認 (Ship Confirm)Pick → Ship Confirm
4開立 AR 發票 → 收款AR Invoice → Cash Receipt

涉及模組：訂單管理 + GOP + 庫存 + 成本（COGS）+ 應收帳款

Modules involved: Order Mgmt + GOP + Inventory + Cost (COGS) + Accounts Receivable

可維護資產Maintainable Asset維護在系統中登錄需要定期維護的設備Equipment registered in the system for periodic maintenance tracking
維護程式Maintenance Program維護定義 PM 計劃觸發條件的設定（行事曆/計量/IoT）Configuration defining PM plan trigger conditions (calendar/meter/IoT)
維護預測Maintenance Forecast維護系統依 PM 計劃計算的未來維護需求排程System-calculated future maintenance schedule based on PM programs
條件事件Condition Event維護IoT 感測器偵測到異常時觸發的事件，可自動建立工單Event triggered by IoT sensor anomaly detection; can auto-create work orders
供應鏈協調Supply Chain Orchestration (SCO)共通將供應規劃建議訂單傳至執行模組的中間協調層Middleware layer passing supply planning suggested orders to execution modules
產品族譜Product Genealogy製造正反向追蹤原料與成品關係，用於品質召回分析Forward/backward tracing of material-product relationships for quality recall analysis
標準成本差異Purchase Price Variance (PPV)成本採購實際價格與標準成本的差異，反映採購效率Difference between actual purchase price and standard cost, reflecting procurement efficiency
